Current Affairs Commentary

A Cross-Sectional Analysis of the Current Situation in Central Europe

— Lang

The failure of the League of Nations' sanctions against Italy represents a significant blow to the collective security system and the forces of peace. When the forces of "righteousness" suffer setbacks, the shadow of "evil" naturally grows larger. The recent compromise between Germany and Austria, and the formation of the German-Italian bloc, are clear examples of this. Germany and Austria, two Germanic nations with the same language and culture, had been largely incompatible in recent years. However, on the evening of the 11th, the two countries suddenly announced a friendly agreement. Germany recognized Austria's full sovereignty, and the two countries agreed not to interfere in each other's internal affairs, declaring that this was entirely consistent with the spirit of the Italian-Austrian-Hungarian agreement. The Austrian cabinet was reorganized accordingly, appointing the well-known pro-German Hürth as a minister without portfolio and Schmidt as the Minister of Foreign Affairs. After this agreement was established, not only would the past disputes between Germany and Austria temporarily cease, but its impact on Central Europe and the entire European political situation would be very significant.

Why have Germany and Austria, once incompatible, suddenly reached a compromise? To explain this, we must examine the past relations between the two countries and the international situation in Central Europe. Germany and Austria are Germanic nations with the same language and culture. After the Great War, there was a strong tendency for the two countries to merge. The German-Austrian Customs Union of 1931 was the initial implementation of this plan. However, the merger of Germany and Austria would significantly harm the interests of the Allied Powers, especially France's hegemony in Europe. Therefore, they vehemently opposed Austria's annexation by Germany. The Treaty of Saint-Germain included a provision prohibiting the merger of Germany and Austria. After the Nazi Party came to power, Hitler's annexation movement intensified. However, at this time, most of the Austrian people opposed merging with Germany, and Italy seized the opportunity to support Austria and oppose Germany's southward expansion policy. This was because if Germany annexed Austria, the borders of Italy and Germany would be connected, which would greatly hinder Mussolini's ambition to dominate Central Europe. Therefore, when the Nazi Party launched an armed coup in Vienna in July 1934, assassinating Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss, Italy immediately deployed troops to the northern border, preparing to use force to counter Germany's annexation movement. Since then, Austria has been under the protection of the Blackshirt Prime Minister, opposing Hitler's southward expansion policy. However, after Italy launched its aggression in East Africa and was subjected to economic sanctions by the League of Nations, its international position became very isolated. Italy then turned to Germany and secretly courted them. Germany, having abandoned the Treaty of Versailles and actively expanded its military, sought to develop abroad, leading to encirclement by France, the Soviet Union, and the Little Entente. Therefore, it was naturally eager to join hands with its comrade in this aggression front. Although the League of Nations sanctions against Italy have been lifted and the Mediterranean Mutual Assistance Agreement has been abolished, the forces of the left-wing People's Front have greatly developed in Europe. Therefore, these two anti-socialist fascist "brothers in distress" have an even greater need to seek cooperation. The past grievances between Germany and Italy were concentrated on the Austrian question. Now, to seek cooperation, this issue must be resolved first. Fortunately, the Austrian government was "made" in Rome. Thus, through the mediation of the Blackshirt Prime Minister, the German-Austrian Friendly Agreement was simultaneously announced in the capitals of the two countries on the 11th.

Therefore, the compromise between Germany and Austria should not be seen merely as a simple matter between Germany and Austria, but rather as a matter between Germany and Italy, the preliminary condition for German-Italian collusion. We can see the collusion between Germany and Italy not only in the resolution of the Austrian question but also in the recent relations between the two countries. Let's cite a few important facts. On the 24th of last month, Italian Air Force Minister and Air Force Chief of Staff General Valle visited Berlin. On the 26th, he signed a commercial aviation agreement with Germany for a period of ten years. This agreement has significant economic and political implications, as it stipulates that both parties may operate routes between Rome and the North Sea and allows Germany to establish an airfield on one of the Italian-owned Dodecanese Islands (in the eastern Aegean Sea). The former could cut across the routes operated by France and the Soviet Union, while the latter would allow Germany to gain a foothold in the Mediterranean. Two days later (June 28), Germany and Italy signed a commercial agreement to enhance their economic relations. More recently, the two countries reached an understanding: Germany recognized Italy's annexation of Abyssinia and guaranteed Austria's independence, while Italy recognized Germany's eastward expansion and recovery of old colonies. The two countries also adopted a common attitude on all international issues. The scope of the collusion between Germany and Italy not only includes Austria but also extends to Hungary and Poland. Hungary, due to the signing of the Rome Protocols, had already fallen under Italy's sphere of influence. Poland, having signed a non-aggression treaty with Germany in 1934, had also joined Berlin's ranks. In this way, the "Central European Group" (Mittel Europa) advocated by Wilhelm II has emerged in the form of an aggressive bloc.

The main purpose of forming this aggressive bloc is naturally to counter the peace front led by France, the Soviet Union, and the Little Entente. With the formation of this bloc, Italy can dominate Central Europe and restore its important position before the East African war. As for Germany, it can escape its current international isolation and actively pursue its outward aggression policy for the Third Reich. Its main targets are eastward expansion and southward invasion of the Balkan Peninsula, and it also seeks to recover its old colonies. Therefore, the development of the forces of this aggressive front is a major blow to international peace and the collective security system. Its impact includes not only European countries but also the entire world. Although the strength of the peace front is greatly threatened, the forces of "righteousness" will ultimately overcome the forces of "evil," because peace is supported by the vast majority of people worldwide, while the policy of aggression is only actively supported by a small number of ambitious individuals.

Telegram from Dayu: Please inform all newspaper offices that we recently sent a telegram to the generals of Guangdong, saying that we have received a true telegram urging us to have our names listed in the telegram to retain Uncle Bo and not to rush to Beijing. Brothers, do you think this is the only way to care for Uncle Bo? We have shared hardships for a long time. How can we not care for Uncle Bo? In my opinion, this is an emergency, and there is no room for hesitation. Those who truly love Uncle Bo should ask Uncle Bo to immediately obey the orders of the central government and go to Beijing to share the heavy burden and work together to resist aggression. Frankly speaking, Guangdong and Guangxi are using the name of resisting Japan to provoke war. Everyone can see whether they have other intentions. We have been involved in secret affairs. How can we not know? When the狂潮轩起 broke out, the entire country went around mediating, but to no avail. General Yu felt the pain of the wall dispute and feared the disaster of national subjugation. Therefore, he did not avoid dangers and flew to Beijing on庚日 to attend the Second Plenary Session of the Central Committee to work together for unity and save the crisis. The佳电 advocated obedience to the central government, cessation of disputes and resistance to aggression, and public loyalty to the country, which is obvious and inspiring to all who have blood. I believe that the national crisis has reached its final stage. It is still insufficient to resist aggression with the combined strength of the entire country. How can we煎萁豆 and藩篱自抉 and give the enemy the benefit of the fisherman? Only unity can resist aggression, and only resisting aggression can ensure survival. At present, there is no way to save the country other than obeying the central government and uniting. Uncle Bo has always been known for his merits and has been entrusted with heavy responsibilities. At this time of national crisis, he should put the central government first and one corner second, the country and the nation first and personal opinions second. If he can overcome all difficulties, release his troops and go to Beijing, then rumors will disappear, and his reputation will be high. His career and future are unlimited. If he still insists on his own opinions, it will inevitably lead to civil war. Not to mention the difference in strength, the morale is already depressed, and it is clear that people's hearts are trending. It is not necessary to await divination to know the outcome. Brothers, you are wise, how can you not know? If you bend to personal favors, it will only destroy our revolutionary group that has been around for many years. Even Uncle Bo will be ruined. The lesson of the 19th Route Army can be learned. How can those who love Uncle Bo bear to do this? Moreover, if this leads to national and ethnic catastrophe, how will we face our ancestors underground? In short, the situation is critical. We soldiers are supported by the country, and all our actions must be based on the interests of the country and the nation. Otherwise, we will not ask. All of you are outstanding people who know the times, love the country, and love your hometown. For the sake of saving the country and resisting aggression, I hope that you will unanimously urge Uncle Bo to go to Beijing on the designated date to assist the central government, so that the long-cherished ambition of leading the resistance against Japan can be fulfilled. Great situation is fortunate. Sincerely reply, waiting for your clear teaching. Li Zhenqiu, Mo Xide, Ye Zhao, Zhang Ruigui, Peng Linsheng, Deng Qichang, Zhong Fangjun, (stamped)

Germany and Austria Restore Friendly Relations, Italian Diplomatic Victory, The Pre-War Triple Alliance Revived, The Stresa Front Dies Young

Rome The Austro-German agreement is widely regarded as Mussolini's diplomatic victory. Several parties are now mutually questioning "Is this agreement a prelude to a new Italian-German agreement?" Well-informed sources here believe that the term "Stresa Front" will no longer be heard. There are even rumors that the pre-war Triple Alliance has been revived, and Italy is no longer in a secondary position as before. (Reuters dispatch on the 20th)

Berlin Political figures stated today that the Austro-German agreement accomplished what thousands of bombers and the Nazi Party's long-term terror campaign had failed to achieve. In other words, it is the two Germanic peoples standing side by side under the same roof. It is generally believed that Germany will use the prestige generated by the new agreement to gradually instill its ideology and policies into Austria. (National News Agency dispatch on the 12th)

Austria's Foreign Policy Still Conforms to the Spirit of the Covenant, The Right to Independence Will Never Be Abandoned, A Step Further Towards Friendship with Germany, Adjusting Trade Relations Between the Two Countries

Vienna Responsible officials recently declared that the recent agreement between Austria and Germany was originally intended to restore normal relations between the two parties. It is quite surprising that foreign parties have misinterpreted it as Austria abandoning its right to independence or assuming that Austria's foreign policy is about to be controlled by Germany. It should be known that before Chancellor Schuschnigg announced this agreement yesterday, he said that Austria's foreign policy conformed to the spirit of the League of Nations Covenant and was in harmony with the Rome Protocols of Italy, Austria, and Hungary. In short, if Austria wants to follow Germany's foreign policy, it should aim for Germany to abandon its imperialistic and territorial expansion desires. Austria should also promote political evolution through peaceful means. Although Austria considers itself a Germanic nation, it has never been hostile to Germany, even during the most intense disputes between the two parties, but it also does not want to be confused with it. (Havas dispatch on the 13th)

Vienna Chancellor Schuschnigg stated to the Associated Press reporter today that although Austria has signed an agreement with Germany, it does not want to conclude military alliances with most countries. It is natural for Austria to practice friendship with Germany due to their common language and culture. However, Austria will remain completely independent and will continue to pursue a peaceful policy. As for the restoration of the Habsburg monarchy, there is no change, but this move is not intended to be realized by force. The idea of a referendum will also not be implemented if it is considered to affect European peace. (National News Agency dispatch on the 12th)

Vienna Chancellor Schuschnigg announced today that all Nazi political prisoners will be released soon, except for those who have committed crimes that harm the lives and property of others. He also warned the Nazi Party that any actions that endanger the government will be prohibited. At the same time, Schuschnigg announced that Austria will soon negotiate a trade treaty with Germany and that Austria intends to retain its membership in the League of Nations and hopes that Italy will not withdraw either. In the future, Germany may trade coal from the Ruhr region for wood and milk from Austria. Obstacles to travel to the two countries will also be removed. As for the starting point of German-Austrian friendship, it actually began when the current German Ambassador to Austria, Papen, visited Austria in mid-October last year. (National News Agency dispatch on the 12th)

Exchange of Congratulatory Telegrams Between Austria and Germany

Berlin - Today, Chancellor Hitler of Germany received the following telegram from Chancellor Schuschnigg of Austria:

"The establishment of an agreement to restore friendship and normal neighborly relations between Germany and Austria provides me with a great opportunity to extend my congratulations to Your Excellency. At the same time, it gives me the chance to express my confidence in this agreement. I firmly believe that the implementation of this agreement will not only benefit the two Germanic nation-states but also bestow blessings upon the entire Germanic people. I believe that Your Excellency shares my view that this agreement makes a significant contribution to European peace."

Hitler's reply was as follows:

"I greatly admire Your Excellency's opinion regarding the establishment of the German-Austrian agreement. What I wish to say is that after the establishment of this agreement, the long-standing historical relationship and shared heritage between the two countries will be restored, and the two countries can work together to strive for European peace." (National Telegram, 12th)

French Newspapers Comment on the New Agreement: De Facto Merger of Germany and Austria Increases Danger in Europe

Paris - After the establishment of the agreement between Germany and Austria, newspapers are concerned about three things: 1. Germany and Austria have effectively merged in disguise. 2. After the two dictatorships of Italy and Germany unite, they will form a single force from the Baltic Sea to the Adriatic Sea, dividing Europe in two and exerting pressure on the Balkan countries. The previous alliance of Britain, France, and Italy against Germany's actions is now a thing of the past." This is not to isolate Italy and Germany but to eliminate the aggressive ideas of the rulers of those countries. What we should do is nothing other than the establishment of an agreement between Britain, France, the Soviet Union, and Czechoslovakia." For these people, it is imperative to admit their mistakes honestly and try to remedy them." (Havas Telegram, 13th)

Britain Adopts a Cautious View: No Decisions Can Be Made Without Clearly Understanding Everything Beneath the Surface

London - The London diplomatic community is now taking a cautious view of the German-Austrian rapprochement. They believe that the new agreement between the two countries can at least temporarily eliminate a dangerous point, but optimism should not be excessive, as the establishment of the agreement may not completely stop Germany from putting pressure on Austria. However, it is expected that Hitler will change his methods and exert pressure from within rather than from without. Although Austria has declared that it will not allow the National Socialist Party to engage in propaganda in Austria, it is the intention of people in the know that many National Socialist propagandists will now be given freedom. These people may not be willing to remain silent. Mussolini must have known and approved of this German-Austrian rapprochement. Whether Mussolini will now issue a new interpretation of the Four-Power Pact of 1933, which recognizes the Soviet Union's greater influence in European affairs, is also a point of speculation for many. The comments on the German-Austrian agreement in the newspapers here vary widely. The Morning Post stated that the agreement clearly cannot be taken at face value and that there must be ulterior motives. The Daily Mail said that the sanctions faction had forced Italy to ally with Germany and that in the future, we should no longer engage in suicidal interference in matters that are not remotely related to our interests. The British and German authorities should urgently seek a closer understanding. The Daily News welcomed the agreement, saying that it was an action toward European appeasement and could greatly reduce Britain's many obligations in Europe. The Daily Telegraph said that from a superficial point of view, the agreement was a good thing, but no decisions could be made lightly without understanding everything beneath the surface. The News shares the same view. The Daily Telegraph said that we must wait quietly to see the truth. The question is whether the extinguishing of one fire will not ignite a new one elsewhere. The Times welcomed the agreement, saying that Hitler could indeed be congratulated. Regardless of the current motives or ultimate intentions of the agreement, it can be used to appease Central Europe, improve its economic situation, and open the way for a permanent solution between the two major branches of the Germanic people. The Manchester Guardian said that Hitler's abandonment of the plan to merge Germany and Austria was because Germany was not currently willing to risk war and was therefore taking this temporary measure to carry out other plans. Encourage Britain to Join This Group, Otherwise Submission Will Be Repeated

Montreux Conference Holds Plenary Session: Turkish Representative Issues Declaration: New Convention Does Not Necessarily Require Italy's Signature, But Declares Reservation of the Right to Conclude a Separate Agreement

Montreux - The Montreux Conference held a plenary session this morning, during which Turkish Foreign Minister Rüştü Aras delivered a surprising speech, commenting on Italy's refusal to participate in the conference and proposing three points: 1. After the new convention is established, absent countries may not sign and join. 2. Once the draft of the new convention is established, the various clauses contained therein should be universally implemented. 3. After the new convention is established, Turkey may conclude similar agreements with any country based on the principles contained in this convention. (Agence Telegraphique Suisse Telegram, 13th)

The Turkish government reserves the right to conclude a separate agreement with Italy in the future. (China Transcribed News Agency Telegram, 13th)

Turkey argued that they should be treated the same as warships. The conference decided to refer the matter to the technical committee for discussion and adjourned until 4:00 p.m. tomorrow. Failure of the Japanese National Policy Cabinet Meeting: Hirota Plots to Handle the Aftermath; The Deep-Seated Malpractices of Various Ministries Are Difficult to Eradicate; It Is Recognized That Administrative Institutions Need to Be Reformed

Tokyo - The so-called National Policy Cabinet Meeting, which the government intended to use to renew all government affairs and for which it had made careful preparations before convening, was frustrated midway. The government believes that the reason for the failure of this cabinet meeting was that it had not clarified the national defense budget before ordering the ministries to submit draft national policies. As a result, the ministries felt insecure about the feasibility of important policies. In order to solve this fundamental problem, Prime Minister Hirota ordered the three chief cabinet secretaries to study the best method. If their conclusion is to clarify the outline of the national defense budget first, then notify Ministers Terauchi and Nagano of the army and navy ministries to convene a four-minister meeting of the prime minister, finance minister, and the two military ministers to jointly study countermeasures regarding the national defense budget and financial plans. (Allied Telegram, 13th)

Tokyo - The government's National Policy Conference was forced to dissolve after only three meetings due to the rampant pretense of national policy by various ministries. This clearly proves that the current administrative institutions are unable to eradicate the deep-seated malpractices of various ministries and demonstrates the major shortcomings of the current administrative institutions. Among the three chief cabinet secretaries, only the director of the Investigation Bureau has substantial policy proposals. Therefore, the director of the Investigation Bureau assists the Prime Minister in implementing national policies by taking and selecting them, and the national policies produced by the Investigation Bureau are naturally at the center. From this point of view, the issues of expanding and strengthening the Investigation Bureau, establishing a minister without portfolio, and reforming administrative institutions such as unifying the ministries should be re-examined. The government's plan centered on the cabinet meeting has completely failed. In the future, it plans to use the three ministers of Prime Minister Hirota, Finance Minister Baba, and Army Minister Terauchi as the center to decide on national policies. This shows that the current cabinet system cannot determine centralized national policies. In the future, when realizing comprehensive national policies from a broad perspective, it is necessary to impose certain restrictions on the cabinet system based on ministries. (Allied Telegram, 13th)

Drought-Stricken Areas in the United States Receive Rainfall: Nearly a Thousand Deaths Since the Heat Wave Began; North and South Dakota Are the Most Severely Affected

Today, various states in the Midwest suddenly received rain, and the East received thunderstorms. The drought and heat wave are gradually decreasing. Today, the temperature in the shade in New York City is 91 degrees. (Reuters Telegram, 13th)

Chicago - The rain that the people of North and South Dakota had been praying for was bestowed upon the disaster areas today. Iowa and eastern Nebraska have also received rain. However, since the heat wave began, nearly a thousand people have died of heatstroke and drowning in the western United States. The loss of livestock and crops is estimated at 400 million yuan. Many residents of North and South Dakota have sold their houses and equipment and moved elsewhere. There is still rain in the Mississippi River basin. The corn in Iowa is gradually withering, but there are dark clouds in the sky, and it seems that it will rain tomorrow. Today, the disaster area is bounded by North and South Dakota, and the climate is completely different. The climate on the east side is still 105 degrees, while the area that received rain on the west side is below 60 degrees. (National Telegram, 12th)

Page 9

French Democracy Commemorated: People Celebrate with Joy; Government Implements Extensive Social and Economic Plans; Improving the Wealth Distribution System Should Be Successful

Paris - Tomorrow is National Day. Last night, it rained heavily, but the people were already dancing hand in hand on the streets, with a very large number of people. The Socialist Party and the Communist Party also held public celebrations in the Mingyue Park and the Buffalo Sports Ground south of the city, with a large number of participants. (Havas Telegram, 13th)

Paris - Tomorrow is French National Day. Since the establishment of the Third Republic in 1871, this is the first time that the National Day commemoration is being conducted under the leadership of the left-wing Popular Front cabinet. In the Great Revolution of 1789 and the Second Revolution of 1848, the general idea was based on "social justice and freedom." This doctrine, which swept through the 18th century, not only inspired the French people but also had a tremendous impact on the economic life of France and most countries in Europe. The social and economic policies adopted by the current Popular Front cabinet are based on this idea. Its power is derived directly from the people. Therefore, observers believe that 1936 is a major turning point in French economic history. The result may be that France will transform into a "socialist republic," which is clearly different from the bourgeois conservative republic. France was originally a prosperous country, and the people could have enjoyed prosperity under a good economic organization. However, although the country is prosperous, "economic life is not fair," and the economic institutions established by the bourgeois republic should be held responsible for this. Recently, social movements have sprung up, leading to increased wages and improved working conditions. In the eyes of most people, this is not only a "real" victory for the working class in economic terms but also the prelude to the establishment of a new economic institution in France. This new institution is based on a "prosperity policy" and is completely different from the "contraction policy" previously implemented. The current cabinet's recent laws on social issues aim to reconcile the interests of the middle class, farmers, and the working class. At present, the public deeply hates and abhors the credit system and the means of selling short and buying long, believing that the credit system should be monopolized by the government and that the quantity of production should also be adjusted so that the production function can be concentrated in the hands of "real" producers. As for the recent labor unrest, people in various trade unions have repeatedly stated that workers on both sides are able to maintain order and not only do not damage the machinery in the factory but also often lubricate its interior. Their love for the machinery is evident. Therefore, these striking workers should not be seen as the sworn enemies of capitalists; on the contrary, they should be seen as liberators. These workers are so diligent that the output of goods will surely increase greatly in the future. Although the current output cannot be sold in full, the improvement of economic institutions will surely increase the living standards of the people across the country and increase their purchasing power. Furthermore, most of the French working class, including those on the far left, believe that the extensive economic plans that the current Popular Front cabinet has implemented to improve the wealth distribution system will surely be successful, leading France to lead the world's social movement and eliminating the atmosphere of the global recession. (Havas Telegram, 13th)

Smuggling: Southern Sales Route Cut Off, Tianjin and Jinan Still Rampant Smuggling Areas

Now, after customs officials rigorously carried out anti-smuggling operations, the southern sales route has indeed been cut off. According to business circles, one-fourth of smuggled goods from North China are sold south of Jinan, and three-fourths are sold north of Jinan. Central Memorial Week: Chiang Kai-shek Reports on Unification and National Salvation

1. The foundation of diplomacy lies entirely in domestic affairs. Therefore, the unification of domestic affairs is the key to resisting foreign aggression.

2. The Central Government has consistently adopted a spirit of leniency towards the changes in Guangdong and Guangxi, resolving everything through political channels and peaceful methods.

3. The unification of political and military orders is a fundamental requirement for dealing with foreign affairs.

4. The Central Government can never abandon the suppression of internal rebellion due to the severity of foreign troubles.

5. In resolving domestic political problems, both reason and emotion must be taken into consideration, but right and wrong, obedience and defiance, must also be clearly distinguished.

6. The revolutionary government is determined to fight to the end amidst internal and external attacks from beginning to end.

Nanjing - Chairman Chiang Kai-shek gave a report at the Central Memorial Week on the morning of the 13th, titled "Unification and National Salvation." The original text is as follows:

Fellow comrades, today the Central Government is holding the Premier's Memorial Week. I have been asked to give a report, and I would like to share my opinions and thoughts on recent national affairs with you. The Second Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee is currently in session, and all comrades of our party, the general public of the country, and foreign friends all over the world are paying close attention to the results of this meeting. Originally, the most important issues of our meeting were domestic and foreign affairs as the center of the meeting. As for the direction of domestic and foreign affairs, the Fifth National Congress last year already had clear decisions. For the past six months, the Central Government has been working hard based on the directions decided by the Congress, and in the future, we will of course only proceed by following the established directions of the Fifth National Congress. However, we must understand that so-called domestic and foreign affairs, although different in name, are actually a completely interconnected thing. As a matter of fact, there is no distinction between foreign and domestic affairs. It can be said that foreign affairs problems are domestic affairs problems. If domestic problems cannot be properly resolved and the country cannot achieve true unification and lay a solid foundation, there is simply no diplomacy to speak of. Therefore, if we want to solve foreign affairs problems, we must first solve domestic problems. (To be continued) (Central News Agency dispatch)

Central Supervisory Committee: Held Second Plenary Session Yesterday, Passed Regulations on Disciplinary Action for Kuomintang Members and Party Branches

Nanjing - The Second Plenary Session of the Fifth Central Supervisory Committee was held at the Central Party Headquarters at 3:00 PM on the 13th. Seventeen members of the Central Supervisory Committee attended, including Lin Sen, Zhang Ji, Cai Yuanpei, Wu Jingheng, Shao Lizi, and Chen Bijun. Seventeen alternate members, including Lu Dangping, Lei Zhen, Wang Shijie, Li Ciwen, and He Siyuan, attended as observers. Chairman Lin Sen presided. Only two cases were discussed: "Regulations on Disciplinary Action for Kuomintang Members and Party Branches." First, the articles were read aloud one by one. Wang Chonghui, Zhang Ji, Wang Shijie, Qin Zhen, Jiang Zuobin, Wang Zizhuang, and Lu Dangping were recommended to form a seven-member committee to review the cases. The committee adjourned for a recess and then the review committee held a meeting to conduct a detailed review, adding amendments until 6:00 PM when the review was completed. The plenary session resumed, and the amendment passed by the review committee was adopted in its entirety and submitted to the Central Executive Committee for promulgation. After the discussions, the meeting adjourned and closed. The disciplinary regulations consist of eight chapters: Chapter 1 General Provisions, Chapter 2 Accusations, Impeachments, and Reports, Chapter 3 General Rules, Chapter 4 Deliberation, Chapter 5 Appeals, Chapter 6 Enforcement, Chapter 7 Restoration of Party Rights and Membership, and Chapter 8 Supplementary Provisions. (Central News Agency dispatch, 13th)

Because of the death of his father, he did not attend various social gatherings. It is heard that Kong, recognizing the hard work of Chen and others on this trip, has scheduled a banquet for the 14th to show his appreciation. (Special dispatch, 13th)

Nanjing - Guo Bingwen discussed the international trade situation after his inspection in the United States, stating that countries around the world, in view of the decline in import and export goods after the implementation of tariff policies and import restrictions, now, except for Germany and Italy, which still adopt import restriction policies due to exchange rate relations, other countries have gradually moved towards liberalization in international trade. The voice of the so-called reciprocal movement has become very clamorous in our ears. Taking the United States as an example, as a result of efforts in this movement for two years, it has established reciprocal measures with 14 countries including Canada. However, although this liberalization and reciprocal movement is effectively implemented in other countries, whether it is suitable for adoption in our country and how it should be adopted still needs detailed discussion. As for the points that should be improved in our country's international trade, they are: 1. Reducing the trade deficit, 2. Encouraging exports, and there are also two basic ways to encourage exports: (A) Improving the quality of products, (B) Strengthening international trade organizations. Poor quality damages trade credit, and without sound international trade organizations, the promotion of direct trade is particularly fragile. The reporter also asked whether the previously reported news that the United States would form a trade company with China specializing in tung oil and other goods was true. According to Guo, the domestic price of tung oil in the United States is unstable, and there is no accurate statistic on how much our country can produce each year, as well as the issue of quality. Therefore, there was this proposal, but when it will be realized is not yet known. (Central News Agency dispatch, 13th)

County Magistrate Yang Guozhen of Pei County waited at Huzhai to greet them. They inspected along the dam. The construction of the dam has been fully completed. The top of the dam is 3 meters wide and 2.5 meters high, about 1 meter higher than the water level last year. Yongding River Water Receding

Beiping - The water level of the Yongding River was 18 Chinese feet on the 12th. At about 5:00 AM on the 13th, it dropped two feet, and the water mark was 16 Chinese feet by noon. Fortunately, the main torrent has passed. If there is no more rain upstream, the water level is expected to return to normal. However, the lower reaches of the Nan Er Bei Wu and other sections are still not out of danger due to the rapid flow. The river authorities are currently supervising the workers day and night to prevent breaches. (Central News Agency dispatch, 13th)

Tianjin - The water level of the Yongding River receded one Chinese foot on the morning of the 13th. The water level at Lugouqiao was 17 Chinese feet. The dikes and embankments along the river have avoided danger. However, the main torrent at Qujiadian is still rapid, with a water level of 6.64 meters, affecting the siltation work in the Hai River. The North China Water Conservancy Association sent Director Gao Jingying to investigate on the 13th. (Special dispatch, 13th)

Beiping - The water level of the Yongding River dropped one Chinese foot today. The water mark is 17 Chinese feet. Because the main torrent is flowing left and right without being channeled, the situation is still dangerous. (Special dispatch, 13th)

Tianjin Huaxin Cotton Mill: Shareholders Resolve to Sell

Tianjin - Due to poor business performance, the Tianjin Huaxin Cotton Mill convened a shareholders meeting on the 13th and decided to sell immediately. Liu Junqing and Xu Jishang were appointed to be responsible for contacting buyers. It is expected that 30-40% of the capital can be recovered. The mill is one of the six major cotton mills in Beiyang and was considered the most successful in operation among the mills. The reasons for the sale are: 1. Old machinery and no funds for renovation; 2. Shareholders feared that the Japanese cotton industry intended to control the North China textile market and dared not continue to invest; 3. Banks refused to grant loans; 4. Overdue foreign debts were urged too urgently and there was no way to turn around. The shareholders also resolved to work hard to maintain operations before the sale to avoid the plight of thousands of workers. (Special dispatch, 13th)

Misunderstanding Between Chinese and Japanese Troops in Dagu; Swift Handling Prevented Escalation; Our Side Apologized, Japanese Side Understood; Japanese Headquarters Dispatched Personnel Southward to Investigate

Tianjin dispatch: On the 9th of this month, a conflict occurred between the 29th Army stationed in Dagukou and the Japanese army due to a misunderstanding. The authorities responded promptly and swiftly, preventing the escalation of the situation. The details of the incident are as follows:

The Japanese resident army in Lutanggu, the Kagawa unit, consisting of thirty infantry soldiers, conducted a forced march along the Hai River during an exercise on the afternoon of the 9th at 2:00 PM. They rowed a small boat towards East Dagu, intending to land. The 1st Battalion of the Liu Regiment, 133rd Brigade, 43rd Division, under Liu Ruming of the 29th Army, was stationed there. The regiment headquarters of the Yu Regiment was located in that area. The Chinese side had not received any prior notification of the Japanese army's march, nor had they received any orders from superiors to provide protection. Upon seeing the Japanese troops landing, they suspected malicious intent and attempted to stop them. The Japanese army did not listen, leading to a misunderstanding and gunfire exchange, lasting several minutes, without any casualties on either side. Both sides' officers received reports, rushed to the scene, and separately ordered their troops to cease fire. The Japanese army then withdrew. Song Zheyuan was informed that evening and immediately telegraphed Regiment Commander Liu to resolve the matter locally to prevent escalation. On the 10th, Liu visited the Japanese army captain Kagawa, expressed his apologies, and explained the misunderstanding. Kagawa, being understanding, also acknowledged some fault on his side. The matter was resolved tacitly that evening. Song Zheyuan, still concerned about potential dissatisfaction from the Japanese military headquarters, ordered Chen Zhongfu to come to Tianjin to investigate and visit Yongjian. Chen arrived in Tianjin on the night of the 10th. On the morning of the 11th, after Zhang Zizhong summoned Regiment Commander Liu to inquire about the truth, Chen Zhongfu visited Yongjian at the Japanese barracks in Haiguang Temple, explaining the details of the incident. Yongjian, claiming not to have received a detailed report, did not express much, only saying that if the incident was indeed unintentional and a misunderstanding, the Japanese side would not take it seriously. Furthermore, at noon on the 10th, Yongjian, accompanied by Staff Officer Ikeda, Senior Adjutant Otake, and more than 30 soldiers, traveled to Tanggu in six cars to meet with Kagawa and investigate Dagu. They returned to Tianjin at 4:00 PM in the afternoon. Although Tianjin Mayor Zhang Zizhong had no direct responsibility for the matter, he feared potential complications. Therefore, upon hearing of Yongjian's return from the investigation, he ordered Municipal Government Secretary-General Ma Yanchong, along with Japanese Secretary Lu Nansheng, to visit Yongjian at Haiguang Temple to further explain the situation after Chen Zhongfu's visit. Yongjian expressed a positive attitude, hoping that the local garrison would be instructed to prevent similar incidents from occurring in the future. That evening, Zhang Zizhong telegraphed Liu Ruming, ordering him to instruct the 133rd Brigade to send Chief of Staff Zhao to Dagu to gather the garrison and give a lecture. After investigating the incident, a report should be prepared for record-keeping. Japanese Army Commander Tashiro went to Yuzhou and Qin areas on the 9th to inspect the troops. He returned to Tanggu on the afternoon of the 11th to inspect the local troops, and returned to Tianjin in the evening. Although he heard about the incident, he did not express any opinion. Therefore, as of the 12th, the matter seemed to be resolved peacefully.

The Japanese Garrison Army Headquarters in North China recently dispatched Senior Staff Officer Ishii Kaho and subordinate Hamada Sakuyoshi southward. They first attended a meeting of military attachés in China convened by the Japanese Embassy in Shanghai, then went to Nanjing, and then traveled along the Yangtze River basin to Wuhan and Changsha for investigation. On their return journey, they entered Henan via the Pinghan Railway, visiting Kaifeng and Zhengzhou, and were expected to return to Tianjin in about 20 days. Military Attaché Imai of the Embassy in Peiping also accompanied them. (12th)

Strict Prevention of Espionage Activities in Chaozhou and Shantou; Spies from a Certain Country Deeply Penetrating the Hinterland; Extremely Tight Organizations

Shantou dispatch: A certain country is becoming increasingly active in plotting against us, and has formed espionage teams, distributing them to the hinterlands of our various provinces to spy on military intelligence and geographical conditions. Such activities have been discovered in the Chaozhou and Shantou areas. These individuals all speak fluent local dialects, dress no differently from Chaozhou and Meizhou people, and maintain close ties with the poor in the shantytowns. They often marry Chaozhou women, becoming sons-in-law and establishing kinship ties. These individuals secretly provide their wives with living expenses of six or seven yuan per month. It has been discovered that there are approximately 600 registered foreign nationals from a certain country in the Chaozhou and Shantou areas. Those who travel back and forth without a fixed residence and who protect the transportation of goods into the interior number about four or five hundred. These individuals are all veterans who have undergone rigorous training, are directed by their highest authorities, and undertake special missions. It is reported that their organization is divided into five major detachments: North China, Central China, South China, Northwest, and Southwest. Each detachment is divided into three battalions, each battalion into three companies, and a special company. Each company is divided into five or six groups. In the Shantou urban area, which is divided into six public security sub-bureaus, the espionage team is also divided into six groups, each group consisting of approximately five to eleven people. The detachment, battalion, and company commanders are all from that certain country, while the organizational elements are Taiwanese and Korean people. The internal structure of the organization is extremely tight and resembles a military organization. Each company has a mobile instructor who works for a very short time, traveling to Taiwan, Fuzhou, Shantou, Xiamen, Guangzhou, Wuzhou, and other places to train and guide the personnel. Those recruited in China are first allowed to acquire Taiwanese or Korean citizenship and receive some form of guarantee before undergoing practical training. The curriculum includes espionage concepts, research on espionage, military reconnaissance techniques, sky communication methods, disguise techniques, photography techniques, Chinese transportation geography, wireless communication and its usage, Roman character codes, espionage and communication techniques, the psychology of the Chinese people, and social skills for entering public places. The training period is four months, followed by correspondence courses in business, national policy lectures, organizational law, and various general courses. There is even training in handling dangerous situations, giving statements, and so on. It is reported that the composition of the members is extremely complex. The situation in Chaozhou and Shantou has become very serious recently, so the garrison has been particularly vigilant against these individuals. Peng Zhifang, stationed in Chaozhou, convened a meeting of district chiefs and police chiefs of the public security sub-bureaus on the 4th to discuss methods for reporting traitors, spies, and communists and reactionaries, requiring the district and township joint security system to complete the reporting according to the deadline. The methods are as follows: If any villager is found to be acting as a traitor or communist within the territory, the district or township chief should secretly investigate and report them. If any stranger or spy infiltrates the territory, they should immediately be reported to the local district or township office in accordance with the reporting procedure, which will be forwarded to the public security bureau for handling. If any district or township chief intends to harbor or conceal a spy or traitor who infiltrates the territory and fails to report them, they will be charged with the crime of harboring them once discovered. All villagers are responsible for finding ways to assist or investigate. When reporting, the reporter may personally go to the reporting agency to report, but must not falsely accuse due to personal grievances, which may result in a counter-accusation. Furthermore, in Jieyang, Chenghai, Raoping, and other counties, the military and police have been urging the thorough investigation of the population in various villages, implementing armed roll calls and a five-household joint security system. In the future, if one household accommodates relatives from other villages without reporting to the district or township office, all five households in the joint security system will be held responsible once the roll call reveals the violation. The inspection is currently being implemented very strictly.

County-Wide Strike in Wuxi Silk Factories; Party and Government Agencies Dispatched Personnel to Mediate in Thirty-Six Factories Including Wufeng

Wuxi dispatch: Female workers in silk factories such as Wufeng and Ruichang in Gushanbang, Wuxi County, went on strike because their demands for improved treatment from the factories were not met. It is reported that on the 11th, a total of eleven silk factories were on strike, including Dingcheng, Wufeng, Ruichang, Wanchang, Yongxing, Ganshen, Baolan, and Yongsheng, involving approximately 3,000 female workers. The iron gates and glass windows of the Ganshen and Baofeng factories were damaged by the crowd, and miscellaneous items in the workshop of the Yongsheng Silk Factory were destroyed. The director of management, Zhang Xian, was also beaten and injured. Upon receiving the news, the Silk Factory Industry Union of the General Labor Union dispatched personnel to persuade them. The Security Brigade, the Public Security Bureau, the Inspection Office, the Mobile Patrol Team, the Water Patrol Team, and the Second and Sixth Sub-Bureaus of the Public Security Bureau also dispatched officers and led all the police officers to the scene to suppress the crowd. The female workers then went to the Silk Factory Industry Union and put forward four demands: 1. Working hours: Requesting a six-in-six-out system. 2. Restoring the standard daily wage of 57 cents. 3. Four days of reward work per month. 4. Stipulating that work be suspended on the 1st and 16th of each month, and wages be paid on the 15th. The Industry Union fully accepted the above demands and promised to negotiate with the employers immediately. At the same time, Sun Xiangfeng of the Party Committee and Tang Puan, a preparatory member of the General Labor Union, spoke to the female workers and advised them to strictly observe order and wait patiently for mediation. The female workers were satisfied and dispersed. At the same time, Qian Fenghao, Xue Shouyi, Chen Zhanru, Hua Shaochun, Jiang Daoshan, Xue Zukang, Xue Runpei, and more than forty other members of the Silk Factory Association also went to the county government to petition, requesting that measures be taken to stop the strike and requesting protection. Secretary Wang Rongsan received them and promised to relay the situation to the county magistrate, convene a negotiation between labor and management with the Party Department, and make a round-table solution. If the workers took any out-of-line actions, they would be strictly dealt with according to the law. At this point, the representatives left. On the morning of the 13th, the female workers of twenty-five silk factories, including Dacheng, Minfeng, Zhenyi, Yichang, Yuji, Qianfeng, Gongda, Sanxing, Guangcheng, Jiatai, Longchang, and Taichang, continued the strike. Only the Ruilun and Luzhuangzhen silk factories in the Yuqi rural area continued to operate normally. The female workers of the Taichang Silk Factory in Nanmen suddenly clashed with the police officers of the Third Sub-Bureau of the Public Security Bureau on the morning of the 13th. As a result, more than ten female workers were injured, and those who were seriously injured were sent to Puren Hospital for treatment. The rest were gathered at the Labor Union, asking for relief. County Magistrate Long Tiyao, due to the expansion of the turmoil, ordered the dispatch of security teams to suppress it and ordered the Public Security Bureau to pay close attention and take effective precautions for the sake of public order. Hua Yanchen, a shareholder of Yongsheng Silk Factory, reported to the court due to the heavy losses suffered by the factory, requesting an inspection. The chief prosecutor of the County Procuratorate led the bailiffs to conduct an on-site inspection and confirmed the facts, as a basis for verification. On the side of the Silk Factory Association, an ad hoc meeting of representatives of silk factories was convened at 6:00 PM on the 13th to discuss solutions, and the situation of the female workers' strike was reported to the Second District Commissioner's Office, the County Government, and the County Party Department, requesting action. However, the workers remained firm and stated that they would not give up until their goals were achieved. County Magistrate Long of the County Government, in order to resolve the labor dispute, convened a mediation meeting of representatives of labor and management at 5:00 PM in the afternoon, urging the representatives to order the workers to resume work first, and then discuss and resolve the issue of improving treatment and increasing wages.

Suzhou: Counterfeit Currency Operation Busted

Wang Jisheng, a 36-year-old from Yancheng, an unemployed vagrant, recently set up a secret operation at No. 34 Old Changshu front gate in the city to counterfeit banknotes and corner notes, distributing them to accomplices to sell in the villages. The villagers, unaware, were often deceived by him. The scheme was discovered by Director Pan of the Second Public Security Sub-Bureau, who sent Inspector Shen and police officers on the night of the 12th at around 11:00 PM. They captured the main offender, Wang Jisheng, on the spot, and also apprehended a woman, Wang Hao. Counterfeit Central Bank and Bank of China subsidiary currency notes, as well as counterfeit one-yuan banknotes of the Chinese Workers' and Peasants' Bank, and counterfeit currency seals were seized and taken to the sub-bureau. On the 13th, they were escorted to the Public Security Bureau. After being interrogated by the Judicial Section, they were transferred to the local court for legal proceedings.

Kunshan: Provincial Government Inspectors Arrive in Kunshan

Wei Zhiqi, an inspector from the Jiangsu Provincial Government, arrived in Kunshan from the province on the morning of the 11th. He went directly to the County Government to visit County Magistrate Peng, inquiring in detail about county administration matters. Subsequently, Wei Xuchu, chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, paid a visit to report on the commercial situation of the county. Wei's visit was to supervise the collection of funds for the purchase of aircraft for birthday celebrations, and he took the opportunity to inspect various agencies that afternoon. He left Kunshan that evening.

East Pavilion Double Lotus in Full Bloom

The double lotus in the East Pavilion of the Justice area of the county was hand-planted by the Ming dynasty recluse Gu Dehui. It has a long history and is extremely precious. Now, in the height of summer, the double lotus is about to bloom in full splendor, charming and moving. It is very interesting to visit and enjoy the scenery, so the number of visitors has gradually increased, and it is expected that the scene will be even more spectacular than in previous years.

Wuxi: Fire Destroys Eight Homes

The home of Shi Asong, a resident of the third Jia, first Bao of Luqu Bridge Town in the fourth district, suddenly caught fire at 4:00 AM on the 11th, burning through the roof and spreading to the homes of Feng Houyan, Sha Zhonghu, Feng Wangzhen, Feng Yushan, Liu He, Feng Peisheng, and Feng Xijin. The fire was very fierce. The local fire brigade responded to the alarm, drove dragons to the scene, and drew water to extinguish the fire. It took three hours to put it out, but the above eight houses had already been reduced to ashes. Among them, the losses of Feng Yushan, Liu He, and Sha Zhonghu were the most severe. As for the cause of the fire, it is said that Shi Asong's family was cooking mianyi bing (a type of pancake), and the remaining fire caused the accumulation of firewood to ignite.

Changzhou: Bandits Extort Huge Sum

Xu Guirong, the head of Laonan Township in the first district of Wu County, recently received two identical letters of intimidation delivered by mail, demanding 3,000 yuan and setting a deadline for payment, otherwise, his life and property would be in danger. Xu then came to the city to report to the First Public Security Sub-Bureau, requesting apprehension. The director of the sub-bureau ordered the police chief of the Fourth Precinct, Li Yuyan, to investigate. Police Chief Li immediately led plainclothes police to the vicinity of Yang Bridge, west of Zhouzhuang Village, and laid an ambush on all sides, waiting until midnight. He vaguely saw a person emerging from the reeds, immediately stepped forward to capture him, and searched him for iron tools, a straw basket, and a cloth bag, which were brought to the precinct together. Under interrogation, he identified himself as Mao Shengda, admitting only to theft and not to extortion. He was escorted to the First Sub-Bureau and transferred to the local court for interrogation on the 12th. The search for the perpetrators of the intimidation case is still underway.

Changshu: Education Bureau Director Accused

Chen Yue, the director of the Education Bureau of this county, has been suffering from a serious illness since mid-April of this year. He has been bleeding from his mouth and nose all day long. He had applied for leave to the Education Department. By the time of the term change, the duties of the bureau were all presided over by Jiang Yinghuai, the director of Social Education. The education sector is very dissatisfied with this. Now, Chen Yue's illness is even more critical, but the bureau has instead applied to the higher authorities to cancel his leave. In fact, Chen is bedridden and unable to go to the bureau to work. Now, the public has listed ten major facts of the Education Bureau and reported them to the department, requesting a thorough investigation. The Education Department has ordered the bureau on the 11th to order Chen Yue to make his own statement.

Baimao Sluice Gate Scheduled for Completion

The Baimao Giant Sluice Gate in this county, which is related to the water conservancy of seven counties in Jiangsu Province, was allocated 400,000 yuan by the National Economic Commission and started construction in Zhangjia City in this county in February of this year. As of today, it will be five months, and 70-80% of the gate foundation and other projects have been completed. If the weather is not rainy, the entire project can be completed in early August. The project office has tentatively scheduled the inauguration ceremony for August 10 and reported it to the Economic Commission for approval.

Hangzhou: Large Whale Donated to Museum

The large whale displayed at the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway City Station, weighing approximately 40 tons, has now been donated by the Railway Bureau to the West Lake Museum for display, so that anyone can visit. On the evening of the 12th, the museum borrowed a crane from the Hangzhou Power Plant to start unloading and transporting. It was not completed until dawn on the 13th. The museum will set up a special room specifically for the display of the large whale.

Fire at Zhakou West Lake

The home of Yu Linyuan, a resident of No. 11 Ganshui Lane, Zhakou, caught fire due to carelessness with mosquito coils at around 12:00 PM on the 12th. In an instant, the fire spread and was beyond approach. At that time, due to the strong northeasterly wind, the fire was even more fierce, taking advantage of the wind. Residents were awakened from their sleep, and they did not even have time to move their belongings. Cries shook the sky. The fire brigade and the fire station arrived one after another to rescue, but due to the lack of water source, they connected to the reservoir of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway, which was about three miles away from the fire, and used belts to draw water to extinguish the fire. It was not extinguished until 3:30 AM. It is estimated that 53 houses, a total of 81 households, were burned down, with losses of more than 50,000 yuan. Also, the home of Wu Meisheng, a resident of Tongli Bridge, Maojiabu, West Lake, caught fire again due to the re-ignition of Maochai ash at around 4:00 AM. After going back to rescue, the fire was extinguished at 5:00 AM, burning down 11 houses, with losses of about 10,000 yuan.

Ningbo: Yao Salt Police Suffers Further Harm

After the Yiyao Light Tax Salt Patrol Team had three salt patrolmen killed and thrown into the river last month, the case has not yet been solved. Unexpectedly, the salt patrol squad leader Zhou Youquan and Xing Yueqiao led Ding patrolmen to suppress smuggling in the Hengxi area the other day. They were surrounded by a large number of smugglers, who gathered and beat them, and took away their guns. As a result, except for one patrolman who managed to escape in the meantime, Zhou Youquan was hit on the head, and his brain matter flowed out. Xing Yueqiao's eyes protruded, and all his front teeth fell out. They both died one after another, and one patrolman was seriously injured. The smugglers then left triumphantly. After receiving the news, the office immediately sent a team to transport the casualties to the city and report to the hospital to apprehend the perpetrators.

Strictly Implement Comprehensive Investigation of Opium and Drugs

The Yin County Government and the Ningbo Public Security Bureau, upon receiving provincial orders to eliminate the remaining opium and drugs in the territory, from the 11th of this month to the 25th of this month, will jointly conduct investigations from house to house with the district and baojia heads, still allowing for lenient supplementary registration. After the investigation is completed, from the 26th of this month to August 4th, the Ningbo Public Security Bureau will conduct a review, ordering the elimination of drug atmosphere by the deadline.

A Beautiful Anecdote from the Southern Tour

— Special Correspondent Shi Ying

North Mountain Waterfall

Scenic spots and historical sites throughout the country are of utmost importance to the nation's culture. According to a survey by the Ministry of Interior, Zhejiang Province has the most scenic spots and historical sites, totaling 1,872. Among these, eastern Zhejiang is particularly rich, and within eastern Zhejiang, North Mountain in Jinhua is the most famous.

North Mountain is fifteen kilometers from the city. The mountain is full of rocky caves and gushing clear springs and waterfalls, making it easy for vegetation to thrive, painting the outskirts into a beautiful, lush, and majestic picture. The local people who "live off the mountain" even try to blast open the rocky cliffs, burn them into lime, and carry them to the city to sell. Lime is a fertilizer, and it's the season for fertilizing fields. Along the way, you see children of twelve or thirteen, all carrying small loads to sell. After all, they are young, and the way they hurry with small steps, hunched over and panting, looks truly pitiful.

A secluded path leads into a mountain trap, and the sound of rushing water is like music played by the mountain spirits, constantly playing for you. The outer cave is spacious like a deep star, about four or five yards high and wide, and about six or seven yards deep. There are five clear springs that flow out from the small opening of the inner cave. Sweating profusely, you feel cool and refreshed the moment you enter the cave. The inner cave is entered through that water outlet. The opening is only four or five feet in diameter and is almost completely filled with the water flow. In search of this eerie, dark water cave, it is said that if you boldly venture inside, you'll find a spectacular view in a fire palace. Don't say you don't believe it. Even Xu Xiake, when he came to visit, probably didn't go in, but kept his honorable legs outside the cave. I leaned back, lying in a specially made wooden basin, and nearly scraped off my nose as I rowed in. It was about two yards long. I left the basin and went ashore, and looked in the light of the gas lamp. It really was another world. If you wanted to use it to hide from iron birds dropping eggs, you could hide at least five thousand people. Stalactites and rocks lined the walls, a dazzling sight. Two rock veins rose from the top of the cave, one blue and one yellow, twisting and dancing, very much like dragons. They had heads, tails, scales, and claws, truly lifelike. This cave is named Dragon Transformation Cave because of this, and the flowing water is called Dragon Transformation Spring Water. Continuing to twist, turn, and slip westward, there are even more strange and bizarre shapes, some resembling lions, elephants, phoenixes, and turtles, too numerous to mention. Following the east wall, you can turn back from the original entrance. The journey is about half a mile.

Leaving Double Dragon Cave and climbing up another slope, only half a mile away, you arrive at Ice Kettle Cave. Double Dragon Cave is horizontal, like a gourd lying on its side, with a large mouth, a very thin waist, and a wide, flat rear. The heart is strange and bizarre. Ice Kettle Cave is vertical, with a small mouth and a large, deep belly. Step by step, you carefully descend the stairs, counting 260 steps (stone steps carved on the spot). After descending the first twenty or thirty steps, the sunlight gradually dims and darkens, and a cold air strikes. You faintly hear the sound of gurgling water. Descending another thirty or forty steps, you suddenly see a large waterfall about ten yards long pouring down from the rock wall at the top, the sound rumbling like thunder. Ice flowers and jade fragments splash on your body, like a fine rain. The water power stirs up a hidden wind, making you want to turn back in fear. But if you summon your courage and go down, you can walk behind the waterfall. At the point where the waterfall falls, there is no deep pool of water. Looking up at the cave entrance from behind the waterfall, a pale line of skylight illuminates the waterfall into a crystal curtain, making you feel an indescribable sense of comfort and beauty. Other waterfalls are outside the mountain, but this one is in its belly. I'm afraid it would be difficult to find such a spectacular sight again, even after traveling through all the famous scenic spots in the country. Continuing to step down a sloping two or thirty steps, you see the water flowing quietly from the bottom of the cave, said to come from True Morning Cave and flow down to Double Dragon Cave. The three caves are all on the same mountain, all facing west. This theory is very plausible. When turning out, the gas lamp light accidentally touched a bat cave. Hundreds of them flew wildly.

True Morning Cave is two miles above Ice Kettle Cave. Fearing that going there would delay my return, I only sat in the Ice Kettle Pavilion outside Ice Kettle Cave, asking the guides about the situation. This cave is also called Upper Cave. The words "Thirty-Six Heavens" are carved at the entrance of the cave. The cave entrance is open and bright, with many inner caves branching out. The places that tourists often visit are about a mile deep. The cave path is flat, sloping, wide, and narrow, without any certainty. Generally, about one or two miles deep, there is a half-moon-shaped hole that allows light to pass through. It is called a "Line of Sky." Further inside, at "Celestial Pool" wall, there are the words "Stop Here" carved, which are said to be written by Zhu Wen Gong.

The Ice Kettle Pavilion mentioned earlier was newly built by Luo Zhuoying, commander of the Eighteenth Army. Tourists entering Ice Kettle from the heat or exiting Ice Kettle from the cold all need to rest in this pavilion for a while. The pavilion is not yet finished and has no plaques or couplets. It is said to be called "Ice Kettle Pavilion." Is this the case? Later, when I saw Luo in Qu County, I forgot to ask him again. Below the pavilion is Golden Flower Temple. According to research, it was formerly known as Cloud Screen Taoist Temple, founded by Cheng Zhou. Anqisheng in the states of the warring period and Chisongzi of the Jin Dynasty both ascended to immortality here. It was renamed to its current name during the Tang Dynasty, and was then submerged in the Yuan Dynasty. The current site was newly developed in 1933 by local Huang Weishi and others. It is a hotel in nature, and can provide tourists with accommodation and food. Nearby, there are also famous scenic spots such as Lecture Hall Cave (where Liu Jun of the Southern Dynasties studied), Deer Field Academy, Stone Chessboard, Pan Spring, and Elixir Refining Mountain. Therefore, there are many tourists in spring and autumn.

Jinhua's Dou Niu

Jinhua is not only beautiful in its scenery and products, but also has a considerable position in Chinese historiography. The so-called Eastern Zhejiang School originated here. However, although Jinhua has always had a strong literary style and developed school education, there is a superstitious custom among the people called "Dou Niu." Every winter and summer rainy season, it is still held from time to time. When the fighting starts, the sound travels far, and the spectators are as thick as the mountains and sea. The enthusiasm and encouragement are several times stronger than any ticketed sports meeting. Although it is said that it does not have much meaning.

Dou Niu, broadly speaking, is also called Cao Niu. When fighting, each bull has a special name. Some are called Wu Song, Weicheng, Su Tianba, or Xue Rengui; some are called Hero Hanging, Moldy Face, Big Actress, or Little Anything. The cattle-raising farmers take their fancy, and announce them on the program of performances. In the eyes of the bull owners, a bull that is about to go out to fight is no longer just a bull, but simply a brave general who can stand out, break through the enemy, make a name for himself, and show glory to his master. In the few days before this great general is about to make a "bull" contribution, the master truly has the attitude of "unclothing to clothe him and offering food to feed him" when it comes to the feeding problem. Every meal must be a well-cooked pot of glutinous rice porridge, mixed with a few taels of opium. Or add ginseng soup and fine wine to the meal. In the hot summer, he also helps to scratch his itch, swat flies, and fan him to cool off. At night, he must hang a cloth tent for him to prevent mosquitoes from disturbing his sweet dreams. It is said that this can greatly increase the power of the bull general, making him brave and invincible on the battlefield. As for the money spent, even borrowing is not a problem. The bull general's power greatly increased, and the bull owner certainly could not ask for more. However, if the bull goes wild and kicks and injures the audience, it is not a good thing. Therefore, the bullfighting field is not selected on a vacant flat ground, but in a rotten and sticky paddy field. During the fight, the bull generals are led in pairs in order, each using their horns to butt each other. If they are slightly tilted and about to butt their necks, a fair person will correct them, and they will continue to butt until one bull cannot support himself and retreats. Only then will the outcome be initially determined. Afterwards, they will have to come back twice, and the overall ending will be announced at the end of the game. At the same time, there is more than one pair of bulls fighting. Each pair fights in their own territory and will not affect other pairs, which is the function of mud binding their hooves.

For the bull that wins the fight, the owner will drape red silk on his tall and upright horns, insert golden flowers, and announce the victory. At that time, the bull owner, with his eyebrows dancing and face flushed, leads the mighty bull general, truly with the spirit of a "top scholar parading the streets on horseback", feeling that there is no equal. Relatives, friends, or spectators are bound to use paper cannons and red flowers to congratulate him. There are also those who lead sheep and carry wine to recognize the "bull-in-law", with an enthusiasm that is even greater than that of the in-laws of children. Afterwards, as the saying goes, "when the birds are gone, the good bow is hidden", the bull general who has removed the golden flowers and red silk is of course invited back to the stable to eat old grass. If the bull general does not understand the owner's intentions and is unwilling to put in a lot of effort on the battlefield, so that he is defeated in "three declines and exhaustion", or is blindly led by someone into a cement beach, and after kissing each other with the enemy general, he seems to know that they are both of the same kind, and is unwilling to let others provoke and harm each other, then after returning, he will definitely be considered unlucky by the cruel owner and driven into the slaughterhouse.

It is said that this bullfighting trend has been passed down since the time of Emperor Renzong of the Song Dynasty. The intention is to thank the gods. It is also said that the land in Jinhua and Yiwu counties is hard (it is not known why). If there is no bullfighting, it is easy to suffer from fire, or a murder case will occur. The land in Lanxi is not hard. Once, there was a fire during a bullfight, and afterwards, no one fought. Years ago, at the Jinhua Railway Station, a grand bullfight was held at the opening ceremony. People from Shanghai and Hangzhou came to visit. Recently, in a certain village on the border of Jinhua and Yiwu, it is rumored that a bullfight is about to take place again. But in this severe heat, who has the mood to watch these stupid creatures fighting each other?
