Local News

Guangdong Air Force Pilots Tang and Tan Arrive in Shanghai Yesterday Evening to Report to Authorities in Nanjing, Announcing Chen Jitang's Ten Major Crimes

Dagong News Agency reports that since the military disturbances occurred in Guangdong Province, all military officers have opposed Chen Jitang's improper measures, regarding the lives of the nation and its people as child's play. They have left Guangdong one after another and returned to the Central Government. At about 9:00 AM yesterday, Tang Xiawei and Tan Xiaoyan, pilots of the Fourth Squadron of the Guangdong Air Force, arrived in Shanghai on the Coolidge Presidential Liner of the Dala Company. After staying at the New Asia Hotel to rest, they took the express train to Nanjing at 11:00 PM that evening to report to the authorities. Tang and Tan met with the Dagong News Agency reporter alone, detailing the process and showing a telegram to the Central Authorities, as well as a written original announcing Chen Jitang's Ten Major Crimes. These are recorded separately as follows:

Telegram to the Central Authorities: Chairman Lin of the Nanjing Central Party Headquarters, Chairman Jiang, Chen, Li, Bai, and other rebels are ostensibly using the beautiful name of resisting Japan and saving the country, but are secretly taking up arms to create chaos. Every air force comrade is heartbroken. Now that the country is in a difficult situation, ending the conflict is the way to resist humiliation, and unification is the way to seek survival. Xiawei and Xiaoyan swear to be the vanguard. We are eagerly awaiting orders. Pilots Tang Xiawei and Tan Xiaoyan of the Fourth Squadron of the Guangdong Air Force, respectfully.

Chen's Crimes: To be forwarded to all compatriots across the country by the newspapers. The rebel Chen Jitang has raised troops in Guangdong, using the name of resisting Japan to carry out the reality of betraying the Central Government. All enthusiastic compatriots are indignant. Xiawei and Xiaoyan, serving in the Guangdong Air Force, have dedicated themselves to the Party and the country, always taking protecting the country and its people as their duty, and never knowing what private tools are. Chen's rebellion is not only a disaster for the country and its people internally, but also incurs international contempt externally. Xiawei and Xiaoyan are driven by their duties and blamed by their conscience, unwilling to be used by others to do evil against their conscience. Therefore, they resolutely leave Guangdong and ask the Central Government to punish the rebels. Here, we respectfully disclose Chen's crimes as follows: Rebelling against the Central Government, Chen Jitang has been occupying Guangdong for many years, using the Southwest organs to restrain the Central Government and treating the Central Government's orders as insignificant. This is his first crime. Selling silver, since the Central Government implemented legal flaws, Chen took the opportunity to collect more than 90 million in silver from the people, not as a fund for legal tender, but sold it to people from a certain country to purchase arms. This is his second crime. Over-expanding the military quota, the Guangdong army originally had three armies, but since Chen raised the banner of resisting Japan, he has expanded four or five armies, hoping to expand his strength to resist the Central Government. This is his third crime. Issuing paper money indiscriminately, Guangdong Province collected only more than 90 million in silver, but Chen issued more than 200 million in mixed paper money. According to the regulation that 60% of the cash is a reserve fund, he has indeed committed a crime. This is his fourth crime. Destroying education, Chen has devastated education in Guangdong Province in every possible way, such as owing the salaries of provincial and municipal teachers for more than half a year. Recently, he has even failed to assess his abilities and has strongly supported Zhongshan Middle School, oppressing outstanding students. This is his fifth crime. Levying miscellaneous taxes harshly, Chen has been entrenched in Guangdong Province, harshly levying miscellaneous taxes, without leaving a single gap. For example, Guangzhou collects a full month's rent for housing, and there are more than three months in a year. This is his sixth crime. Transporting smuggled goods, Chen Weizhou uses warships or anti-smuggling ships to travel between Guangdong and Hong Kong to transport smuggled goods. This is his seventh crime. Harming loyal people, Chen is small-minded and suspicious, secretly executing loyal people at any time. The recent murders of Wu Cangsang and Wang Yangchong are clear evidence. This is his eighth crime. Purchasing real estate, Chen has been entrenched in Guangdong Province for several years, scraping the people's fat and blood for his own use, and has purchased millions of houses in Hong Kong. This is his ninth crime. Believing in demon magic, since Chen appointed his brother Chen Weizhou, he has become particularly superstitious about surveying and physiognomy. Anyone who wants to get a job from Chen must be evaluated by Chen Weizhou, who looks at his physiognomy and arranges his eight characters before hiring him. This is his tenth crime. In addition, there are also crimes such as controlling public opinion, raping popular will, deducting salaries, killing young people, and forcibly occupying Hong Xiuquan's tomb. It is impossible to record all the crimes. This is just what Xiawei and Xiaoyan have seen in their daily lives, exposing them to the people of the country so that they can all know that this evil warlord only knows how to devastate the people and cannot take on great responsibilities. If this rebel is not eliminated for a day, the country will never have peace. I hope that the Central Government will make plans as soon as possible to eliminate the rebels. Xiawei and Xiaoyan, whose duties belong to the military, should do what they should do, and dare not resign even if they are wading through boiling water. We respectfully inform you, hoping that you will examine it. Pilots Tang Xiawei and Tan Xiaolai of the Fourth Squadron of the Guangdong Air Force, respectfully.

Continued Arrivals from the North: Furthermore, Mr. Tang told the Dagong News Agency reporter that there were a total of more than 280 air force personnel in Guangdong Province. Now, they are all dissatisfied with the authorities' actions and have resigned one after another. It is estimated that more than 20 people have already entered Nanjing, and the rest of the personnel will also take ships north one after another.

Silver Syndicate to End at the End of the Month, Most of the Money Has Been Returned, the Remainder Will Be Returned This Month

The Jiangzhe Spring Silkworm Cocoon Loan Syndicate, organized by the financial community of this city in the 25th year, includes 20 institutions such as the China Communications Bank, the Four Banks Savings Association, the Postal Savings Bureau, and Fuyuan Money House, with a total investment of 30 million yuan. The general office is located in the General Office of Communications, and branch offices are located in the Bank of China in Wuxi and Hangzhou. Loan registration began on May 10 and ended on June 10. The amount of money released has exceeded 10 million yuan, of which Jiangsu Province accounts for 80% and Zhejiang Province only accounts for 20%. After the fresh cocoons in the two provinces were collected, the loans were returned one after another. The general office reimbursed each lending bank at any time. It is known that the amount already returned has reached 80 to 90% of the total loan amount, and there are still more than 200,000 yuan. It is expected that it can be repaid within this month. It is heard that the syndicate plans to hold a meeting at the end of the month to handle the closing matters.

Consular Body Requests Revision of the Draft Agreement on Factory Inspection, the Bureau of Public Works Has Informed the Municipal Government

Faithful talk about future negotiation steps, this case is difficult to get a final solution at one time

Regarding the draft agreement on the Factory Law in the inland factories of the Shanghai Public Concession, it has not been approved by the Consular Body. The leader and consul Bai Hezao Nan sent a letter to Arnold, the General Manager of the Bureau of Public Works, requesting revisions to our side, believing that it cannot be applied to the Enjoy Sound Agency. The reporter visited Faithun yesterday to inquire about everything. Fei was the representative of the Bureau of Public Works in negotiating this agreement draft. He has done his best to support this case, but he has not been understood by the Consular Body. Of course, he is unhappy. After investigation, the Chinese side of this case entrusted the Municipal Government to handle it through the Ministry of Industry and Commerce. Now, the Municipal Government and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce must consult with each other and wait for a negotiation strategy to be obtained. Ask the Central Government for instructions before continuing negotiations, and it may be difficult to get a final solution at one time.

Murder of Japanese Resident Xuan Sheng, Talk by Responsible Person of the Municipal Government, Orders the Public Security Bureau to Offer a Reward for the Arrest of the Murderer, the Public Security Bureau Engages in Detective Work Day and Night

Central News Agency reports that regarding the stabbing of Japanese resident Xuan Sheng Kuangzuo on Dusiwei Road and Qimei Road on the 10th of this month, yesterday, the person in charge of the Municipal Government issued a statement saying that since the stabbing of Japanese resident Xuan Sheng Kuangzuo occurred, the Municipal Government has decided on detailed and concrete measures for arresting the murderer and strengthening the protection of Japanese residents, ordering the Public Security Bureau to strictly and earnestly implement them. It is hoped that the murderer will be arrested and brought to justice soon, the content of this case can be revealed, and the citizens of China and foreign countries can live and work in peace and contentment. However, in this autumn of national crisis, I deeply hope that the people will flash the serious state of national crisis, follow the correct path of patriotism and saving the country, and obey the entire policy of the Central Government. Those who disregard the overall situation, violate the repeated instructions of the Central and local governments, and engage in actions that harm the country in the name of saving the country, the Municipal Government will enforce the law strictly and will never tolerate them.

Reward for the Arrest of the Murderer

The Municipal Government believes that the case has occurred for several days and has not been solved, so it issued a strict order to the Public Security Bureau yesterday to offer a reward for the arrest of the murderer. The original order of the Municipal Government is copied as follows: The case of the Japanese resident Xuan Sheng Kuangzuo being robbed and killed near Dusiwei Road and Qimei Road on the 10th of this month has been strictly ordered by the Bureau to arrest the murderer in this case quickly and carefully protect the Japanese residents in the case. It has been three days since the evening of the incident. The results of the investigation have not yet been reported. A reward should be set up to arrest the murderer as soon as possible. The reward is as follows: The police detective who leads the team to arrest the murderer and accurately confirms the information will be rewarded with 2,000 national currency. The person who knows the news and reports it, thus arresting the murderer and accurately confirming the information, will be rewarded with 1,000 national currency. The Bureau should immediately comply with and report it. This order, July 13, 1936.

Special Team Handling

After the Municipal Public Security Bureau received the strict order from the Municipal Government to investigate and arrest the murderer, it immediately gathered its cadres in the bureau to set up a special team to handle this case. Day and night, they engaged in investigation, interrogation, and evidence collection. In the section near the road built across the border, where there are many Japanese residents, the Public Security Bureau has also added patrol police to travel back and forth to provide protection.

The Three-Nation Goods Group Gave a Farewell Banquet Last Night for the Nanyang Inspection Team and Requested Minister Wu of the Ministry of Industries to Give Instructions

The Nanyang Commercial Inspection Team, organized by the China Industrial Foreign Trade Association, has been fully prepared since its inception. The group of fifteen people, with over two hundred boxes of goods, is led by the head of the delegation, Mr. Gao Shiheng. They are scheduled to depart on the 16th aboard the "Tjipanoek" of the Java Mailboat Company. Last night, the United Association of Machine-Made National Goods Factories of this city, the Shanghai National Goods Movement Association, and the National Goods Production and Sales Association jointly hosted a farewell banquet for the team at the Jinlong Hotel, and invited Minister Wu of the Ministry of Industries to give instructions. Details are recorded as follows:

Purpose of the Trip: According to Mr. Gao Shiheng, the head of the delegation, in an interview with the Central News Agency, Chinese trade is lagging behind. To seek development, the Nanyang Commercial Inspection Team was formed. Its purpose is to investigate the commercial conditions in various parts of Nanyang as a basis for development, to establish national goods companies in major ports in Nanyang, and to strive to improve the quality and manufacturing methods of national goods in preparation for foreign trade. The expenses for this trip are five boxes, which will be distributed by over thirty factories and exhibited in various ports in Nanyang in turn.

Government Support: Overseas Chinese have high expectations for national goods. Because China has had very little export trade in the past, it has been difficult for overseas Chinese to purchase them. The commercial responsibility of this delegation is very heavy. It is hoped that it will achieve considerable results so that it can move forward step by step in the future. This morning (that is, yesterday morning), I visited Minister Wu of the Ministry of Industries and reported everything, which was met with great concern. On the evening of the 14th, I will go to Beijing with Chairman Zhang Huikang of the Association to ask for instructions, and it has been decided to depart on the 16th for a period of three months.

List of Team Members:

The delegation consists of fifteen people. The list is as follows: Head of the delegation Gao Shiheng (Meiya Silk Weaving Factory), Deputy Head Hu Shicheng (Huachang Steel Refined Factory), General Affairs Zhang Zuyin (Washeng Electric Appliance Factory), Accountant Zhuang Maoru (Family Industry Cooperative), Public Relations Xu Xuejie (China Chemical Industry Cooperative), Secretary Yang Chong, Li Shenyan (Xingye Ceramic Tile Company), Lu Zixian (Meiya Silk Weaving Factory), Deng Qiyao (Yonggu Paint Manufacturing Company), Xu Zhaolin (Yakang Sock Factory), Jiang Junrui (Sino-French Pharmacy), Gao Juxin (Forest Rattan Willow Straw Utensil Factory), Zhou Guojun (Tianyuan MSG Factory), Wang Gongquan (Tianxiangweibao Factory), Zhu Qizu (Kangyuan Biscuit Factory, will join in Singapore), etc., a group of fifteen people, representing more than thirty factories.

Inspection Schedule: The delegation has now received many welcoming telegrams from overseas Chinese groups in various parts of Nanyang. The inspection locations are designated as Manila, Surabaya, Batavia, Singapore, Penang, and Siam. If time and funds are sufficient, they will go to Medan. The schedule is as follows: Depart from Shanghai on July 16th, arrive in Little Luzon on July 23rd, stay for 14 days, leave Little Luzon on August 6th, arrive in Surabaya on August 13th, stay for 7 days, leave Surabaya on August 20th, arrive in Batavia on August 20th, stay for 10 days, leave Batavia on August 31st, arrive in Singapore on September 31st, stay for 12 days, leave Singapore on September 16th, arrive in Penang on September 16th, stay for 5 days, leave Penang on September 22nd, arrive in Siam on September 23rd, stay for 10 days, leave Bangkok on October 3rd, arrive in Singapore on October 15th, stay for 10 days, leave Singapore on October, arrive in Hong Kong on October 22nd, and return to Shanghai on October 26th.

Farewell Last Night: The Shanghai National Goods Movement Association, the United Association of Machine-Made National Goods Factories, and the National Goods Production and Sales Association hosted a farewell banquet for the delegation at the Jinlong Hotel at 7 p.m. last night and invited Minister Wu Dingchang of the Ministry of Industries to give instructions. Guests included Minister Wu, Hu Xiyuan, Zhi Xue, Xiang Hongchang, Xu Ruoruo, Lu Qianyi, Chu Yaoyao, Wang Xingyao, Cheng Shouzhong, Ren Shigang, Xiang Kangyuan, Zhang Huikang, Zhang Zuyin, Yang Chongxun, Zhu Bochen, Pan Yangyao, Gu Yixin, Youcai, Zhang Shenzhi, Li Kangnian, Sun Daosheng, Huang Renzhi, Chen Junwu, Gao Shiheng, Qi Yangnan, Xu Xuejie, Li Shenyan, Wang Gongquan, Gao Juxin, Deng Qiyao, Lu Boyu, Xu Xiaochu, Jiang Junrui, Hu Shicheng, Zhuang Maoru, Tang Qiongxiang, and more than thirty other people. Hu Xiyuan, Wang Xingyao, and Cheng Zongzhong formed the presidium.

Chairman's Speech: Chairman Hu Xiyuan rose to give a speech, stating that the three associations of this city jointly hosted a farewell banquet for the Nanyang Commercial Inspection Team, and invited Minister Wu of the Ministry of Industries to come and give instructions. The national goods business in our country has made considerable efforts in recent years. The delegation has a very important mission on this trip. To develop national goods, we must first understand the needs of the outside world and seek overseas promotion. The purpose of the Nanyang Commercial Inspection Team is to introduce national products to overseas Chinese in various places to comfort their ardent hopes.

Minister Wu's Speech: Minister Wu Dingchang gave instructions, stating that the members of the Nanyang Commercial Inspection Team are striving for their careers and are admirable. Thirty years ago, Chinese businessmen occupied a considerable position in the international arena, but later gradually declined, almost to the point of being unable to recover. The reason for this is that Chinese businessmen only knew how to struggle individually and could not unite, and were therefore unable to compete with others, leading to lagging behind. It is rare for domestic businessmen to form an inspection team to go to Nanyang for inspection in our country, but compared with advanced countries, it is still far behind. However, although the inspection team is behind, it is better than sitting still and doing nothing. The plan for now is to hope that all factory merchants will unite, concentrate their strength, and seek common development, learn from the backwardness of national goods, strive forward, and move forward step by step. Huang Renzhi and others also gave speeches, and the banquet ended at about nine o'clock.

Income Tax to Be Levied Next Month; This Year's Collection Estimated at Five Million Yuan

The income tax promoted by the Ministry of Finance, its draft has been amended and passed by the Legislative Yuan. The reporter specifically inquired from the financial circles in this city yesterday. The tax rate is expected to be implemented next month. All procedures have been prepared by the Ministry of Finance, and the preparatory office of the Ministry of Finance will preside over the levy, divided into three items: profit, salary, and interest. The amendments made by the Legislative Yuan include changing the total profit to net profit under the profit item, and changing the original rate of one dime for every ten yuan from thirty yuan to one hundred yuan under the salary item to five cents for every ten yuan from thirty yuan to sixty yuan. The tax revenue has been included in this year's budget by the Ministry of Finance. It is estimated that the first year of collection will yield five million yuan, and will gradually increase to twenty million yuan in the future, which is a major source of revenue for the national treasury.

Sujia Railway to Hold Inauguration Ceremony Tomorrow; The Railway is Seventy-Five Kilometers Long; Inauguration Ceremony to Be Held Tomorrow Morning

The Sujia Railway, which was planned and built by the Ministry of Railways, has been completed and tested several times, and the results are exceptionally good. The Jinghu and Huhangyong Railway Administration has been ordered to manage the matter on behalf of the Ministry. It was originally scheduled to open on the first of this month, but due to procedural delays, it has been rescheduled to officially open tomorrow morning. According to a reporter from the Industrial Society who inquired from the Railway Administration yesterday, the railway is located between Suzhou Station on the Jinghu Railway and Jiaxing Station on the Huhang Railway, starting from Suzhou and ending in Jiaxing, with a length of seventy-five kilometers. There are eight stations in between, including Wuxian, Xiangmen, Wujiang, Baqi, Pingwang, Shengze, Wangjiangjing, and Jiaxing. The one-way trip takes only two hours and fifty-six minutes. There are four mixed trains running in each direction every day. The up trains (from Jiaxing to Suzhou) are scheduled to depart at 2:00 a.m. and 6:00 a.m., and the down trains (from Suzhou to Jiaxing) are scheduled to depart at 7:20 a.m., 10:30 a.m., 2:20 p.m., and 5:30 p.m. The passenger fares are set at an exceptionally low price. In the future, the railway will connect with the Jingkai and Kaijing intermodal services. Passengers traveling from the customs to Beijing can take the Sujia Railway train from Jiaxing Station to Suzhou and then transfer to the train to Beijing. Its speed is unmatched by other railways. It is reported that a grand ceremony will be held when the railway opens.

Ministry of Communications Approves the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Budget for This Year; Totaling 6,974,093 Yuan; Reduced by 250,000 Yuan by Order of the Ministry

Since Cai Zengji took over as General Manager of the state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, it has thoroughly tightened its belt, rigorously laid off employees, and eliminated waste. In terms of shipping, fuel (i.e., coal used by each ship) has also undergone precise testing and strict assessment, and the amount of consumption has been stipulated, saving a huge amount annually. In terms of business, expenditures have also been restricted and repeatedly reviewed. Now, after review by the Ministry of Communications, it has ordered a further reduction of 250,000 yuan from the total expenses, stipulating that the actual expenditure shall be 6,974,093 yuan. Any remaining amount will be included in the depreciation item, so that old wharves, warehouses, and old ships can be depreciated and modified annually without being included in the cost. The Su-Zhe Railway Bondholders' Association Telegraphs the Zhejiang Chamber of Commerce for Assistance; Please Telegraph the Ministry of Railways to Oppose Discounted Repayment; Will Not Cease Until the Principal and Interest Are Fully Repaid

Regarding the Ministry of Railways' allocation of 800,000 yuan from the new Huhangyong loan to repay the 1,580,000 yuan of previous Su-Zhe Railway shares and debts, the Su-Zhe Railway Bondholders' Association believes that the Ministry of Railways' rash announcement of discounted repayment, disregarding the original debts, greatly affects the interests of the bondholders. In order to jointly maintain creditor's rights, it once sent personnel to Hangzhou to consult with the bondholders, and the results were unanimously opposed. They also appealed to various organizations and groups, vowing not to rest until the principal and interest are fully repaid. It is reported that Jin Shifan, Wang Weigao, Chen Shangpei, Gao Shenxing, and others, holders of the Zhejiang Railway Company's bonds, telegraphed the Zhejiang Provincial Chamber of Commerce yesterday, requesting permission to telegraph the Ministry of Railways to fight for their rights. The original text is as follows: (Titles omitted) The report states that the Ministry of Railways has announced the reorganization of the former Zhejiang Railway Company's bonds and the repayment of principal and interest, and the discount repayment method it has set is difficult to accept. These bonds were originally needed for the urgent completion of the Yong section at that time. Bondholders and others responded with patriotism and love for the railway, investing their daily sweat and blood. According to the history of the Zhejiang Railway, they were the ones who contributed to the initial establishment and maintenance. Now that the Zhejiang Railway is operating with huge annual profits, the government has profits, and employees have bonuses, while bondholders' principal and interest have been suspended for eighteen years, and the losses are already not small. Now, they are repaying by discounting the securities, causing the initial founders and maintainers to bear huge losses alone, which is unreasonable, insensitive, and detrimental to the national credit. We have always admired your association's efforts to protect merchants' rights without reservation. In addition to organizing a bondholders' association and issuing a notice, we specifically request that your association promptly telegraph the Ministry of Railways to fight for our rights, and we vow not to rest until our mission is completed, awaiting your command.

The Farmers Bank of China Relieves Various Counties in Border Provinces

The Farmers Bank of China was established to revive agriculture and rural areas, and is endowed with the right of issuance by the government. All banknotes of the bank are allowed to be used in the same way as the legal currency of the Central, China, and Communications Banks, and it is designated to focus on helping the rural economy in remote provinces and regions such as Shaanxi, Gansu, Sichuan, and Yunnan. Therefore, the bank has established branch banks or offices in these provinces and regions to handle agricultural loan business, which has been quite effective. It is now learned that President Chiang has ordered the bank to allocate 200,000 yuan as soon as possible to handle loans and relieve the victims, because the counties of Longshan, Laifeng, Enshi, and others on the border of Hubei, Hunan, and Sichuan have suffered greatly from the banditry, and the people's production is in extreme distress. After receiving the order, the bank has instructed the branch banks in the respective areas to engage in handling production loans to provide relief.

New Rice Is Prone to Mold and Cannot Be Stored; Rice Prices Fall Back; A Drop of Seven Corners in the Last Two Weeks; The Opening Market This Morning Remains Weak

Rice prices in this port have tended to fall back. In the past two weeks, it has fallen from a high of twelve yuan to eleven yuan slightly. The reason is that the current rice stock in Shanghai is still sufficient, the market is soft, and it is the mold season. The new rice cannot withstand storage, so people are rushing to sell. The opening rice prices in the northern market this morning are summarized as follows: Changbang White Glutinous Rice (i.e., Special Grade No. 1 Rice) highest eleven yuan three corners, lowest ten yuan, Thin Rice highest ten yuan seven corners per stone, lowest ten yuan one corner, Bian Yuan (i.e., Sticky Rice) highest ten yuan seven corners per stone, lowest ten yuan four corners.

It is also understood that the Association's operating expenses require funding. Yesterday, based on the Executive Committee's resolution, separate letters were sent to various organizations requesting financial assistance to facilitate its operations. The original letter stated: 'We hereby inform you that the Association's purpose is to assist the government in combating smuggling, safeguard tax revenues, and revive commerce and industry. Since the formal establishment of the Executive Committee through the joint meeting of various organizations, the first Executive Committee meeting was held on July 8th to appoint Standing Committee Members and Department Heads to actively work. Regarding the necessary funding, it was resolved that each organization would undertake to contribute (with a minimum of five yuan). This matter concerns public assistance in combating smuggling to maintain market stability. We respectfully request your organization to provide financial assistance to facilitate our operations. We earnestly hope for your support.'"

Chamber of Commerce Asks Ministry of Finance to Ban Smuggled Cigarette Paper

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, noting the discovery of smuggled cigarette paper in Shanghai, telegraphed the Ministry of Finance to report the situation and request measures to prevent and stop it. The telegram read: "To the esteemed Ministry of Finance in Nanjing: On the 11th of this month, according to a letter from the Paper Trade Association, since rampant smuggling has prevailed in North China, smuggled cigarette paper has been discovered in Shanghai. As a result, the domestically produced cigarette paper of our member, Minfeng Paper Mill, cannot be fully sold. Although no smuggled goods of other papers have yet been discovered, in the past four months, the sales volume of our members' paper shipped to North China has decreased by 60% compared to previous years. Areas within the Jinpu and Longhai Railways, such as the provinces of Shanxi, Shaanxi, Henan, Hebei, and Shandong, are the most prosperous regions for our paper sales in the north. However, since the rampant smuggling, the sales of both domestically produced and Western paper in these areas have almost completely ceased. Furthermore, large commercial ports along the Yangtze River have also experienced the intrusion of smuggled goods, which will severely impact the entire operation of our industry. Moreover, currently, the small quantities of foreign and domestically produced paper that our members ship to various places are often mistakenly identified as smuggled goods by the anti-smuggling offices, resulting in frequent detentions. We have reluctantly appointed a specialist to review and inspect paper samples batch by batch, investigate whether taxes have been paid, and issue certificates after confirming that they are not smuggled goods. However, the procedure is cumbersome, and our members find it inconvenient. Cigarette paper is mainly sold to mechanized cigarette factories. Formal cigarette factories have rules and restrictions on the purchase of cigarette paper, with strict audits. However, home-made cigarettes are very scattered, and some may risk purchasing smuggled goods in violation of regulations. Based on the aforementioned information, we request that your ministry instruct the relevant authorities to devise thorough fundamental auditing measures to prevent smuggled cigarette paper from gaining a foothold in Shanghai. As the association stated, the area within the Jinpu and Longhai Railway lines is almost entirely affected by smuggling. Although this only applies to the paper industry, other industries can be inferred similarly. We request that your ministry instruct the Anti-Smuggling General Office to deploy strictly and increase anti-smuggling forces at the important stations along these two railway lines. The import licenses originally specified various imported foreign goods listed by your ministry. However, now, domestic and foreign goods are often not distinguished, which may lead to potential abuses and fail to effectively stop smuggling. Instead, it may hinder the circulation of domestic products. We also request that your ministry devise simple and appropriate measures to avoid harassment. This would be most fortunate. Sincerely, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce."

Reporting of Opium Smokers to Be Completed by Deadline; Unregistered Smokers to Be Prosecuted; Public Security Bureau Issues Final Notice for Opium Smokers to Come to Their Senses; Commissioner's Office Scheduled to Close at the End of August

The deadline for the registration and reporting of opium smokers in this city is fast approaching. In addition to continuing to implement strict reporting measures, the Municipal Public Security Bureau has decided to issue another reminder. The details obtained by the Dagong News Agency reporter are as follows:

Opium Smoker Registration Deadline Approaching

The Municipal Public Security Bureau, having begun the general registration and reporting of opium smokers on May 10th of this year, in accordance with the order of the Military Affairs Commission, has reached the two-month mark to date. The originally set three-month deadline will soon expire next month (August) on the 10th. In the past two months, the Anti-Drug Commissioner's Office of the Anti-Opium General Office of the Military Affairs Commission stationed in Shanghai has been actively assisting and supervising the Municipal Public Security Bureau in implementing the reporting measures. A significant number of opium smokers in the city who had previously failed to register and obtain licenses have voluntarily reported themselves.

Strict Reporting Urges Awareness

Recently, the Municipal Public Security Bureau has found that a considerable number of people within its jurisdiction are evading registration. In addition to continuing to implement strict reporting measures according to the established reporting plan, it will issue reminders to those few opium smokers who still refuse to register within this final month, urging them to finally repent. After the 10th of next month, all opium smokers who fail to register by the deadline will be arrested and sent to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters for prosecution in accordance with the Interim Regulations on the Punishment of Drug Offenses, without any leniency.

Commissioner Ma Liang Returns to Shanghai Today

Mr. Ma Liang, Jiangsu Province and Shanghai Anti-Opium and Opium Smoker Registration Commissioner, reported to the Military Affairs Commission in Beijing on the 10th to report on the situation of the anti-opium administration in Shanghai. According to sources from the Commissioner's Office, Mr. Ma has completed his official business in Beijing and is scheduled to return to Shanghai today to work with the Municipal Government to negotiate the transfer of anti-opium administrative power in the concessions, with the aim of achieving a resolution as soon as possible.

Office to Close at the End of August

According to information obtained by the Dagong News Agency reporter, the establishment of the Anti-Drug Commissioner's Office was originally temporary. As the reporting of opium smokers in this city will conclude on the 10th of next month, the office's mission will also be completed at the same time. Therefore, it is scheduled to close at the end of August and report to the Military Affairs Commission.

Hopeful That This Year May Be Spared From Cholera; As It Is Already Mid-July And No Cases Have Occurred; Highest Summer Temperature Was 97.2 Degrees; 350,000 People Have Been Inoculated Against Cholera

The Shanghai Temporary Cholera Prevention Office issued its second announcement yesterday, stating: "Since the publication of the first announcement on June 3rd, the health authorities of this port have been closely monitoring the signs of cholera. All summer gastrointestinal illnesses have been subjected to examination and stool bacteria testing. Now that it is mid-July, this terrible disease has not yet occurred, which is encouraging. If no cases are found by the end of this month, then the remaining days of summer are few, and we may even be able to pass through safely. In Asia, only two major cities have continuously experienced cholera outbreaks. One is Calcutta, India, which reported 15 cases per week starting from January 4th of this year, and as many as 268 cases per week by May 16th. By July 4th, this had decreased to 52 cases. The other is Bangkok, Siam, which reported 15 cases per week on January 4th of this year, increasing to 60 cases by February 29th, and then gradually decreasing. On July 4th, there were still 6 cases. On average, the cases in the cholera risk areas this year are not numerous. The cold and damp period this spring was very long. Since the beginning of summer, it has suddenly turned hot. The temperature was 95.2 degrees on the 1st of this month, 96.6 degrees on the 9th, and even hotter on the 11th, reaching 97.2 degrees. Humidity has also fluctuated. It was 88 on the 1st of this month, rising to 100 on the 4th and 5th. Last summer, the highest temperature was 100.8 degrees on July 14th, and the highest humidity was 98 on July 1st and 12th. Regarding cholera prevention, clean water supply, vaccination, food management, fly eradication, and personal hygiene are essential. However, housing issues are also very important and should not be overlooked. If the poor lack access to sanitation and cannot live and work in a hygienic environment, they will not be able to understand the way to health and will still use ditch water for washing rice, vegetables, and utensils. To improve this situation, the Mayor of Shanghai has built four model civilian villages in the city over the past three years, each with a plaza for recreation. The rent for the houses ranges from three to four yuan per month and is rented to the working class. One village is located on Zhongshan Road with 330 rooms, one on Pusan Road with 250 rooms, one on Qimei Road with 252 rooms, and one on Damuqiao Road with 158 rooms. The above four locations have a total of 990 rooms, each of which can accommodate at least five people, for a total of about 5,000 people. This number is a small beginning compared to the size of Shanghai. It is hoped that other cities will also actively promote this. The health authorities of Shanghai and the two concessions are making efforts to carry out cholera vaccination. The number of people vaccinated by the end of June is listed below, along with last year's numbers for comparison: (A) Number of people vaccinated this year: Shanghai 200,000 (approximate figures for May to June), Public Concession 82,413 (May to June), French Concession 66,039 (May to July 10th), Health Department of the Two Railways Bureau 8,242 (end of May), total 356,694. (B) Number of people vaccinated last year: Shanghai 210,909 (May to June), Public Concession 84,885 (May to June), French Concession 44,890 (April 16th to end of June), Health Department of the Two Railways Bureau 5,594 (April to May), total 346,276."

Renji Hospital June Report

Renji Hospital's report for June 1936 states: Number of outpatients: 15,494; Number of newly admitted inpatients: 364; Number of inpatient days: 6,116; Average daily number of people supplied with meals: 453; Number of male suicides: 55; Number of female suicides: 48; Number of emergency surgeries: 318; Number of emergency surgeries for accidental mechanical injuries: 49; Number of patients sent by the Shanghai Public Concession Police: 496; Number of patients sent by the French Concession Police: 59; Number of deliveries: 20. According to the above statistics, it can be seen that the number of outpatients in the summer months is no different from previous years, and has even increased by more than 1,000 compared to May. The number of patients sent by the Shanghai Public Concession Police has also increased by 10%. The most common diseases in June were malaria and typhoid, but more cases of lung disease were also found, which may be due to the hot weather. The most interesting abnormal case was a child whose heart was not on the usual left side but was found on the right side. In recent years, we have seen cases that are practically incurable. It is one of the hospital's urgent tasks to have another location to handle such cases, so that their beds can be used for other emergency, curable patients. For example, our hospital has a patient, Mr. Zhang, who has been in the hospital for five years. If he can continue to survive and the hospital cannot prepare another place for him, then it is conceivable that Mr. Zhang will stay in the hospital for another five years. Although Mr. Zhang is unfortunate and has been plagued by illness for a long time, he is still in a good mood, and his excellent influence has benefited many patients in the same ward. However, if the bed he occupies can be vacated, it can be used for countless other short-term patients.

Opium Den Busted on Li Mei Road

Zhao Zhang, a 52-year-old woman from Zhenjiang, is the owner of the Dechang Tobacco and Paper Shop at No. 133, Yaxianfang, Huageni Road, French Concession. Since the government has strictly prohibited opium and drugs, she has taken the opportunity to secretly set up a morphine injection den at No. 16, Jixiangfang, Li Mei Road, specializing in providing injections to lower-class addicts. Recently, it was discovered by French Concession police detective Ni Xiafei. At 9 PM the day before yesterday, he first went to No. 16, Jixiangfang, Li Mei Road, and arrested injection assistant Chen Daomin (42 years old, from Haimen) and customer Yu Wanrong (36 years old, from Yangzhou). Thirteen small packets of morphine, one morphine needle, two needle heads, one glass tube, and ninety copper coins in cash were confiscated. They were taken to the police station. Zhao Zhang was then arrested at the Dechang Tobacco and Paper Shop on Huageni Road, but she had already fled upon hearing the news and was not caught. Only one large packet of morphine, weighing three taels, and nine small packets were confiscated. Yesterday, they were escorted to the Second Special Court, where Judge Zhang Chaozuo conducted the preliminary hearing. The police attorney prosecuted based on Articles 259 and 262 of the Criminal Law, and the confiscated evidence was presented to the court. After the court questioned the defendants, they were ordered to be remanded for further questioning at a later date. The defendants were returned to custody.

Taikang Company Discovers Counterfeit Biscuits; Sues in Court for Losses

Taikang Biscuit and Canned Food Company of this port discovered in May of this year that someone was counterfeiting its Rooster Brand, Pistol Brand, and Tank Brand biscuits, which have been registered and patented by the Trademark Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, and selling them in the market, which greatly affected its business. It then issued a warning in the newspaper and sent people to investigate closely. The day before yesterday, it was discovered that Huatongchangji Food Company at No. 103, Wier Meng Road, French Concession, was privately manufacturing the above three trademarked foods, profiting by deception. Zhu Qinhuai (26 years old, from Ningbo), manager of the Taikang Company branch at Nos. 566 and 568, Xiafei Road, French Concession, reported to the French Concession Police. Police detectives Qin Youyu and Zuo Qihong were immediately dispatched to Huatongchangji Food Company, disguised as customers, to purchase the above three types of biscuits. The company manager, Zheng Yanling (resident of No. 48, Chengqingli, Baier Road), was arrested, and four large cans of counterfeit biscuits, weighing 160 catties, and three sets of molds were confiscated and taken back to the police station. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Eighth Criminal Division of the Second Special Court, where Judge Qiu Huan'ying conducted the trial. Police attorney Fei Xizhen explained the case and prosecuted the defendant for harming agriculture, industry, and commerce under Article 253 of the Criminal Law. The plaintiff, Qinhuai, recounted the previous events and appointed attorney Wang Henggu to file an incidental civil lawsuit, requesting a judgment ordering compensation for losses of 21,600 yuan. According to him, the plaintiff company sells 12,000 catties of biscuits every day. Since the defendant's counterfeiting, business has been greatly affected, with the price dropping from 18 yuan to 16 yuan per 100 catties. Calculated at two cents, the daily loss is 240 yuan, and the total loss for three months is 21,600 yuan. The court verified the statements, questioned the defendant, ordered the opening of the debate, declared the conclusion, and scheduled the verdict for the 20th.

Gangsters Slash Laborers; Dispute Arises During Cool Evening Gathering

Chen Longcai and Wang Yuanhe, both around 30 years old from Anhui, are laborers at various wharves in Nanshi. Chen lives in the Tiger Stove in Fuyu Garden, Kaitaili, Fengji Wharf, Nanshi, and Wang lives at No. 10 in the same neighborhood. Around 11 PM the night before, Chen and Wang were cooling off at the entrance when they suddenly had a verbal dispute with Xu Jinfang, a local gangster. People intervened and dissuaded them at the time, and Xu left in a huff. Unexpectedly, around 10 AM yesterday, Xu invited more than a dozen accomplices, each wielding a sharp axe, and gathered at the entrance of the Changchunlou Teahouse at the Pig Row Wharf, waiting. Before long, Chen and Wang arrived and were attacked with axes by the throng of gangsters, throwing the two to the ground and slashing them indiscriminately. As a result, Wang suffered four axe wounds to the back of the head, right hand, and right leg, while Chen suffered three axe wounds to the back, left, and right sides. By the time the nearby police officers arrived, only one accomplice, Zhao Fusheng, was caught, while the rest fled without a trace. Chen and Wang were rushed to Shanghai Hospital for treatment, and it is reported that their injuries are quite serious and life-threatening.

Missing Japanese National Swimmer, Kamei, Found

The day before yesterday (the 12th) afternoon, four members of the Japanese Domei News Agency went to Takahashi Beach to swim. The beach rescue motorboat, having seen another yacht capsizing in the distance earlier, had set out to rescue it. Swapping Prizes with Counterfeit Cigarette Packs; Arrested; Tobacco Shop Owner Also Detained

The Company Brand cigarettes produced by Ruilun Tobacco Company at No. 9, Lane 150, Kaifeng Road, can be redeemed for household items if a complete set of empty packs and wrappers are collected. Major tobacco shops also act as redemption points. At 11 PM the night before, Tian Kunzhen, a 17-year-old from Zhenjiang, brought twenty empty packs of the Company Brand to Chengchang Tobacco Shop at No. 149, Xinwen Road, intending to redeem them for a prize. Chengchang Shop assistant Yi Fan, seeing that the empty packs were very suspicious, asked Tian to go to the Ruilun Company for verification. After inspection by Company Investigator Dong Cai, it was discovered that the paper of the empty packs was inconsistent and that the patterns on the side of the packs had been added. It was clear that they were counterfeit. The company reported to the Huisi Police Station, ordering the detectives to arrest Tian. Forty more similar packs were found in his pocket. Under questioning, Tian confessed that he was an apprentice at Wanshun Tobacco Shop at No. 174, Xinqiao Street, French Concession. The empty packs were entrusted to him by the shop owner, Cai Hechun, to be redeemed. A fellow apprentice at the same shop, She Weiqing, had redeemed over 300 packs. The detectives, together with detectives from the French Concession Police, went to arrest Cai and She, who were temporarily detained by the French Concession Police. Yesterday morning, Tian was escorted to the Fifth Criminal Division of the First Special Court. Ruilun Tobacco Company also engaged attorney Tang Mingshi to appear in court to file an incidental civil lawsuit. Police attorney Qian Xunjiu explained the previous events and requested that, since the two criminals Cai and She were still detained at the French Concession Police Station, a letter be issued to transfer them. Therefore, the case was temporarily not prosecuted. Only permission for [illegible word, possibly "detention"] was requested. It was also stated that, according to the defendant's confession at the police station, these cigarette packs were received from others for less than one copper coin per pack, while the Company Brand cigarette packs were worth about one cent each. Judge Ye Shengchao asked Tian Kunzhen briefly and approved the [illegible word, possibly "detention"] and rescheduled the hearing.

Shen Zhenshen, a 24-year-old native of Jiaxing, was employed as a relief fund officer at the Xie Shou Xiang silk firm owned by Huang Zuoqing in Puyuan Town, Jiaxing. Huang Zuoqing, after discovering his whereabouts, tracked him down to Shanghai the day before yesterday, going directly to Shenderi, Route Robert to await his arrival. At about 9 p.m., Shen Zhenshen indeed arrived and was seized. Upon questioning, Shen admitted to embezzling 670 yuan from the firm and implicated five other employees in the fraudulent scheme. Huang then went outside and summoned Chinese constables Nos. 163 and 464. Unexpectedly, Shen at this moment swallowed sleeping pills, intending to commit suicide. He was taken to the Putuo Road police station and later transferred to Renji Hospital. Fortunately, he had not taken many pills, and after treatment, he recovered and was taken back to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. He now requested permission to escort Shen back to Jiaxing Court for prosecution and to dispatch personnel to collect him. Robbery Shooting: Chen Jiusheng Dies; Corpse Claimed by Friend for Examination

Chen Jiusheng, a 24-year-old native of Pudong, was the manager of the Xie Yu Cleaning Company (contracted by the Public Works Department for sanitation matters). At 9:55 a.m. on the 10th of this month, he and the company's accountant, Zhu Zhongkang, were traveling by car with 917 yuan in cash, intending to distribute wages to workers at the Binlang Road and Mazaki Road branch offices. Their plan was discovered by bandits, and two robbers, one armed with a handgun, ambushed the company entrance. When Chen's car arrived, the robbers stepped forward to seize 800 yuan in cash. The armed robber shot Chen in the abdomen, causing him to fall to the ground injured. The robbers fled the scene. After receiving a report, the Gordon Road police dispatched detectives to investigate. Chen was rushed to Shilong Hospital for treatment, but he died at 1:20 a.m. the day before yesterday. The body was taken to the forensic examination center on Avenue Foch. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Zhang, appointed by the First Special District Court, arrived to examine the body. According to Zhu Zhongkang's testimony, he was 30 years old, a native of Jiading, and worked as an accountant for the cleaning company. On the day of the incident, he and the deceased were traveling by car to the branch office to distribute wages. He got out of the car first and entered the company. Therefore, he only heard a gunshot and did not witness the robbery or the shooting of Chen. Xi Xinyi testified that he was a colleague and friend of the deceased. Since Chen's family had not yet arrived, he volunteered to claim the body. Prosecutor Zhang concluded that the deceased Chen Jiusheng, male, had indeed died from a gunshot wound inflicted by robbers while alive. The body was released to his friend, Xi Xinyi, upon signing a guarantee.

Central Savings Society to Hold Lottery Drawing Tomorrow

The Central Savings Society has held three lottery drawings since its opening, and all special prizes of 25,000 yuan have been fully guaranteed by the society. The fourth lottery drawing will be held publicly at the City Chamber of Commerce tomorrow (the 15th) at 2 p.m. The special prize of 25,000 yuan will be guaranteed by the society. According to regulations, half a yuan is drawn from each membership to calculate the value of the special prize, so there must be 50,000 memberships to reach 25,000 yuan. Although the number of membership cards included in this drawing does not reach 50,000, the special prize will still be 25,000 yuan, so more than 10,000 yuan must be supplemented. In addition to the special prize, there are also a first prize of 2,000 yuan, a second prize of 300 yuan, a third prize of 200 yuan, and a fourth prize of 100 yuan, each with nine winners, as well as several consolation prizes. Every ten numbers will have at least one prize. Because the prizes are large and numerous, it is easy to win in the lottery, and depositors are enthusiastically joining the society. After the winning numbers are drawn, they will be broadcast on the Shanghai Radio Station of the Ministry of Communications tomorrow afternoon at 3:30, 5:00, and 6:45 p.m. (frequency 1300). Because there is not enough time to fill out the membership cards, temporary receipts containing the numbers are issued first so that they can be included in this lottery. Therefore, those who wish to save can still pay the society to participate in this month's savings.

Cyclone Moves Towards the East China Sea; City Will Return to Heat

The cyclone that originated in the Yellow Sea several days ago passed over Shanghai last Saturday and gradually moved towards the East China Sea on Sunday, causing a sudden cool-down in Shanghai. Yesterday, part of it still hovered, but it finally dissipated last night. After the large-scale summer showers come from Chengdu tomorrow, the city will return to heat. The temperature yesterday was 83.5 degrees, with a low of 71.9 degrees.

Selling Drugs Sentenced to Eight Years; Claims All Morphine Was Purchased From Japanese

Yin Tingyun, from Shandong, recently profited from selling the drug morphine at No. 592, Lane, East West Huade Road. Chinese detective Sun Shaokun found out and secretly went to arrest him the day before yesterday at 9:45 p.m. He found twelve small bags of morphine on him, and a cloth bag, two corners, and 145 copper coins were found on the ground in the lane. He was taken to the Huishan Police Station, and a piece of double-haired subsidiary currency was found in his pocket. The head constable ordered him to be detained. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the First Special District Court. Zhang Shizhu, a lawyer from the Public Works Department, stated that the defendant had previously been convicted of red pills and served a six-month prison sentence. Detective Sun then reported the circumstances of the arrest and presented the evidence for inspection. When questioned, the defendant confessed that the morphine was purchased from a Japanese person in Guantang Lane, Huaji Road, and gave evasive answers to other questions. Judge Zhong Qing sentenced Yin Tingyun to eight years in prison as a warning, and the evidence was confiscated.

British Sailor Beats Rickshaw Puller to Death

Forensic Examination Reveals Skull Fracture; Life of a Chinese is Too Pitiful

Chen Huizhang, a 36-year-old native of Yancheng, who lived at No. 2, Jingde Lane, Hengfeng Road, Zhabei, worked as a rickshaw puller. At about 3 a.m. on the 8th of this month, while soliciting business in front of the British Seamen's Club on Rue Cardinal Mercier, three sailors from the club, who had just returned from a dance hall on Avenue Edward VII in the French Concession, suddenly and inexplicably beat Chen to the ground, causing him serious injuries. When the police arrived, they reported the incident to the Xinzha police station, which dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to investigate. The three sailors were taken back to the police station, and Chen was sent to Renji Hospital for treatment, but he died at 5:45 p.m. on the 12th. The body was taken to the forensic examination center on Avenue Foch. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Zhang Zongru, appointed by the First Special District Court, along with forensic doctors Wei and Zhang, and clerk Wang Zuji, etc., arrived at the center. To clarify the cause of death, forensic doctors Wei and Zhang, together with doctors from the Public Works Department, dissected Chen's body and conducted a detailed examination. The examination revealed that Chen's skull was fractured, and he died from the injuries. Prosecutor Zhang then took testimonies from witnesses Li A Si, Zhou Ri Tang, and Chen Xuezhong, all of whom were rickshaw pullers. They stated that they had pulled the three sailors from a dance hall on Avenue Edward VII, but they had gotten out of the rickshaw before reaching the Seamen's Club and had not paid the fare. Therefore, they did not witness the beating until they went back for the fare and saw the deceased already on the ground. Li A Si also claimed that he was also beaten in the left chest by the sailors at the time and showed a plaster on his injury as evidence. Prosecutor Zhang concluded that the deceased Chen Huizhang, male, had indeed died from injuries sustained in a beating while alive. The body was released to Chen's wife, Chen Zhang, upon signing a guarantee. The British sailors who committed the crime should be investigated by the police and dealt with according to the law.

Notice from the Hydrographic Office: Changes in the Position of Beacons

Hydrographic Office of the Navy Department, Notice to Mariners No. 174: Changes in the position of buoys and leading light beacons at the port of Longkou, Bohai Bay, North Coast of the Republic of China. Date of change: August 1 of this year. No further notice will be given at that time.

Longkou Zhou Buoy: New position: 243 degrees from the Customs flagstaff, distance 1.42 nautical miles, i.e., approximately 120 degrees 18 minutes east longitude, 37 degrees 38 minutes north latitude. Explanation: The above buoy will be moved to the new position on the above date. Other characteristics remain unchanged.

Longkou Inner Harbor Buoy: New position: 236 degrees from the Customs flagstaff, distance 1.07 nautical miles. Explanation: The above buoy will be moved to the new position on the above date. Other characteristics remain unchanged.

Longkou Zhou Leading Light Beacon: New position: 165 degrees from the Customs flagstaff, distance 5.5 chains (every 10 chains equals 1 nautical mile). Explanation: The above leading light will be moved to the new position on the above date. Other characteristics remain unchanged. The rear light bearing is unchanged. When the two lights are in a straight line, their new direction is 84 degrees. Related charts: Navy Department Hydrographic Chart No. 520, Navy Department Coastal Beacon and Buoy Table (Buoys) First Edition Nos. 118 and 119, Navy Department Coastal Lighthouse Table First Edition No. 185. Original reporting agency: Shanghai Customs. Note: The direction given in this Notice to Mariners is calculated clockwise from 0 degrees due north to 359 degrees. However, the direction of the light is calculated from the sea. Light intensity is based on clear weather. Fog signals are only used in foggy weather. If necessary, further explanation will be given. Depth records are based on the datum used in the largest scale chart. (July 8)

Car Plunges into River in Pudong; License Plate Retrieved; Owner's Family Tight-Lipped

At 0:05 a.m. yesterday, a Zilpa car plunged into the Huangpu River at the Jinliyuan Wharf of the China Merchants Bureau in the French Concession. The incident has already been briefly reported in this newspaper. After receiving the news, the French police immediately notified the fire brigade to dispatch vehicles to salvage the car, but it was not recovered. It was not until about 3 a.m. that it was salvaged. A black license plate was found on the car, number 5109 in the concession. The car belongs to Ye Wenfu, a Ningbo native residing at No. 98, Zhexing Lane, Ditsville Road. Reporters have repeatedly inquired at Ye's residence, but the family members have been tight-lipped, only saying that the car is a Buick and that they do not currently employ a driver. Ye himself drives the car when needed. When asked how the car drove to the Jinliyuan Wharf, they replied that Ye had gone to a friend's house for a banquet last night (i.e., the night before last), and the car was stolen by someone, causing the accident. However, according to reporters' inquiries from various sources, it is said that although the car appears to be a private black-plated car, it is actually a clandestine taxi.

Kicked and Then Illuminated with Electric Light; Police Officer's Son Falls into River; Tragedy Amidst Evening Cool

The Shanghai Local Court Prosecutor's Office, according to a report submitted by the Minhang Township Office, which was instructed by the Shanghai County Public Security First Sub-bureau to report for examination. The police officer Yang Dianchen reported that his son Bingsheng, 16 years old, was apprenticing at the Feilong Auto Shop on Jiuguolu in this town. On the evening of the 11th of this month, at about 9 p.m., he went to the railing of the Minhang ferry terminal of the Construction Bureau Highway Management Office to cool off and fell asleep shortly after. However, the ferry manager Zhan Wei Zeng kicked him hard with his leather shoes and shone a 1,500-foot flashlight in his face. After being startled, the child's eyes were violently exposed to the electric light, and he could not distinguish directions, causing him to fall into the river. Zhan did not call for help and left quietly, causing him to drown. The police officer, after hearing the news, rushed to the scene to investigate. Witnesses Li A Fu and Zheng Buyun stated that they were also cooling off at the dock at the same time and witnessed the incident. Zhan denied the facts and claimed that the child died due to fate. The police officer argued with him, which angered Zhan. Zhan then struck the police officer with the flashlight, injuring his wrist. Hearing others say that the flashlight was used to shine on the child, the police officer was even more saddened. The police officer, seeing the object and thinking of his son, was even more grief-stricken, so he snatched the flashlight back. The police officer is over half a century old and only has this one son, and he is the inheritor of three families. The whole family hopes that this son will grow up and inherit the family business. Now, what can the living endure? He recently received a letter from his family saying that his mother is seriously ill and is very concerned about her son. Now that she has heard this bad news in her illness, it is unknown how much grief she will feel. The manager could have woken him up gently, but this tragedy would not have occurred. The manager has indeed committed the crime of causing death by injury. Thinking of this, his heart is broken. He begs the director to ask the court to punish him according to the law and to provide generous compensation. Based on this, he requested the court to dispatch personnel to examine the body. Prosecutor Zhao Chuanjia and examiner Shen Qixiu were appointed and arrived at the scene. They found an injury to the deceased's right eye, which confirmed that he had fallen into the river after being injured and had died. The family was ordered to collect the body and await further investigation.

Young Woman Who Cannot Read Accuses Husband of Fraudulently Obtaining Divorce Agreement; Court Orders Further Hearing After Witnesses Are Subpoenaed

Chen Qiaogeng, 27 years old, residing at No. 350 Qichang Stock, Pudong, and working as a clerk at Chen Bingji Transportation Company, married Bao Huifen, 23 years old, of No. 331 Lujia Ferry, Pudong, in February of the 21st year of the Republic of China. However, in May of this year, he suddenly produced a mutual consent divorce agreement drafted by attorney Cheng Zhengping. Bao Huifen recently hired a lawyer to sue Chen Qiaogeng for fraudulently obtaining the agreement and requested that the divorce agreement be revoked. Yesterday morning, Judge Sun Jikang of the Civil Division of the District Court heard the case in the fourteenth courtroom. Bao Huifen testified, "After marrying Chen Qiaogeng, he disliked me because I couldn't read, so our relationship was not very harmonious. On May 14th of this year, he gave me 500 yuan to go to school and took me to attorney Cheng Zhengping's office on the Fourth Road. He wrote my name and forced me to trace it on four sheets of paper. I thought I was filling out a school application, but unexpectedly, the next day, a public announcement appeared in the newspaper stating that we were divorced. I do not want a divorce, so I am requesting that the divorce agreement be revoked." After speaking, she burst into tears. The judge then questioned Chen Qiaogeng, who testified, "Bao Huifen has always been literate. Because she is very hot-tempered and often goes out, I often advised her, but she would often throw a tantrum and say she wanted a divorce. Therefore, on the morning of May 14th, we first went to attorney Cheng's office to discuss the matter, and in the afternoon, we both went to have the documents stamped. This was a mutual agreement, and we both knew attorney Cheng. Furthermore, my salary is meager; how could I have given her 500 yuan for school expenses? There is no such fact. After the divorce, she took all her belongings. Moreover, the Yangjing Literacy School investigated and found that she claimed to have a primary school education." Bao Huifen then stated, "After going to the lawyer's office, Cheng, Chen Qiaogeng, and his family packed my clothes and belongings into three rickshaws and forced me back to my mother's house. My mother was furious and refused to let me in, so the belongings were sent to the Pudong branch of the police station and only retrieved three days later, which can be investigated." The plaintiff's lawyer added, "All the words 'primary school education' on Bao Huifen's household registration card were written by the defendant; the plaintiff did not know." The defendant's lawyer stated, "Regarding the circumstances of the case, I request that attorney Cheng Zhengping, who handled the divorce, be summoned to testify." The judge ordered that a subpoena be issued, and the case was adjourned for further hearing. The court then adjourned.

Shanghai East District Slum Dwellers Petitioned Yesterday in Separate Groups

After the Shanghai East District Lan Road and other slum areas were ordered by the Free Municipal Council to relocate within one month, thousands of slum dwellers were shocked and frightened upon hearing the news. They have specially appointed representatives to submit petitions to all sectors of Shanghai society, requesting assistance to maintain their livelihoods. Huangpu River to Have a Breakthrough; 12-Foot High Tide; Less Than One Foot from Bund Embankment; Low-Lying Roads Will Inevitably Be Flooded; Date: Morning of the 21st of This Month

According to the dredging bureau's forecast, there will be a high tide of more than 12 feet in the Huangpu River on the 21st of this month, less than one foot from the 13-foot embankment on the Bund. If there is additional wind, rain, and low pressure, the tide may exceed the predicted height, which deserves attention. The predicted time is recorded below. The high tide on the 21st of this month will begin to rise at 10:49 p.m. on the 20th. The rising trend will accelerate at 1:12 a.m. the next morning, with a water flow rate of 1.4 nautical miles per hour. The tide will reach its peak at 1:47 a.m., with a predicted height of 12 feet and 5 inches. The Bund embankment is 13 feet high. Embankments near the 16th pier are less than 13 feet. Therefore, the high tide on that day will not only cause backflow and flooding on low-lying roads, but also potentially inundate low areas of the embankment.

Consultation by National Physician Hu Chunxiang

The Songqing Hall Medical Clinic, located at the west end of Er Ma Road and Shilu Road in this city, was founded by the national physician Mr. Hu Chunxiang. Mr. Hu has been practicing medicine in Shanghai for nearly forty years, and his medical knowledge is profound, especially in internal medicine. His clinic is thriving and has long enjoyed a great reputation. His nephew, Mr. Hu Zhongming, has a family background in medicine and also studied Western medicine. Later, he specialized in the scientific study and experience of venereal diseases. His secret remedies, such as Zhuji Yijianxiao, New Medicine for Gonorrhea, and Baituo Duangen Wan, are exceptionally effective and attract many buyers. The original building of the clinic is being renovated, and it has temporarily moved to the Health Hotel for consultations.

Yang Jixian Commits Suicide by Jumping from Building; Suspected to Have Been Frightened by Robbers; Corpse Inspected by Court Yesterday

Yang Jixian, 44 years old, from Songjiang, opened an oil mill in his hometown and was quite wealthy. Recently, he suffered from a foot ailment, so he came to Shanghai with his son Zhaohua to seek medical treatment. However, on the way to Minhang, he was spotted by bandits, who threatened him with guns. Therefore, after arriving in Shanghai, Yang reported the incident to the Sixth District Public Security Bureau. At 10:40 p.m. on the 12th of this month, Yang suddenly jumped out of the window of room 545 at the Central Hotel on Wu Ma Road, where he was staying. When two of his friends left, the police noticed and immediately summoned an ambulance to rush him to Renji Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective. He died shortly after and the hospital reported it to the Laozha Police Station, which ordered an investigation. The body was then taken to the Feilun Road Morgue. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Zhang was dispatched by the Special First Court to inspect the body. According to Chinese Detective Lu Dagong's report of the previous events, Mr. Zhang declared that the deceased, Yang Jixian, male, had committed suicide by jumping from the building and died. The corpse was handed over to the deceased's son, Yang Bohua, who signed an agreement to claim and bury it.

Traffic Accident on Gonghe Road; Five Men, Women, and Children Injured and Killed

At around 5:00 p.m. yesterday, a truck with municipal license plate 13430, rental license plate 17180, and freight pass 1094 was traveling on Gonghe Road near the Xiaocai Market in Zhabei. As it passed by, a boy about four or five years old was crossing the road. The driver, trying to avoid him, drove the front of the truck into the entrance of the Wei Dasheng fresh pork shop at No. 78, smashing the meat racks. At the same time, it injured a total of five men, women, and children. The patrol police saw this and arrived, taking the driver to the Xinzha Branch Bureau. The injured were sent to Pushan Hospital on Xinmin Road. The driver confessed that his name was Shen Wurong, 24 years old, from Xinghua, and that he drove for the Tongde Lane No. 90 on McTaggart Road in the British Concession. Today, he was loading goods from the Yuncheng Lane No. 10 freight room on South Railway Station Branch Road to be delivered to the Yuanyuan Factory on Changan Road. He was traveling west on Gonghe Road from Datong Road when he saw a child in front of him and immediately turned the steering wheel to the left to avoid him, causing the accident. Among the five injured, one boy died before medical treatment could be administered. The parents of the deceased child identified him as Hang Ada, 46 years old, from Nanjing, who made a living buying pig intestines. His wife, Tao, 34 years old, and the deceased child, their son Changsheng, were only five years old. Doctor Jia Shirong ordered the body of the deceased child to be taken back and placed in Yuqing Lane on Gonghe Road, pending a court inspection. The other four injured individuals include Gao Rixin, a boy, only three years old, from Funing, residing at No. 31 Haichang Branch Road; Gao Xu, 34 years old (Rixin is her son); Xu Baofu, 31 years old, from Jiangyin, residing at No. 78 Gonghe Road, the tenant of the Dasheng pork shop; and Xu's son, Maotou, five years old, who was also playing at the entrance and was injured. Except for Gao Xu, whose injuries were more serious and who is currently hospitalized, the others have been bandaged and discharged.

Sports News

My Country's Soccer Team's European Tour

— Written and Sent by Captain Li Huitang

Rangoon, August 8 (Continued from yesterday)

(June 24) At dawn, the sound of crows in front of the courtyard pierces the ears. Looking into the distance, the crows on the electric wires form a line, like a page of Western sheet music. At 8:00, I recorded old man Xie and Huang manager coming to the dock to pick up Yu Junzhuohua. First, whether the team was approved when passing through Singapore for the competition in Rangoon and India was not properly arranged, so I asked old horse Yu Jun, who knows the way, to go to the two places on behalf of our team to negotiate. The local community in Rangoon prepared the event very well and warmly welcomed us. It was all due to Yu Jun's prior publicity. This morning, Yu Jun returned from Calcutta, India. He said that the various matters there have been discussed and arranged, and they are waiting for us to arrive. At 3:00 p.m., the entire overseas Chinese community in Rangoon held a welcome meeting. The venue was decorated magnificently, and hundreds of people participated, making it an unprecedented event. During the meeting, Consul Cai and the leaders of the overseas Chinese community gave speeches one after another. Director Rong and the reporters stood up to thank them in Mandarin and English. There were also many British people present. Among them was Dr. Gray, who used to work at the Shanghai YMCA and had close ties with Chinese sports. When the 6th Far Eastern Games were held in Japan in the 12th year of the Republic of China, he also accompanied the team to the East as an advisor. Today, we met again in a foreign land, and we almost did not recognize each other. Fourteen years of vicissitudes and changes, we sighed facing each other. At 5:00, we were invited to watch this leisure A-level round-robin match. There is only one football team here, and all competitions are held here. The football field is wide and long, with a red wall thousands of feet around. There are two football fields inside, and the A and B level competitions are held at the same time. The stands are built majestically and have roofs to protect from the rain. The super-class seats are also equipped with fans, and flowers and trees are planted around them, matched with gardening. Its magnificence and spectacle are beyond compare, except for the three Far Eastern stadiums in China, Japan, and the Philippines, and the stadiums in one or two major cities in Australia. In the Far East and Southeast Asia, there is really no one better than it. The arrangement of the field is also very proper. The water drainage is rapid. Unless there is a heavy rain, you will not feel its muddy and obstructive. It is said that the level of football here is very high. There are thirty or forty teams competing in the A level. The Indian team that was selected a few years ago also returned with its feathers clipped, and has not dared to come again. Although what I saw today was not particularly good, their short passes were excellent, the ball control was proper, and the average was quite remarkable. Our team has successive injuries and illnesses, and the forwards feel that their strength is weak. In the upcoming competition, with strong enemies ahead, I am extremely worried. In addition, the overseas Chinese here have even higher expectations. Whether the future is good or bad, I really want to predict it as soon as possible, so as not to be worried and uneasy all day long.

(June 25) The rain master who must patronize once a day has never broken his promise in recent days, but we do not feel annoyed, but rather welcome him, because the weather is cool and the sleep at night is comfortable, so that we do not toss and turn. Today is our first battle. We also asked to postpone the welcome party to another day, so that the teammates could rest and sharpen themselves. At half past four, we changed clothes and went to the football field. The audience was full. It was said that it was already full at half past three and ticket sales were stopped. It is estimated that the total number of people was around 20,000. Our team's lineup that day was as follows:

Bao Jiaping

Li Tiansheng Mai Shaohan

Li Guowei Liang Rongzhao Chen Zhenhe

Zheng Jiliang Tan Jiangbai Li Huitang Sun Jinshun Yang Yongyi

Today's opponent is the English Army Rifle Team, one of the strongest teams in the A level. After taking the stage, our team was unknown to the opponent's reality, and calmly dealt with it. Ten minutes later, Tan, the left forward, got a short pass from the reporter, and shot cleverly. Soon, the reporter also got the benefit of a cross from the right wing and made another contribution. After these two losses, their team launched a fierce counterattack, and their right forward returned a goal. Then Tan Jiangbai volleyed a shot, creating a 3-1 situation in the first half. In the second half, Jinshun went to the meeting alone and returned with success. Before long, the enemy's center forward retaliated with a close shot, making it 4-2. At this time, the ball came and went, and the battle situation was quite tense, but later our team's forwards became very active and broke through four barriers one after another by the reporter alone. The enemy's entire line collapsed. However, before the end of the game, our defense was lax, and the left wing shot another goal, so our team won with a score of 8-3. The overseas Chinese community was beaming and expressed satisfaction with our performance. Even the Western media believed that the art was outstanding and rare to see. Our team's formation on that day was not very neat, but everyone worked hard and worked together, so the kick came from the heart. Although the defense lost three goals, which was the highest record of goals lost in the Southern Tour, each person's performance was also full of their duties. Because of the lack of materials in the front, Jiangbai was forced to be transferred to the team. Jiangbai's heading skills are excellent, taking advantage of unlimited advantages, and good at stabbing, which is very helpful. The whole line's short passes are excellent, and the ball arrives when the person arrives, which is most appreciated by the audience. The reporter made five goals alone, winning the approval of Chinese and foreign people, which is really gratifying. In the evening, we were invited to watch a movie, and we returned together at midnight.
