U.S. Olympic Track and Field Trials: Two Black High Jumpers Break World Record - Six Feet Nine and Three-Quarters Inches (2.07 Meters)

Reuters, New York, 12th - In today's high jump at the U.S. Olympic trials and National Amateur Athletic Championships, two black athletes broke the world record. Johnson of Los Angeles first cleared six feet nine and three-quarters inches (approximately 2.07 meters), followed by Abberton of Ottawa University, who equaled Johnson's record. The previous record of six feet nine and one-eighth inches (2.06 meters) was held by American athlete Mado. Owens, who won the 100 meters and long jump yesterday, completed the 200 meters in exactly 21 seconds today.

Several famous athletes were eliminated, including mile champion Buslan, who finished fourth in the 1500 meters, and Eastman, who finished sixth in the 800 meters. The complete results are as follows:

Miscellaneous News from the 11th Olympic Games

Ling Gymnastics

We have recently received news from Sweden that the country has decided to hold a "mass gymnastics" performance at the upcoming Olympic Games in Berlin, to promote Ling gymnastics (Lingache Gymnansik). This performance is scheduled to take place at 6:45 PM on August 8, after the track and field competition, inside the stadium. Six hundred Swedish athletes, male and female, will participate in the performance. This "mass gymnastics" performance will promote Ling gymnastics' method of educating the body, which is of great importance to the training of the whole body. In Sweden, this gymnastics has long become a mass movement.

Ling gymnastics has many advantages, the most notable of which is its "adaptability." Because of its adaptability, it can be practiced by people of all ages, genders, strengths, and weaknesses, unlike other sports that require various conditions that are not accessible to everyone. To ensure that sports figures from various countries participating in the Olympic Games gain a sufficient understanding of Ling gymnastics, the Swedish National Gymnastics Association has prepared several excellent performances to showcase during the Olympic Games. Sweden is currently preparing to hold six performances at the "International Sports School Association" as a rehearsal, and will also have a special performance by a team of boys and girls aged 11 to 15 and male and female adult teams. Each performance will involve 16 to 24 people. The expanded performance planned by Sweden is unprecedented at the International Sports School Federation, so its performance is sure to add unparalleled glory to the federation.

Olympic Basketball Court

At its recent regular meeting, the International Basketball Association decided to use the basketball court designated by the Olympic Committee for this year's Olympic basketball competition. In addition, another basketball court will be built next to the tennis court next to the stadium, specifically for the finals. After detailed inspection, the court, hoops, etc., were deemed to be quite qualified. The preliminaries and semi-finals will be held on the basketball court set up next to the tennis court. All basketball competitions will be held at 5 or 6 PM, so the location of the court must be chosen to be shielded from the sun. The surface of the court will be constructed with special soil so that it can be played even after rain. The International Basketball Association has decided that all basketball competitions will be held outdoors and is making every effort to ensure that the competition is no less than it would be in a gymnasium.

"Honor Book" of This Year's Olympic Games

The Olympic Organizing Committee will produce an honor book to pass on the names of those who sponsored this year's Olympic Games to posterity. The book will begin with the signature of the German leader Hitler, followed by the signatures of various dignitaries and the names of the first, second, and third place winners in each event. The content of the book will be particularly rich, and the binding will be beautiful, making it a highly valuable souvenir of this year's Olympic Games.

Oak Tree for Olympic Winners

The Olympic Committee for this year's Olympic Games accepted the suggestion of artist Ruth to present each winning country with a small oak tree that can be taken back to their home country for cultivation as a permanent memorial. The tree has been cultivated for more than a year and is very lush, with heights ranging from 70 to 100 centimeters. It is planted in a specially made pot with the Olympic bell and the following slogan burned into it:

Increase the glory of victory, promote deep and light industry

The small oak tree is packed in a suitable carrying case for easy transport and comes with a cultivation guide for future care. During the voyage, the ship's owner is responsible for cultivation. According to past experience, this tree can live and grow in any soil and climate. In this way, this tree can serve as a centennial memorial of the Berlin Olympics.

Bicycle Competition Venue

The original plan to build a permanent bicycle track for the Olympic bicycle competition could not be realized due to unforeseen circumstances. The Olympic Organizing Committee therefore decided to build a temporary track. The track will be open from July 1 to August 9 and is located next to the German Hall on the sports field of the Berlin Sports Association, making transportation very convenient. The track is currently being built by the famous German architect Xu Man, an expert in building this type of track, who has built bicycle tracks in Rome, Berlin, and other major cities. The track is 400 meters long and 6.5 meters wide, with a 3-meter high bank in the curves and a 1.6-meter high edge. The total area is 2,980 square meters. The grandstand next to the track can accommodate 1,500 people, with changing rooms for athletes underneath. The perimeter of the track can accommodate 12,000 people. Construction of the track began on June 15, and public practice on the track can begin on July 1. The Olympic bicycle competition will take place on August 6, 7, and 8.

Visitors to the Olympic Games Venue

Recently, many well-known figures from foreign countries have come to Germany to visit the Olympic Games venue and investigate the preparations for the Olympic Games. Among the most notable are the King of Sweden, the Queen of Denmark, members of the Bulgarian Olympic Committee, the directors of the Finnish Gymnastics and Sports Association, representatives of the French Ministry of Sports, and seven or eight members of the British Parliament and other sports organizations.

Municipal Federation Requests Investigation of Education Fund Case: Municipal Government Approves Investigation of Progress - More Than 170,000 Yuan in Unified Public Bonds Have Been Redeemed - Current Storage at the United University Closure is Not a Fact

(From the Dagong Society) The Shanghai Municipal Government yesterday approved a document from the First Special District Citizens' Federation regarding the request to investigate the case of the 100,000 yuan previously allocated for the Labor Education Fund and properly deposited in the National Bank. According to the submission, the Municipal Labor Education Finance Committee has been instructed to investigate and report. The reply stated that the 100,000 yuan for the Labor Education Fund had been properly deposited in the National Bank. The association stated that the initial allocation from the Municipal Executive Committee was 116,000 yuan in face value of 25 Treasury Bonds, with a current amount of 44,741 yuan. According to a resolution of the Municipal Labor Education Committee, only interest was allowed to be used, not the principal. Therefore, the society deposited the current amount with the United Bank Company, holding a fixed deposit certificate. After it expired on June 1 of last year, it was renewed for two years and has not yet expired. According to commercial practice, it would be difficult to withdraw it rashly. The original submission stating that the company had long been closed is not true. The principal of the 25 Treasury Bonds was gradually collected and used to purchase various public bonds. After the Ministry of Finance issued the unified public bonds, it was legally exchanged, resulting in 178,170 yuan in face value of unified public bonds. These public bonds were all deposited with the Shanghai Silk Industry Bank, holding the bank's No. 34 custody certificate. The accounts of previous sessions of the association have been reported to the Ministry and the Municipal Executive Committee for review and approval. Now, the Municipal Federation's proposal to properly deposit the fund in the National Bank will be submitted to the Ministry and the Municipal Executive Committee for review and implementation after the fixed deposit expires. According to the order, the facts have been stated in detail, and it is hoped that they will be reviewed and approved. The Mayor of the Republic of China, Wu, on July 13, 25th year.

Municipal Education Bureau Bans Xingguang Elementary School: Corrupt Content Leads to Order to Shut Down

Wang Shijie rented a bungalow at No. 4 Tonglefang, Intersection of Puen Ji Shi Road and Mayer Xi Ai Road, French Concession, and opened Xingguang Elementary School. The school building was narrow and dirty, and the content was particularly corrupt. The Municipal Education Bureau found out about this and ordered the school to be shut down because it was opened without approval and the content was extremely corrupt. It also sent a letter to the French Concession Board of Directors to assist in the ban. (According to the French Concession Board of Directors, it often fails to fully assist the Education Bureau in banning schools, resulting in a few schools taking shelter in the Concession and continuing to be corrupted. For the sake of the future of education and the interests of the residents of the Concession, it is hoped that the French Concession Board of Directors will not take it lightly.)

Jia Guanli Receives Honors in the United States

Jia Guanli, a native of Shanghai, is the son of educator Jia Jiying. He graduated from the Taxation College of the Ministry of Finance last summer. Due to a delay in assignment, he went to the University of Colorado in the United States at his own expense for further studies. He always topped his class in every exam. In the graduation exam this summer, he took six exams, ranking first in five and second in one. He won the overall championship and received a Bachelor of Science in Business Administration with special honors. It is said that no one has received this degree in the past three years. The department head praised him as an advanced student from an advanced country at the graduation ceremony and expressed great appreciation for our country's tax schools. It is said that the student plans to go to the Graduate School of Business at the University of Chicago to continue his studies.

(Explanation) (1) Since the 21st year of the Republic [1932], the Ministry of Education has restricted liberal arts subjects, so the number of students in science and engineering has increased year by year, while the number in liberal arts has decreased. Finance: Many Long Positions Liquidated; Gold Futures Decline; Trading to Be Suspended for One Month Starting from the 16th; Commission to Be Changed to One Jiao in National Currency per Bar

The gold market yesterday saw a decline in London spot gold and a lowering of the standard price, with swap points approaching, leading to the liquidation of many long positions, and a renewed weakening. The overall trend was uncertain, resulting in a drop of 2.4 yuan. In the early morning, the overseas silver market saw a slight reduction in the London large bar spot to forward spread, while New York remained flat. The Comex forward silver price narrowed by one to three li. London spot gold fell by four pence. The Central Bank's posted rates were unchanged for both British and American currency, and the customs gold unit fell by seven li. The standard gold bar price was lowered to 1127.6 yuan. Off-exchange pre-market trading opened at 34.0 to 34.5 yuan. Yue Xinxiang sold bars, while Futai Yong slightly purchased. After the opening, short positions were slightly covered, causing a slight rise, but with many long positions selling off, the market gradually declined. The HSBC posted rates were unchanged for both British and American currency and there was much trading. The silver equalization tax was announced, dropping by one fen. Afterwards, there was still a flow of liquidations, continuing the weakness. However, there were many struggles along the way. At noon, the market stabilized slightly after the decline. The afternoon session continued the weakness, but buyers were active for a time, causing a slight rebound, but the final result was still quite calm. Gold trading will be suspended for one month starting from the 16th due to the hot weather, and the commission will also be changed to one jiao in national currency per bar from that date, as already announced. The day's market conditions are recorded below:

The morning opening was at 1134.4 yuan, down 0.8 yuan from the previous close. Yue Xinxiang sold to 34.1 yuan. Yu Kang Dafu Yong purchased bars, rising to 34.6 yuan. Qingfa Yongfu Xing Yongyicheng sold off, falling to 33.7 yuan. HSBC's posted rates were unchanged for both British and American currency, and there was much trading. The silver equalization tax was announced, dropping by one fen. Qingfa Yong Qiafeng Yong Ju Tai Ding Kang sold bars, then falling to 32.8 yuan. Chunyuan Yong Dafu Yong Jiao Heng Yu took advantage of the low price to enter at 33.4 yuan. Shengyuan Yong and others maintained limit orders. The noon close rose to 1132.8 yuan.

The afternoon session opened at 1132.4 yuan. Qianchang Xiang Yicheng purchased bars, rising to 32.6 yuan. Fuxing Yong sold bars, falling back to 32.1 yuan. Yuanmao Yong Ding Kang purchased bars, rising to 32.9 yuan. Qingfa Yong Dafu Yong sold off, falling to 32.6 yuan. After some fluctuation, the closing price was 1132.8 yuan. After the close, the market was stable.

The closing price, based on the Central Bank's standard gold bar price, was lowered to 1127.6 yuan. In terms of the closing price, it was raised by more than 5 yuan, 0.3 yuan higher than last Saturday. The registration price for this month is 1129 yuan, and for August it is 1133 yuan. The morning water compensation was 1129 yuan, and the afternoon was the same price. The price of pure gold was increased by 8 yuan, to 1142.4 yuan. The spot market was stable. Tianjin goods were increased by 15 yuan, and smelted pure gold was increased by 13 yuan, but there were few sellers. Smelted pure gold was increased by 16.7 yuan, sold by Shengyuan Yong to Xinfengxiang Silver Shop for 150 taels. The swap market remained calm.

There was not much off-exchange trading. In summary, Yu Kang Heng Yu Chunyuan Yong Tongfeng Heng Wanxing Hengchang Yong Tongtai Chang Yuanmao Yong Yicheng and others were on the buying side, while Yu Xinxiang Shunli Dachang Xiang Ding Kang Dade Cheng Qiafeng Yong Qingfa Yong Fuxing Yong Xiangfeng Fuyu and others were on the selling side. Dafu Yong advanced first and then exited, while Yuanmao Yong exited first and then advanced.

Looking at the day's market conditions, the market was weak, opening in the morning at 1134.4 yuan and closing at 1132.8 yuan. The highest price was 1134.6 yuan, and the lowest price was 1132.1 yuan, a difference of 2.5 yuan. The result was a drop of 2.4 yuan compared to last Saturday. There are 1,953 bars remaining in this month's strips, with 11 long positions and 9 short positions. The total number of chips for the August term is 12,705 bars, with 45 long positions and 32 short positions. The total number of transactions was 3,514 bars in the morning session and 448 bars in the afternoon session.

Due to the hot weather recently, the Gold Exchange announced yesterday that starting from the 16th of this month, the morning session will be open as usual, but the afternoon session will be closed for one month.

In order to maintain operations, the Gold Exchange announced yesterday that starting from the 16th of this month, the handling fee will be changed to one jiao in national currency per bar. After deducting the broker's commission of 2.5 fen, the Gold Exchange will net 7.5 fen in national currency. However, the Broker's Association has not yet formally held a general meeting to discuss this matter.

Exchange Market: British Currency Flat, US Currency Looser

The exchange market yesterday saw a rise in British and American exchange rates, resulting in British currency being flat and US currency being looser. In the early morning, overseas cables indicated that the London large bar spot to forward spread had narrowed by 0.1875. The New York silver market was unchanged. The Comex forward silver price narrowed by one to three li. London spot gold fell by four pence. British currency rose by 0.25 against the US dollar, and was unchanged against the French franc. The US dollar rose by 0.1875 against the British pound, and fell by 0.01375 against the French franc. The Central Bank's posted rates were unchanged for both British and American currency. The customs gold unit fell by seven li. The exchange market opened in the morning with the near-term selling price of British currency at one shilling, two pence and 0.375, and the US dollar at 30.125 yuan, indicating that British currency was flat and US currency was looser by 0.01325 compared to last Saturday. Although banks were selling, Mobil Oil Company had covering operations. HSBC's posted rates were unchanged for both British and American currency, and the process was peaceful. After entering, interbank trading was more active. The silver equalization tax was announced, narrowing by one fen. Although Chinese merchants slightly stuffed shillings, banks still had appetite, resulting in a lack of change. In the afternoon session, Sassoon Bank was conducting interbank trading of shillings, and the opening was peaceful with not much trading. Market sentiment was tepid, and since the silver dollar was unchanged in both instances, the industry became more of an observer. Extending to the close, the near-term selling price of British currency was one shilling, two pence and 0.375, and the US dollar was 30.125 yuan, indicating that British currency was flat and US currency was looser by 0.03125 compared to last Saturday. The forward market was also the same. Chinese merchants continued to slightly sell shillings, while Mobil Oil Company covered near- and far-term US dollars. Yarn and Cotton: Spot Yarn Buying Turns Strong in the Afternoon; Initial Decline in US Cotton No. 3 Causes Market Price to Fall; Later, Rumors of Market Recovery Lead to Sudden Rise

The yarn market fell in the morning and rose in the afternoon, with the situation still chaotic. Long positions at Run Kang and Feng Tai were continuously increasing their positions. However, overseas yarn and cotton had been rising sharply for several days, and yesterday the upward trend slightly subsided, so some of it was sold off. In the afternoon, rumors of currency inflation resurfaced, boosting confidence and causing the market price to turn from decline to firmness.

Spot Yarn Near-Term Up, Distant-Term Down

The spot yarn market opened before noon with near-month contracts still firm, rising by 0.5 to 0.6 jiao. Bidding for distant-term contracts, considering that No. 3 yarn and US cotton had both fallen back, confidence suddenly loosened, and the market situation changed abruptly. In addition, after the increased special certificate, scattered accounts greatly decreased. Each month fell by more than one yuan, and the second and third sessions were flat. By the close, there was a slight rebound. The result was that near-month contracts fell by 0.1 to 0.5 yuan compared to the previous day's closing price, and distant-term contracts fell by 1.3 to 1.4 yuan. The afternoon session opened with the market stable, falling by 0.1 to 0.3 yuan. November and December reversed and rose by 0.5 yuan. During the second session, each month jumped wildly again by 1.7 to 1.8 yuan. This was because long positions continued to absorb and increase their positions in the morning, and the market again heard rumors of currency inflation, so buying strength increased. By the close, it was heard that spot yarn transactions were not smooth, slightly declining by 0.3 to 0.4 yuan. The result was that each month rose by an average of 1.3 to 1.8 yuan compared to the morning closing price, and distant-term contracts rose by 1.1 yuan. Rumors of Squeezing Short Positions in Old Cotton - New Cotton Returns Slightly by 0.5 Jiao

The rising trend of old cotton in the cotton market is becoming more intense. It is rumored that a certain party will sell 70,000 dan of linters to a certain gentleman, which has already been transferred to the warehouse. Therefore, the rumor of squeezing short positions is very intense. The August contract broke through the 50 yuan mark, but gave up on the new cotton, so the distance between near-term and distant-term contracts is getting farther and farther. As for the needs of the current cotton mill, it is exceptionally quiet.

Old Cotton's Rising Trend Intensifies

The spot cotton market opened before noon with US cotton, which had been rising for many days, falling back by 6 to 10 pound notes, Indian cotton rising by 1 to 3 rupees, and Osaka No. 3 cotton falling by 0.6 to 0.7 jiao. Market sentiment was mediocre, and each month opened at a low price. The downward trend of new cotton was particularly strong. After the second session, old cotton gradually rebounded, with many saying that long positions intended to squeeze the shorts, but distant-month contracts fell downwards. As a result, near-month contracts rose by 0.15 to 0.3 yuan, and distant-term contracts fell back by 0.5 to 0.55 yuan. The afternoon session opened with a large trader limiting the purchase of 10,000 dan of old cotton at 49.5 yuan, causing the market to tighten and rise. The new cotton was affected and rose. After the second session, the momentum of the July and August contracts became stronger and stronger. In the third session, the August contract jumped out of the 50 yuan mark. At this time, Changfeng sold 8,000 dan in one go, but the October new cotton contract fell back. At the close, the old cotton was flat, and the August contract fell back into the 50 yuan mark. As a result, the old cotton rose by 0.45 yuan compared to the closing price of the morning session, and the new cotton rose by 0.05 to 0.25 yuan. Osaka telegram on the 13th, No. 3 yarn futures rose or fell by 0.5 to 0.6 jiao, with the near month at 212.2 yuan and the distant month at 208.9 yuan. Cotton futures fell by 0.25 yuan to 1.35 yuan, with the near month at 74.85 yuan and the distant month at 707.15 yuan.

Bombay Cotton Industry Saw Sharp Rise Last Week

Since the US Cotton Government report was released, Bombay's cotton industry has seen speculators and short positions actively buying due to the benefit to buyers, causing market prices to rise sharply. Overseas inquiries were limited, and exports were average. The spot market was quite active due to buying to cover short positions. Indian yarn mills bought a lot, but the market price of textiles failed to keep up with the rise in the market price of raw cotton. Rainfall was not heavy, and it would be more beneficial if it was sunny and rainy at times. Generally speaking, the condition of new cotton can be described as satisfactory. Food: Wheat Prices Gradually Approaching Foreign Prices

Yesterday's wheat futures market was flat and soft in the morning session, but the decline was still small. In the afternoon session, near-term and distant-term contracts plummeted at the same time. The quoted prices of foreign wheat: Chicago fell sharply by 1.65 yuan to 1.78 yuan, and Canada fell by 1.34 yuan. When the opening price was announced, the supply of current wheat was strong, and the factories were unwilling to open for purchase, so confidence naturally weakened. Therefore, July, August, and September fell by 0.6 to 0.8 yuan. The November and December contracts were still stable, falling slightly by 0.3 to 0.4 yuan. When the afternoon session opened, the current environment was inevitably not good, and the non-industry long positions were dwarfed by the actual selling of the code, so each month fell sharply step by step. In terms of the most distant-term contracts at present, it seems that the price has approached the price of foreign wheat. If the government cares about people's food, it can freely order wheat according to past practice, then speculators will find it difficult to persist. Moreover, this phenomenon is not reasonable soon after the new wheat is released. I wonder if the authorities are paying attention to this. In the current wheat market, the factory appetite is still good, and customers are selling back. The price of Zhongguan goods has increased by 0.1 to 0.2 yuan, and the price of high-quality goods is only 0.3 to 0.4 yuan. The prices are: Nanjing wheat 4.3 yuan, next grade 4.37 yuan, Pukou wheat 4.42 yuan, Huaian wheat 4.49 yuan, Luhe wheat 4.46 yuan, next grade 4.33 yuan, Zhuzhen wheat 4.489 yuan, Hushu wheat 4.44 yuan, Gaoyou wheat 4.48 yuan, Yangzhou wheat 4.367 yuan, Hankou wheat 4.323 yuan, Yanghe wheat 4.5, ship wheat 4.04 yuan, as high as 4.2 yuan. Shan Shen, Da Fu, and Feng each went to 3,000 bales, and Fuxin went to 12,000 bales.

Flour Transactions Virtually Halted

Yesterday's flour market was still calm in both the morning and afternoon sessions. Since it is rumored that the price limit cannot be lifted for a while, transactions between the two sides have mostly halted. Under this situation, long positions will inevitably hoard and refuse to resell at the limit price. Therefore, short positions who urgently need to close are rumored to secretly offer discounts to solve the problem. The prices rumored are different, ranging from 0.5 yuan to 1.5 yuan, but it soon fell to 0.8 yuan to 0.9 yuan, and there was still a lack of acceptance. This situation has no basis and can only be tentatively spoken of and tentatively listened to.

In addition, the current price of each factory is still at 1.5 jiao. In recent days, customers from all over the country have been reduced and are not as urgent as before. Therefore, if we consider the facts, there should be no disputes between the two sides.

New Soybeans Continue to Arrive in Shanghai

Yesterday, another 135 bales of June white soybeans from Hankou and 73 bales of Chengmen soybeans from Jiujiang arrived in Shanghai. The harvest in various places this year is still abundant, and the products are of good color. The market price is also higher than in previous years. The price of Jiujiang Chengmen soybeans is 6 yuan, and the price of Hankou Shan Yuebai is 6.27 yuan, distributed by the Fuzhou gang on this street. There are also new Wenzhou soybeans that arrived on Saturday, but because they arrived late, they did not enter the warehouse, which caused a delay of two days. The soybean products were found to have mold due to the new goods, so the goods were sold off at a reduced price, and they were handled by the Ningbo gang at a price of 5.75 yuan.

Twenty Tons of Pure Antimony Sold

Yesterday, a certain foreign firm sold twenty tons of pure antimony at a price of six hundred and sixty yuan per ton, an increase of about ten yuan from before. It is noted that recently, Changsha antimony merchants have become more bullish due to the changing situation, so they are keen to see a continued improvement in the price of pure antimony.

Spring and Autumn

Speculative Rice Worries about Steaming Damage Leading to Price Cuts and Sales

The market conditions for speculative rice have been declining continuously in recent days, seemingly without end. Yesterday, speculative dealers remained inactive, while local merchants showed no interest. Fearing spoilage from heat and losses in weight due to pests, owners and merchants reduced prices again to expedite sales. As a result, prices decreased slightly by ten to fifteen cents, leading to a slight improvement in trading activity. 4,000 bags of late-harvest Jiangxi machine-milled rice, 1,500 bags of early-harvest rice, and 837 bags of other rice, broken rice, and brown rice, along with 584 bags of Hunan rice and 100 bags of Jiangbei brown rice, were sold off entirely by local merchants. However, the market's overall trend remained flat and weak.

River Rice Market Shows Slight Improvement Due to Cooler Weather, Less Spoilage; Shops Increase Purchases at Low Prices

Yesterday, over ten dealers from the central regions (South Shanghai) arrived with a total of more than 3,000 piculs of goods. Due to overcast weather, market sentiment stabilized slightly, and local sales saw a slight improvement, tightening market conditions. Prices for thick-grained early rice rose slightly, with Southern merchants purchasing over 300 bags of thin-husked rice, stabilizing market trends. Northern merchants also purchased over 600 bags, with prices yet to be announced. Fine-grained rice from Duyang followed suit with a slight increase, showing no significant gains or losses aside from spoilage.

(North Shanghai) Recent hot weather has made river rice prone to discoloration, causing prices to fall daily. Yesterday, arrivals from various river-based dealers were slightly higher, numbering about 34 or 35. As the weather turned cooler, the arrived river goods could be stored for a few days. Shops also slightly increased purchases during this period of low prices. As a result, sales of early-morning white rice showed slight activity, with fresh local white rice prices rising nearly ten cents. Prices for older, less fresh rice remained stable. Arrivals of thin-husked rice were limited, with active sales and firm prices. Arrivals of fine-grained rice were slightly higher, with average sales and firm prices at higher levels. Speculative fine-grained rice remained weak.

Piece Goods: Local Mills' Fine Drills in Short Supply, Prices Rise; Dealers' Purchases Remain Strong

Yesterday, although cotton yarn prices showed a slight recovery, they remained very firm. After sharp increases last week, there was no firm market base until yesterday when prices were set. Dealers purchased actively based on market prices. Local mills experienced significant shortages of stock. Fine drills from local mills saw the largest price increases, rising by 20 cents per piece compared to last week. Fine cloth, market cloth, and 84 cloth also rose by 15 cents per piece. Light-weight coarse cloth and coarse drills rose by 10 cents, while heavy-weight coarse cloth and coarse drills rose by 10 to 15 cents per piece. Lower-grade bleached cloth and Ewo Factory's Golden Pagoda brand had no market activity. Miscellaneous brands rose in price by 20 to 30 cents per piece. Dyed cloth, Shelin cloth, and blue cloth rose by 20 to 30 cents per piece. Serge, broadcloth, woolen cloth, and printed piece goods rose by about 30 cents per piece. Merchants and factories maintained firm positions, with market prices remaining 10 to 20 cents above prevailing levels. Dealers' purchases were brisk. Ningbo-Shaoxing dealers purchased over 100 pieces of heavy-weight coarse cloth and over 200 pieces of light-weight coarse cloth, along with dozens of cases of serge and broadcloth. Henan and Shanxi dealers purchased over 100 pieces of printed broadcloth, serge, plain serge from local mills, white goods, fine cloth from various factories, and fine drills. Demand was also good in Changsha, Hankou, Nanchang, Luzhou, Wuhu, and along the Yangtze River, with fine cloth and fine drills from local mills being the most popular. Sales in Yantai on the northern route and the two Guangdong provinces on the southern route remained sluggish. Yesterday, over 100 pieces of fine cloth and over 200 pieces of fine drills were traded.

Domestically Produced Camel Wool Continues to Enter the Market

Domestically produced wide and narrow striped plain camel wool has gradually entered the market. Local merchants, such as Baodaxiang and Xiedaxiang in the southern city and Chunheyonghua and Xinyonghua in the northern city, have significant orders and transactions. Shanghai offices representing Chengdu, Yunnan, and Guiyang have also negotiated and completed deals. Existing stock from Wei Yi, Da Dong, Wei Lun, Shen Chang, and Tian Xiang factories continues to be shipped out. Neither buyers nor sellers have made any announcements.

Silk and Tea: Yokohama Silk Hits New High Price

Yesterday, the New York market was closed. The Yokohama silk market was firm, exceeding previous levels. Spot prices opened at 750 yuan, and futures opened at 740 yuan, up 7 to 13 yuan from last week, marking a new high price since the arrival of new silk. In Europe, the silk market remained unchanged. Shanghai yarn prices remained firm, difficult to reconcile with overseas markets. Yesterday, yarn merchants purchased fifteen bales of Zebra and other brands at very firm prices. Foreign firms saw limited transactions in grey silk and Wan Shou silk, with prices also rising accordingly.

Sun Beauty Rayon Sales Especially Strong

120-count Sun Beauty brand rayon is selling exceptionally well. Hangzhou dealers made special trips to purchase a total of over 50 cases, and local Shanghai silk factories purchased over 20 cases, all at a price of 395 yuan. Tian Qiao brand was priced at 404-405 yuan, with several cases sold. Stocks of Tian Tan brand were already sold out, but demand remained strong. Clients from Hangzhou and Shengze are currently gathered in Shanghai, awaiting news of tomorrow's customs auction at the Shanghai Jianghai Customs. Shipments are unable to be made today because under the new customs regulations, goods cannot be transported without a tax-paid sales permit. From today onwards, local firms are unable to obtain tax-paid sales permits due to unclear procedures.

Ping Shui Tea for American Sales Also Active

Zhejiang Province's Ping Shui green tea has traditionally sold well in the United States. In recent years, due to competition from Japanese tea, its market share has declined. This year, Hua Tea's trade with the United States has shown slight activity due to stable exchange rates. Yesterday, Huzhou Gao Zhuang Da Bang and Jinlong Hua Tea firms have already opened for business, with over 1,600 cases traded at prices ranging from 39 yuan to 44.50 yuan. High-quality Lu Zhuang and Tu Zhuang Zhen Mei tea sales are exceptionally strong, while lower-grade teas have been sluggish. In the black tea market, there has been no major progress. Fragrant teas continue to sell well to Russian merchants, but due to abundant arrivals, market prices have fallen by 3-4 yuan.

Sugar Market: Guangdong Coarse White Sugar Price Rises by 20 Cents

Yesterday, the sugar market trend was stable and positive. The association's set prices were 22.10 yuan for current goods of 24 coarse white sugar, and 6.90 yuan for re-export goods. Transactions were made. Dongbai sugar was still being processed, with current goods priced at 22 yuan for #4, 21.40 yuan for #8, and 21.15 yuan for #9. Re-export goods were priced at 6.90 yuan for #4, a slight decrease; 6.80 yuan for #8; and 6.20 yuan for #9, a slight decrease. Prices for local mill's refined white sugar brands, such as Ji Dahua Jin Xin, remained unchanged. Chaozhou dealers offered excellent Zhiyang white sugar at 14.70 yuan, with over 100 bags traded. Refined red sugar was priced at 14.30 yuan to 14.10 yuan, and also at 13.40 yuan to 13.20 yuan, with over one hundred bags traded. Ordinary Huanggang Qing sold 200 bags at 10 yuan, up 10 cents. Xinghua dealers offered over 100 bags of standard Mingjing red sugar at 12.90 yuan to 12.80 yuan, up 30-40 cents.

A joint company held its first weekly exchange of Guangdong sugar yesterday. The total fixed quota was 7,637 bags. The quoted price for Guangdong's Wuyang coarse white and refined white sugar each increased by 20 cents. The sale of 250 bags of Qu Xi Factory's Wuyang coarse white sugar was priced at 21.30 yuan, and the Shunde Factory sugar was priced at 21.80 yuan. The Dongguan Factory sugar was priced at 21.70 yuan, none of which were sold. #4 refined white was priced at 20.60 yuan for 20 bags, but there was no #2 refined white sugar available.

North and South Goods: New Zhong Xing Vegetables Arrive Today

According to a long-distance telephone message from Zhenjiang yesterday, the first batch of Zhong Xing vegetables, totaling over 100 packages, was loaded onto vehicles yesterday and should arrive today. New vegetables from Xuzhou have been arriving continuously at a firm price of 20 yuan. It is said that at the beginning of the new vegetable season, price fluctuations are relatively large, and the industry will follow past practices and coordinate with each other to avoid losses from competition.

According to a telegraph message from Hankou yesterday, wood ear fungus prices rose again to 93 yuan and are expected to reach 99 yuan. The Shanghai market is expected to follow this trend.

Metals: Sales of Large White Lead Become Sluggish

Large white lead is a frequently sold product to military factories, copper coin bureaus, and machine factories. Since the production of domestically produced white lead, imports have gradually decreased. Currently, imported products are quoted at 21 yuan, while domestic products are quoted at 19.50 yuan. Yesterday's market transactions were only 40-50 dan.

Food for Thought

You must first give others some benefit and joy, and then you will have benefit and joy yourself; respect the happiness of others, and then you will have your own happiness. (Tolstoy)

The joy of life is in the fierce battles of life. (Strindberg)

A man who stakes his whole life on the love of a woman, and then gets angry and loses control when he loses, and is unable to do anything, cannot be considered a real man. (Turgenev)

Life is not about enjoyment, but about labor. (Tolstoy)

It is the power of words, not the sword, that enables mankind to conquer hypocrisy and injustice, and to achieve mutual love and lasting peace. (Zola) (Han Mei)

Summer Day at Gaoqiao: A Small Record of Seaside Swimming

— Ping

Shanghai is neither hell nor heaven. During the hottest days of summer, the scorching sun steams everyone, causing them to complain endlessly, like ants in a frying pan. Those who are accustomed to living in cramped quarters need not be told, but even the pleasure-seeking class in high-rise buildings are unable to move; at this time, everyone racks their brains to find places to escape the summer heat. The most miserable are the middle class who are neither rich nor poor. Hey! Should the middle class always suffer? No! No! We must find a way to break the myth of fate.

Some people say that although Shanghai is not as good as Qingdao, Dalian, Guling, or Putuo, fortunately Gaoqiao also has a natural seaside swimming area, where all the facilities are enough for you to enjoy yourself to the fullest. The day before yesterday, I gathered more than a dozen good male and female companions to take the city ferry from the Bund directly to Gaoqiao. Although the sun was blazing, the cool breeze from the ocean swept away all the summer heat. During this one-hour water journey, you can see the scenery on both sides of the river, the docks and warehouses of various countries, the power plant that ranks third in the world, foreign textile factories, and oil tanks such as Mobil, Asia, and Texaco. So many large economic enterprises have given us a huge shock! Fortunately, we also have the newly built fishing market and the Qiu Jiang pier, which boosted our spirits. After arriving at the Gaoqiao pier, we transferred to a "bus" and passed through winding, flat roads, reaching a beautiful village. Coming from the smoky city to the green fields, it made you feel refreshed and exhilarated, shouting praises endlessly!

Gaoqiao seaside has a vast beach, elegant grass huts, and Mongolian-style tents. Standing far away, you can see islands scattered, and sails dotting the sea, as if you are in a painting. Such beautiful scenery makes you want to linger and forget to return. The red and green-clad bathers, regardless of East or West, male or female, young or old, are all sorts. It seems that foreigners are more enthusiastic than Chinese people. What is most noticeable is several old foreigners, sitting on the beach, holding their foot-long white beards with both hands, as if they were tired from swimming. There are also foreign old ladies, swimming with their chests out and buttocks protruding, and even five or six-year-old boys can swim the breaststroke. Our team also bravely went into the sea to swim until sunset before returning with satisfaction. A certain lady said: "Seawater bathing is really indescribably pleasant, after all, it is more comfortable than drinking ice in an air-conditioned room." Perhaps this is her insightful remark.

Gaoqiao Seaside

— (Photography) Hao

It's Also Speculation

— 19

He studied a certain foreign language thirty years ago. At that time, he was a young man with great ambitions. He was indignant about the deterioration of national affairs and thought of learning a certain foreign language; his motivation was to go abroad to study and then return to the country after completing his studies, so that he could fulfill his grand ambition of saving the country.

Unfortunately, things did not go as planned. The pressure of life relentlessly drove and beat him, forcing him to abandon his grand ambition of saving the country; therefore, he was too lazy to learn a certain foreign language, and he had no time to learn it. For the sake of food and clothing, he ran around, accumulating every penny, until today he has become a wealthy man. Naturally, he no longer mentions saving the country, but now he wants to learn a certain foreign language again.

He has wanted to learn a certain foreign language again for the past five years. However, his mind is constantly shifting with the news in the newspapers. When the news is tense, his heart pounds; when it is relaxed, his desire to learn a certain foreign language fades slightly. He often thinks: So-and-so has become a "expert" in something, and So-and-so has been appointed as a comprador in a certain company. These young classmates live in foreign houses, drive cars, and have foreign wives who are good at being gentle and considerate. It's really too comfortable. Isn't this due to their knowledge of a certain foreign language? Who am I, how can I fall behind?

Thinking of this, his heart rises and falls like the tide, unable to control himself. At first, he thought that a sixty-year-old man learning boxing would be laughed at by others, let alone learning a certain foreign language, so he couldn't help but feel disappointed. But then he thought, if I don't learn now, when will I learn? Then he felt a hundred times more courageous. However, he has abandoned a certain foreign language for a long time, and he doesn't even recognize the letters anymore. What can he do? It's okay, there are many books like "100-Day Fluency" and "Introduction" now. Buying them and looking at them will always be helpful. If someone asks him what he is doing reading these books, he always replies lightly: "I'll need it in the future!"

Mourners Greatly Pleased

— Rong Yu

Because of the crowded population in Shanghai, the residences are pitifully narrow—of course, self-built Western-style houses are an exception. Once there is a wedding, funeral, or celebration, with guests arriving in droves, how can a ceremony be held in a snail shell? One has to borrow the auditorium of a restaurant or public hall. As for the place to hold a funeral, most of them are in temples, because temples have spacious grounds, and most of them have kitchens, preparing dozens of tables of vegetarian banquets is not a big deal. The arrangement of the mourning hall is also magnificent, and the monks chanting sutras are also comfortable and convenient. Therefore, people are willing to spend more money.

Funerals are different from celebrations. Relatives and friends arrive in the morning. There is no business for military bands here, only a group of small horns, sitting at the entrance, and as soon as a guest arrives, they start blowing mournfully. A servant dressed in plain clothes, holding up an invitation, leads you to the mourning hall. The drum beats several times. You can kneel and bow, or bow. The filial sons and grandsons also prostrate themselves and return the bow as a courtesy. Then you sit in the living room, drink tea, smoke cigarettes, and wait for a sumptuous vegetarian meal.

During lunch, the wine is poured cup by cup, and the dishes are served one after another. The guests cheer and laugh, just like at a wedding, except there is no finger-guessing game. The filial sons, grandsons, daughters, and daughters-in-law also drink heartily at this time, and have fun with their relatives and friends.

After lunch, several happy relatives and friends even pull out a table to play eight rounds of mahjong. In this way, the atmosphere of sadness in the mourning hall is completely eliminated. The sound of mahjong tiles clattering, the noise of people talking, and the chanting of Buddhist scriptures truly create a situation where "the dead rest in peace" and "the mourners are greatly pleased."

However, when I open the obituary, the filial sons always say "unconscious with grief" and "weeping blood," so we should be thinking of consolation. How can we bear to have fun? But if there is really a hall full of sorrow and desolation, I think relatives and friends would not want to come to accompany the tears!

A Phoenix Replaces the Oriole

— By Zhang Henshui

Chapter 4: Seeing and Hearing Are Uncertain, Sinking and Floating Doubts Reappear; Life and Death Can Be Entrusted, Giving Heartfelt Grieving Poems

He just circled and looked, looked and circled, almost obliterating a large portion of the several sheets of paper. The words crossed out on the letter were of course incoherent, so if he wanted to send a letter to Guoqi, he would have to throw this letter away and rewrite it. Did he have this intention? He crumpled the scribbled letter into a ball of paper and began to grind ink and spread out another sheet. But just as he lifted his pen, a rooster crowed in the distant, cold sky. Looking again out the glass window, the edge of the sky in the southeast seemed to have a bit of fish-belly color. He had only focused on writing the letter and hadn't realized it was so late. At the same time, he noticed a chill on his feet, creeping upwards. He put down the pen and yawned twice in a row. His eyelids felt unusually dry and he couldn't help but sleep. So he threw what he had written in the corner of the table. Then he held the lamp and shone it in the corner of the table, found the paper ball, tore it to shreds as well, and then threw it into the spittoon. Still not reassured, he looked around again, making sure there was nothing written anywhere, before going to bed to sleep. This night's hard work was no less exhausting than having a minor illness, so he lay in bed without even turning over, and slept for eight or nine hours. The family had called him two or three times in the morning. In a daze, he mumbled that he was sick and went back to sleep. It wasn't until lunchtime that Madam Jiang went upstairs to check on him, and he finally got up. Thinking about what had happened last night, he felt very troubled and couldn't really eat anything at mealtime. After eating, he simply didn't go to school. His family thought he was feeling unwell, so of course, they didn't urge him. But there was someone outside who hoped he would go to school today, even more intensely than on ordinary days. Who was this? It was Zhang Guoqi, who had written the letter to test him. After sending the letter, the longer the time passed, the more anxious he became. He kept thinking to himself, if he was angry, he would definitely write back a few sentences. Judging by the time, the letter had already been written and should be in the post office. If he thought the letter was acceptable, then there would also be a reply. The letter was definitely on the way. Whether it was good or bad, it would surely be revealed in a few hours. Guoqi first thought this at home, but when he went out the door to go to school, he walked along the road looking like he had solved a difficult math problem, his face full of smiles, nodding his head several times. Thinking, why wait for his reply? He could meet him on the road and see him clearly. If he was happy, his face would definitely be smiling. If he was unhappy, he would definitely have a stern face, and might even curse. No, no, he wasn't that kind of person. Thinking of this, he shook his head a couple of times to show that he didn't mean that. (47)

Special Feature

Impressions of the Air Raid and Poison Gas Defense Knowledge Exhibition (Part 2)

— Special Correspondent

In addition, there was also an exhibition on battlefield first aid, including three parts: how to search for wounded soldiers, how to transport wounded soldiers, how to treat wounded soldiers. The content was very rich, especially the part on transporting wounded soldiers, which had many photos taken, most of them taken inside Wusong China Public School, which was destroyed by enemy fire. It is said that there was a reason why they took photos there, which was to make the public recall the pain of the past. The first aid supplies that first aid workers and the public must carry during evacuation were also displayed. Under the first aid charts were eye-catching slogans: "We need first aid workers as much as we need soldiers," "First aid workers are the loving mothers of soldiers," "Perfect first aid equipment can increase the courage of the army," "We will not let loyal and brave soldiers die in vain," "Saving one more wounded soldier preserves one more strength," "Careful battlefield first aid saves effort in rear treatment," "Many wounded soldiers cannot bear the pain and smash their heads," etc. The public's poison gas defense and first aid exhibition was organized by the Military First Aid Team of Tongji University. Their intention was to arouse the deep attention of the public and Chinese university students to battlefield first aid because the existing first aid personnel were far from meeting the actual needs.

The association also set aside a corner to display books on public air defense, poison gas defense, and other topics.

There were several small booklets on air raid and poison gas defense and first aid knowledge for sale at the venue. It is said that the association strived to keep the price of these books low, and one could buy one for just a few copper coins.

The exhibition period of the association is tentatively set for three weeks. After the closing ceremony, it will be exhibited in rotation at various youth associations.

Although the scale of this exhibition is not large, its effect on arousing public attention to air defense, poison gas defense, and first aid is not small. One more thing worth mentioning: it was heard that some of the charts displayed by the association were deemed to be of an aggressive nature by a certain official and were interfered with. After repeated explanations by a foreign affairs officer of the Youth Association, they were allowed to be displayed. In this environment, what kind of feeling do you have when you see such an exhibition? I'm sure those of you who plan to visit will be able to appreciate it!

Prepare! Prepare! This is the public's preparation!

Random Thoughts

Occasional Writings on the Lake (Part 1)

— Sent by Tianxu Wosheng from West Lake

From afar, I pity the young traveler stranded in a foreign land,

How could he easily forget the kindness and hatred of his homeland?

In my dreams, I see my kind parents with hair like snow,

Silently facing each other, talking about family matters.

Ten thousand calamus and mugwort sway by the Jian Pavilion gate,

Vivid tiger heads quiver, tender and yellow.

Slanting mist and swirling smoke fly without end,

My old garden is once again in a state of apprehension today.

No scheme can relieve the sorrow of separation,

For twenty years, my heart has been filled with the thought of repaying my parent's kindness.

I sent a painted silk fan, but it has been delayed,

By the time it arrives, I expect the weather will be deep autumn.

This is a poem written ten years ago by Cui'er to Shi'er. At that time, Shi'er was in Japan, and I was in Hangzhou celebrating the Dragon Boat Festival. I also wrote a poem, which is slightly similar to Cui'er's second poem, also about seasonal objects. In the old customs of our Hangzhou, every festival must have a traditional seasonal item passed down through generations. Most of these have a scientific function, regardless of the widespread sanitary and cleaning movements. For example, sweeping the house before and after the winter solstice, and sweeping the tombs before and after the Qingming Festival, are both examples of cleanliness starting from one's own home and extending to the remote and uninhabited areas of the countryside. The word "Duanyang" uses "Duan" to mean "correct." The sun travels along the central path, upright and without deviation. The time of the upright noon is called the Tianzhong Festival. This is the only day and time of the year that is aligned with the Zi hour of the fifteenth night of the eleventh month, when the moon travels in the middle of the sky, following the same path. The poem by ancient people, "How many times in life do you see the moon overhead," refers to this night, not the Mid-Autumn Festival. The burrows of naked insects are usually in warm, deep places. Even when the thunder of the Awakening of Insects season rumbles, they remain dormant and do not come out, because they fear the cold. Only in the Wu month, Wu day, and Wu hour, does the sunlight directly shine underground, penetrating every pore. This is similar to the mirage seen in the dark room, through the cracks in doors and windows, where the slanting sunlight shines in. When there is water in the ground, steam is generated. Naked insects have no armor, so they cannot bear it. Therefore, they urgently seek to move. Snakes, scorpions, centipedes, millipedes, and shrimp, all five poisonous insects, appear on the ground. Once out of the ground, the sun scorches them even more intensely. So they hide in dark and secluded places, and eventually, unable to return to their burrows, they settle permanently and become a nuisance to people. When people cool off on summer nights, they may accidentally touch them and be stung. They are merely defending themselves, not intentionally stinging people, just like a bee sting. The ancients deeply understood physics and devised preventative measures. Before the first day of the fifth month, on the night before, they would sprinkle weathered lime around the corners of the doors and the bases of the walls to absorb moisture and prevent snakes and insects from hiding there. Once the lime absorbs moisture, it becomes caustic calcium, with the same effects as caustic soda and potash. It can burn the skin, and naked insects, upon encountering it, would feel severe pain and dare not approach. On the fifth day, at noon, they would burn Atractylodes lancea and Angelica dahurica in a charcoal basin to create smoke to fumigate the rooms. They would also mix realgar with liquor to sprinkle around the four corners. All of these measures were intended to prevent poisonous insects from entering the house. The carbon dioxide was used as a disinfectant, Atractylodes lancea dries dampness, Angelica dahurica kills insects, and realgar contains arsenic, which has physical and chemical effects. Any insects about to move would smell these odors and fear being poisoned to death, so they would inevitably burrow back inside. Even if they did not suffocate to death, they would retreat further down, unable to escape. After this time, when the sun shifted to the west, any direct paths and pores would no longer receive sunlight, and all the accumulated vapor would naturally evaporate completely. As long as the dwelling is comfortable, they would not think of moving to a better place. As for hanging calamus and mugwort on the doors, this is to prevent external spider webs from entering the room, avoiding the sun. Garlic is also hung on the lintel of the bed curtain, because the smell of garlic can ward off mosquitoes and flies, and it can also be used for acupuncture during illness. Generally, acupuncture always uses moxa, and water acupuncture uses garlic slices as a compress instead of needles. Women often apply garlic slices to their temples on the Dragon Boat Festival to treat headaches, or if they suffer from chronic tuberculosis, they apply garlic paste to the spine, called water acupuncture, which is the same principle as Western medicine's use of drawing agents. To draw out illness, one must use drawing agents. Blister beetles are poisonous, so garlic is preferred for its stability and convenience. Coating children's foreheads with realgar is to prevent sores and boils, and drinking realgar wine is to prevent summer cold drinks from easily causing E. coli. This is all because it contains arsenic, which is the same principle as Western medicine's use of serum injections, and it also benefits travelers. Anyone suffering from heatstroke can take any calamus or mugwort hanging at a door, mix it with water, and drink it to save themselves in an emergency. Willow branches are inserted during Qingming Festival and are replaced during the Dragon Boat Festival. The use of willow branches is to extract the salicylic acid they contain, which can treat smallpox. Those suffering from smallpox often contract wind-cold, which prevents the rash from coming out, causing blood poisoning and death. Bathing in a decoction of weeping willow can help the rash reappear, which is the same principle as Western medicine's use of salicylic acid.

Shenbao Drug Special Issue

Summer Aestivation

— Yao XingShu

The cold and warm weather has a significant impact on human health; People are more prone to illness in the hot summer, which everyone knows.

The most common illnesses in summer, such as acute gastroenteritis, cholera, typhoid fever, dysentery, heatstroke, and boils, are in addition to the so-called summer aestivation.

What is summer aestivation? In the few new medical books I have at hand, I searched back and forth but couldn't find a corresponding medical term. Old medical texts say that summer aestivation is a common name for summer weakness: weakness refers to the softening and weakening of the hands and feet, with joints that are loose and uncontracted; when it occurs in the summer, it is called summer weakness. In Japanese folklore, it is called summer wasting, referring to the body becoming thin in the summer. Childhood memories are the most profound. When I was around ten years old, whenever summer came, I always had a poor appetite, a sallow and thin face, a dispirited mind, and a fondness for lying down; when the weather was cooler, my body felt much lighter. Older people would say this was summer aestivation. Other children and adults also experienced this.

Old medical texts say that the cause of summer aestivation is due to the weakness of the spleen and stomach, with damp heat and fluid retention. However, it doesn't explain why these symptoms don't occur in the cold season, which is a shortcoming. It turns out that the cold and heat of the climate have a close relationship with the physiological functions of the human body. Take the dogs we raise as an example. In winter, they often like to curl up. This is because the weather is cold, and they want to reduce the surface area of their bodies to minimize heat dissipation, so as to achieve the purpose of maintaining body temperature; but in summer, especially when it's hot, even if they lie on the ground, they naturally don't curl up. Their heads are often raised, their tongues hanging out, and they are constantly panting. Such stretching of their limbs and rapid breathing with mouths open and tongues out are meant to increase heat dissipation and prevent heat accumulation. This kind of life adaptation is visible; there are many more that we can't see.

Accordingly, in the hot summer, the human body, because of the increase in temperature, undergoes various physiological adaptations to maintain a normal healthy state, which is undoubtedly imaginable. If this adaptive function is impaired by other factors, the body will naturally feel uncomfortable. In my personal opinion, the cause of summer aestivation lies in this.

Based on my personal childhood experience and observations after starting my medical practice, the symptoms of summer aestivation are: loss of appetite, weakness in the limbs, mental fatigue, laziness to work, dizziness, chest tightness, restlessness, weakened complexion, and weight loss. Such a rough and simplistic observation is truly laughable; however, in my current environment, even if I encounter patients with summer aestivation, it is very difficult to conduct more detailed examinations to enrich my descriptions.

We must not deny the existence of summer aestivation in our country simply because there is no record of summer aestivation in the literature of advanced medical countries. As citizens of the Republic of China, we should be responsible for researching diseases unique to China's climate and soil. If we read a few foreign medical books and ignore the inherent diseases of our motherland, that is backwardness, not scientific medicine.

The treatment for this disease in old medical texts is to clear summer heat, nourish qi, strengthen the spleen, and support the stomach. My family has been in the medical profession for generations. When I was young and suffered terribly from summer aestivation every year, my father, although loving and caring for his son, didn't force me to take bitter medicine; when the weather was slightly cooler, or when the autumn breeze brought the summer heat away, I would completely recover my health. From this, it seems that this disease can be treated with expectant therapy.

According to my shallow understanding, although this disease is related to increased temperature, people who are physically weak, nervous, or have worms are more likely to develop it. Especially for children with summer aestivation, deworming should be paid attention to. This point comes from a bit of experience I gained from my son.

Regarding the treatment of this disease, relocation therapy is impractical, symptomatic drug therapy is meaningless. The most important thing is to eliminate the contributing factors, and improving summer lifestyle is the most important, which can prevent the occurrence of summer aestivation or reduce its symptoms. These are described below:

(1) You must take a bath once a day to keep your skin clean, so that the metabolic function of the skin is active. The temperature of the bath water depends on personal preference.

(2) If you have the opportunity and can tolerate it, taking a shower (shower head bath) once a day is also very good; residents in tropical areas must take a shower every day. Although the weather is so hot that it makes people tired, after taking a shower, you feel refreshed and your health is not impaired.

(3) The diet should be light, and fatty meats should be used less. Fatty foods can produce a large amount of heat in the human body, which is not needed in an environment where the temperature has already increased.

(4) You must get enough sleep at night. After it cools down in the evening, you should go to bed immediately, do not go out at night, go to bed early and get up early, and taking a nap can also help to revitalize the spirit.

(5) Drinks such as boiled water and light tea can be drunk in sufficient quantities. The supply of water has an important meaning for the dissipation of body heat. An appropriate amount of fruit is also very helpful for the intake of vitamins and the excretion of bowel movements.

A Visit to the North Sea Islands of Germany (Part 2)

— Ding HuiKang

It is very convenient for the people living on the island to take sea baths and perform air baths, because the beach is in front of their houses, and there is no need to travel far. The yellow sand is extremely soft, and it is safe for young children to bathe here. There are three sports fields on the entire island, some in sheltered forests.

The wind direction mostly comes from the west, and almost all of it is ocean air. The temperature of the seawater is easily heated. Sea bathing is possible in mid-May. In terms of air temperature, on December 15, 1933, the temperature in Triesden was 24 degrees below zero, while the temperature in Föhr Island was 2 degrees below zero. The coldest day on the island does not exceed 5 or 6 degrees below zero. From this point of view, the climate on the island is almost 20 degrees different from that on the mainland. As for the duration of sunlight exposure, it is also the longest among the German sanatoriums. For example, in December 1933, the duration of sunlight exposure was 64.6 hours. (Note that the weather in Northern Europe is often cloudy and rainy in winter, which is different from our country.)

The center of the island's sanatorium has a music pavilion, tennis court, golf course, shooting range, seal farm, sailing and other facilities. In addition, there are seventeen small villages on the island, all hidden deep in the forests, away from the world. The chapel, built in the 13th century, is a famous ancient monument. A cemetery is next to it, with flowers like brocade and dense shade, the scenery is very quiet. The island's museum has a very rich collection, including everything about geology, botany, zoology, history, and folk tales. The specimens of astronomy and marine climate are the most valuable. This is due to the lifelong perseverance of Dr. Haibeilin, the founder of the island, and it was not achieved overnight.

From a medical point of view, the air in this area is clean, contains moisture, and the climate has no drastic changes, which is very beneficial to the respiratory organs. Sea bathing and sunbathing can give the skin a longer temperature retention capacity. In terms of metabolism, although the consumption of human body heat (calories) almost doubles, the storage of protein, calcium, and phosphorus, which are the main substances of the human body, can be increased. Therefore, it can eliminate many allergic reactions. In other words, it can enhance the resistance to infectious diseases. According to experts on the island, the greatness of this resistance is almost the same as the function of diphtheria antitoxin in diphtheria.

From this point of view, (1) inflammatory conditions of the upper respiratory tract, nasal cavity, trachea, and bronchi, as well as bronchial asthma, (2) skin and glandular tuberculosis, bronchial tuberculosis, bone and joint diseases, (3) developmental disorders in children, general weakness, (4) poor digestion, loss of appetite, nervous gastritis, (5) anemia, nervous heart disorders, poor blood circulation, (6) overwork, and neurasthenia, (7) the recovery period after serious illnesses, especially respiratory diseases, are all suitable for the principles of marine therapy.

On the contrary, those who are not suitable for marine therapy include pulmonary tuberculosis, kidney and bladder diseases, heart diseases, malignant neoplasms, and epilepsy.

The duration of treatment is usually six weeks, but for chronic or stubborn inflammation, such as asthma, it takes three to six months. It is worth noting that the effectiveness of winter treatment on the island is such that in the winter of 1928, 3,650 people went to the island for treatment, most of whom were patients with inflammation that was difficult to treat in the mainland climate. Therefore, the island has a boast that the value of one winter is equal to two summers.

The island has a municipal management office, specialist physicians such as pediatricians, surgeons, and orthopedists, as well as pharmacies, dentists, sports rooms, sanatoriums, natural science research institutes, schools, kindergartens, seal halls, post offices, telegraph offices, and telephone bureaus. In terms of transportation, there are airplanes and ships. The cost of living is sufficient with four or five marks per day.

Hamburg Children's Sanatorium on Föhr Island

Historically, in the mid-17th century, the British physician Russel advocated that the ocean has therapeutic functions. Later, the French also agreed with him. The first marine hospital was established in 1792 in Margate. The German university professor Beneke founded the first German marine hospital on the island in 1881, which is today's Hamburg Children's Sanatorium. But within a few months, Beneke passed away. The physicians all came from London and Margate, which was the beginning of the introduction of marine therapy. During World War I, this kind of assistance disappeared completely. In 1921, Mr. Martini of Hamburg resolutely bought and rebuilt the hospital, such as winter treatment equipment, water and gas heating equipment, X-rays, and everything else that is indispensable for children's sanatoriums.

Indications All children suffering from chronic inflammation, glandular disease, tuberculosis other than of the lungs, bronchial asthma, general weakness, and developmental delay are suitable for marine therapy, but special attention must be paid to whether children with heart and neurological diseases can go for treatment. The hospital does not accept patients with serious illnesses.

Treatment methods The doctor's job is to determine the time for lying-down therapy. Sun lamps, Soolux lamps, air baths, sun baths, sea water baths, and cod liver oil are all commonly used treatment methods. Attention is also paid to nursing. Blood tests are also extremely important, and there is a chemical laboratory to manage them specifically.

The sources of therapeutic power, such as sunlight, wind power, and sea water, all have staff to pay attention to the time and quantity of their application.

Treatment period From January to April is the winter treatment period, which can accommodate 100 children. From April to October is the summer treatment period, which can accommodate 270 children. From October to November is the autumn treatment period, which can accommodate 200 children. One treatment period in each period is 50 days. December of each year is a holiday period, so that all hospital staff can rest.

Treatment results Based on the weather and the original physical condition, generally speaking, each child can increase their height by one-tenth of a meter in a short time, and their weight can increase by an average of six to seven kilograms.
