Common Knowledge Q&A on Diseases

— Cheng Hanzhang

(88) Pyelonephritis

What is pyelonephritis?

This is an inflammation in the renal pelvis of the kidney caused by the invasion of bacteria.

What kinds of bacteria can invade this area and cause inflammation?

Primary pyelonephritis is usually caused by the invasion of E. coli; secondary pyelonephritis is mostly caused by typhoid bacillus, influenza bacillus, or inflammation in neighboring organs. In addition, it can also be caused by stones or parasites in the renal pelvis.

What are the symptoms when pyelonephritis occurs?

The symptoms of pyelonephritis are nothing more than changes in urine, pain in the kidney area, fever, and neurological symptoms.

How does the urine change?

The patient's excreted urine contains pus cells and renal pelvic epithelial cells. The urine is acidic, voluminous and thin, and sometimes contains protein or blood.

What is the pain in the kidney area like?

There is spontaneous pain in the kidney area, or pain caused by pressure. The pain can be very severe, spreading to the ureter or bladder, but there may also be no pain at all.

What is the nature of the fever?

The patient has a fever that is not very regular; it is remittent, sometimes with chills and rigors leading to high fever.

What are the neurological symptoms?

Neurological symptoms include headache, delirium, and stupor. These symptoms are all due to kidney dysfunction, leading to blood poisoning and uremia.

How long does this disease usually last?

The course of pyelonephritis varies depending on the underlying disease. Cases secondary to puerperium, acute infectious diseases, or cystitis tend to have a faster course. Gonococcal pyelonephritis is mainly characterized by high fever and pain in the kidney area, and has a slower course.

How is pyelonephritis diagnosed?

It is only necessary to check the urine for pus cells and renal pelvic epithelium, and refer to whether there is pain in the kidney area, or perform cystoscopy, to confirm the diagnosis.

What is the treatment for pyelonephritis?

During the fever period, the patient should rest quietly in bed, with the upper body elevated. The diet should avoid irritating foods, and drink plenty of soups and beverages.

What methods should be used to treat local pain?

Apply warm compresses, warm damp cloths, or a hot water bottle.

What medications should be used for treatment?

Uva ursi decoction, hexamethylenetetramine, helmitol, salol, borovertin, trypaflavine and other agents can be used. Recently, the internal administration of acidic beverages has been used, which is said to be able to make the urine acidic and inhibit bacteria. Washing the renal pelvis with a 0.02% silver nitrate solution is also effective.

Domestic Medicinal Plants (Continued)

— Zhou Mengbai

Solanaceae

1. Capsicum annuum, L.

Spanischer pfeffer (German) Chilly, Red pepper (English)

"Plant" Originally from the tropics of America, cultivated in dry fields, an annual herb, the stem reaches 60-90 cm in height. The leaves are petiolate, lanceolate or long oval, entire, with acute tips. In summer, it produces five shallowly lobed sympetalous flowers from the leaf axils. The berry is conical, and turns red when ripe.

"Cultivation Method" Sow seeds in the nursery bed from late March to mid-April, and transplant them to the main field in late May. The bed width is two feet, the spacing between plants is one foot, and fertilizers such as compost, bottom fertilizer, and wood ash are used. It matures in September. The whole plant is pulled up, dried, and the fruits are picked. The yield is about thirty catties per mu.

"Crude Drug" Capsicum Fruit, Fructus Capsici, is collected by drying the ripe fruit. The product is conical, with a five-lobed green calyx attached. The pericarp is thin, the surface is wrinkled, but lustrous, and it is red or dark red. The seeds are bright yellow, flat and oval, and do not exceed two millimeters in diameter. It is extremely pungent.

"Ingredients" The pungent component in the fruit is called Capsaicin C18H27NO3, which is a crystalline substance with the following structural formula:

H3CO

HO:—CH2—NH CO—(CH2)4—CH CH —CH(CH3)2

The pericarp contains the red pigment Capsanthin C34H48O3 (0.41%) and the yellow pigment Carotin-C40H56 (0.057%).

The seeds contain about 25% fatty oil.

"Medicinal Use" Capsicum is a pungent stomachic (Pharmacopoeia). It is also used topically on the skin to cause local redness to promote blood circulation, and is mixed with ointment and used as a rubefacient for frostbite, rheumatism, etc. It can also be made into Capsicum Tincture (Pharmacopoeia) and Compound (Chloroform-morphine) Tincture (Pharmacopoeia).

Folk: For frostbite, the Capsicum fruit is chopped and boiled into a juice, which is applied to the affected area and can heal it.

New Drug: Capsolin, which is a ointment mainly composed of Capsicum, croton oil, and camphor, is used to rub on painful conditions such as pleurisy, neuralgia, and rheumatism to relieve pain.

"Other Uses" Capsicum has the effect of stimulating appetite and is often used as a seasoning. Capsicum leaves can be cooked and eaten.

2. Datura alba, Ness.

"Plant" Grows wild in Taiwan, Ryukyu, and other places, an annual herb. The stem reaches one meter in height and is light green. The leaves are petiolate, ovate, with wavy edges and acute tips. In summer, it produces white long funnel-shaped flowers from the leaf axils. The corolla has five lobes, the tips of the lobes are sharp, the calyx is tubular, and its length is less than half of the corolla. The capsule is spherical and sparsely covered with short spines. The seeds are white and slightly flattened.

"Ingredients" The seeds contain several alkaloids. The content of the main components is as follows: Scopolamine 0.24%, Hyoscyamine 0.02%, Atropine 0.0025%. It also contains 20-30% fatty oil. The fatty acids are mainly oleic acid (61%) and linoleic acid (24%).

"Medicinal Use" The seeds are used as a raw material for the manufacture of Scopolamine. The by-products are many. (To be continued)

Q & A on Dental Knowledge (37)

— Lin Jianxian

(Question 186) Why must one see a dentist for toothache?

Answer: Because the cause of toothache is difficult to find by oneself. It must be through the dentist's rigorous examination to know whether it is due to the disease of the teeth themselves, or the disease of the surrounding tissues of the teeth, or other diseases. What is the cause, and what method can be effective? Even when it comes to symptomatic treatment, it also varies according to the symptoms. Either external application, internal administration, or other methods should be adopted, which is not easy to decide on one's own.

(Question 187) If a dentist cannot be found temporarily, what expedient methods can be applied?

Answer: Severe toothache is indeed feared by everyone. If you cannot get treatment from a dentist temporarily and the pain is unbearable, you have to find a way to relieve the pain first. For local methods, rinse frequently with cold water. Adding some alcohol to the water and rinsing the inside of the mouth is also very effective. Or mix two grams of peppermint, twenty-four cc each of alcohol and Ida, and ninety cc of chloroform, and rub the painful part vigorously. Other methods, such as warm water bath and warm water foot bath, can also reduce pain. As for internal medicine, ready-made painkillers sold in pharmacies are generally reliable. Take them according to the instructions, and they will not be harmful. However, you must not continue to take them regularly because they are effective, to the point of overdose.

(Question 188) Are the toothache relief medicines sold in many markets effective?

Answer: This kind of lotion is mostly for external use, and it only provides temporary relief. It can never achieve the purpose of radical cure. Moreover, it is not effective for all kinds of toothache.

(Question 189) What should I do if I have severe toothache and cannot sleep?

Answer: Taking an appropriate amount of sleeping pills is beneficial and harmless. Generally, sleeping pills often have both pain-relieving effects.

(Question 190) How effective are the methods used in our country to treat toothache?

Answer: Chinese people have always had very little real understanding of dental problems. They think that all toothaches are caused by tooth worms, or virtual fire rising, or wind evil accumulation. Therefore, the treatment guidelines are mainly to catch tooth worms or take some wind-dispelling and dispersing or fire-clearing medicines. These methods have no value at all. The absurdity of catching tooth worms has been said before. As for sweat-inducing drugs, although they originally have the effect of relieving pain, it is useless if the real cause of toothache is not removed.

Section 6 Treatment of Other Dental Problems

(Question 191) What is an impacted tooth?

Answer: Any tooth that is hidden in the gums and has not yet grown out can be considered an impacted tooth.

(Question 192) Which impacted tooth is most likely to develop disease?

The one that tends to be is the last tooth inside the top, called the third molar, or wisdom tooth. It should have grown out at the age of eighteen or nineteen, but it is different from other teeth and often cannot grow out on time? Sometimes it is buried until it is thirty or forty years old before it comes out. There is also a layer that often hurts and is difficult to come out when it comes out, causing very severe symptoms.

(Question 193) How should impacted teeth be treated when they hurt and are difficult to come out?

Answer: If it is because the gums are too thick and not easy to break through, and therefore it hurts and is uneasy, just ask the dentist to find a way to cut open the gums, it will be easy to grow out, and the pain will be reduced immediately. But if it is because the position of the impacted tooth is crooked, or even lies horizontally, and it cannot grow out or cannot grow out completely due to the obstruction of the adjacent teeth, then you should ask the dentist to remove the impacted tooth as soon as possible, otherwise not only the pain cannot be stopped, but it is also easy to develop serious diseases. The surrounding tissues are inflamed by stimulation, often causing suppuration, unbearable swelling and pain, pulling the head and face, and the temporomandibular joint is tight, and the mouth cannot be opened. At this time, treatment is difficult, and it is necessary to wait for one or two weeks for the inflammation to subside and the mouth to be opened before treatment can be applied. However, the body has been greatly affected, and the hospital has been ruined.

(Question 194) Why is the removal of impacted teeth more difficult than ordinary teeth?

Answer: Because part or all of it is buried in the alveolar bone, sometimes it is necessary to chisel open the alveolar bone, and sometimes it is necessary to drive the tooth into two sections before it can be taken out. Therefore, the operation is very troublesome, and the cost of the operation is also more than usual.

(Question 195) The occlusal surface without cavities sometimes feels sore and painful. How should it be treated?

Answer: For teeth that are maloccluded or have been rubbed for a long time, most of the enamel on the surface is consumed, and the yellowish dentin inside is exposed, so it can feel sore and painful. The treatment method is only to open the pulp chamber, remove the pulp, and then fill it, or simply drive away and fill the exposed dentin.

— (Jichao)

— (Yunsheng)

Favus is a kind of parasitic spherical filamentous blastomycete. It is divided into scalp favus, villous hair favus, and nail favus. Scalp favus is commonly known as ringworm. The parasitic bacteria of this disease are not only contagious between people, but also between people and chickens, mice, dogs, cats, rabbits, etc. They mostly invade the periphery of the hair follicles on the scalp. The villous hair and nails are less common. The affected area is characterized by the formation of favus scutula. The so-called favus scutula is a pure colony of favus fungus. It is formed around the hair shaft to form a hard, sulfur-colored dry scab. Sometimes it emits a strange odor. The hair then loses its luster. After a long time, all the hair in the resting area falls off. The skin gradually atrophies. Almost like baldness. Those that occur on the villous hair are very mild. Because the hair roots of the villous hair do not reach the deep part of the skin. Those that occur on the nails. The nails are thickened and have yellow spots. And if it affects the fingers. Talk

What will we report to the people of the country?

— I

The League of Nations meeting was held the other day, and the Ahuang attended the meeting and gave a painful speech. At first, he bitterly accused Italy of its cruelty and blamed the League of Nations for its incompetence. At the end of his speech, he said, What will I report to the people of the country? The listeners all applauded and sighed, which aroused general sympathy. However, the A country was finally destroyed. Even the debt-raising proposal put forward this time was rejected in full. It is feared that there will be no more opportunities to say a few words in the League of Nations General Assembly. According to the Paris telegram on the 5th, Swiss Federal Political Minister Muda has already informed Ahuang that after the League of Nations General Assembly has completed its work, he should be asked to leave the country within 24 hours. Paris's Echo reporter Bertina also sent out the same news from Geneva. The monarch of a destroyed country is despised everywhere and humiliated everywhere. As for this, if the people of a destroyed country, I don't know how they are treated by others.

A country is destroyed. Whether it can restore its old business and me in the future is a question that I will put aside for the time being. I will talk about the League of Nations again. A country is destroyed. The League of Nations can also be said to have died with it. Although the name of the League of Nations has not died, it is actually equal to death. Just look at the A representative reading a declaration in the League of Nations meeting the other day, saying, "Will the League of Nations abandon the invaded country and listen to the domination of the invaded country? The League of Nations General Assembly passed a resolution on October 10 last year, announcing Italy's crimes and judging it as an aggressor. The iron case is as solid as a mountain and cannot be shaken. May I ask whether the resolution this time is consistent with the previous resolution?" This kind of tone, when heard by the member states of the League of Nations, is so heart-wrenching and so sad.

Dr. Qi previously published repeatedly in Independent Review, saying that the League of Nations can still raise its head. I don't know how the League of Nations can raise its head. This is really Dr.'s high opinion, which is not what Dr. can dream of. Since the September 18th Incident, the League of Nations has been seen through by people, saying that it is equal to a paper tiger. This deliberate A war has been seen through by people even more, saying that it is like a mud god in an ancient temple. Moreover, since the League of Nations has failed twice, the attacks of difficult problems are increasing. For example, the Danzig problem that is currently on the table may soon break up with the League of Nations. The problem of the merger of Germany and Austria, and the problem of the hegemony of the Mediterranean Sea will gradually arise, and each one will cause anxiety to the member states of the League of Nations. This is an unavoidable fact.

The League of Nations itself also feels the failure and difficulty of dealing with various environments. Therefore, it wants to reorganize the League of Nations, or wants to strengthen the power of the League of Nations. I say this is mostly nonsense. If you want to reorganize the League of Nations, it is originally possible, but it is also changing the soup without changing the medicine. If you want to strengthen the power of the League of Nations, you can wait until after the Second World War. Why is this? Those who ridicule the organization of the League of Nations say that it is a spoils-sharing agency. In fact, the League of Nations is enough to be worthy of this. If the spoils can be divided properly, then the current international chaos will not occur. In fact, the failure of the League of Nations is also the failure of Britain and France. Britain and France are the main members of the League of Nations. Because the ambitious countries now have wild ambitions, seeing the weakness of Britain and France's abilities and the inconsistency of interests, they want to rise up and transform into a new situation. Therefore, the chaos in the European situation is just beginning and is not yet on the wane.

What are the protagonists who want to overthrow the old situation and recreate the new forces? Then Germany and Italy are. According to a Rome telegram on the 5th, General Favalay, director of the Italian Ministry of Aviation, signed an aviation agreement with the German authorities on the 26th of last month. The effective period of the agreement is set at ten years, and it contains major significance in both economics and politics. If any one of the two countries disrupts the current situation, the League of Nations will be difficult to deal with. If Germany and Italy unite, countries such as Britain and France can really be chilled. Under the current situation, it is not only He country that is suffering from the pain of destruction. Those who follow A country and are defiled by violence are not few. Ahuang can also comfort himself.

A Family

— Xu Ji

Evening fell, and thin, weak wisps of smoke rose from the fields. Dogs barked sparsely in the distance, once or twice. Mosquitoes buzzed, still swirling and biting at the sweat-soaked people just as they had ten or twenty years ago, sucking their blood. Very few families, as they had done three or five years ago, still brought their low bamboo stools to the threshing ground to eat soaked rice. The men's faces turned red from drinking, and the children, startled and uncomfortable by the adults' rough voices and the mosquitoes' bites, cried ceaselessly and chaotically. In summer, perhaps only from these "rare" fragments could one find that the village was still the old one, that the land was not new, strange, and ominous. However, in recent years, everything had become desolate and bleak. The years worsened year by year, and the people on this land could no longer live and reproduce in peace. Some were in prison, some were vaguely lost in the distance (perhaps permanently lost in another world), and some wandered in the docks of strange, "prosperous" cities... Everything had changed. Resentment and curses made people forget some of their innate emotions, and a terrible, fermenting life completely transformed—destroyed—them.

Granny Chang Geng was the first to be frightened by this "changed" world. She was nearly eighty years old and wanted nothing more than to have a "good death." However, desolation, cruelty, and decline attacked every small corner from the outside world. Even eighty-year-old Granny Chang Geng had been awakened by terrible nightmares many times. Her eyelids twitched, her heart raced, and according to her, that was not a "good omen." Her son, whom she had raised alone for thirty years, could not farm last year. He went to the city to carry bricks and tiles for someone, earning twelve copper coins a day. After working for two months, his body became increasingly gaunt and weak. When he walked and talked, he was constantly out of breath. After a month or so, the brick and tile shop in the city, feeling he couldn't do much work, abruptly dismissed him. Chang Geng cried and knelt, but it was no use. He finally came back, but after sleeping in bed for two days, on the third morning, he vomited a lot of phlegm. When they took it outside to look, it was all bloody red, terrible blood clots that had congealed...

Then, everything came to the last chapter of the book of life. Granny Chang Geng used her eighty-year-old, frail heart to laboriously finish reading it! All the hard work and suffering of the past decades were now equal to a deliberate all-in bet in a gamble, and she was destined to lose! Because, three months later, they reached the inevitable day: they could no longer find a way to make a living. The family ran out of food, and she could only cough and vomit blood. The young Mrs. Chang Geng resentfully left her three children, all under ten years old, and went to Shanghai with someone to "help people" (Note: Meaning to work as a maid). She felt that she could no longer find a comfortable life with that "consumptive ghost," so she decided to use her youth to try her foolish "fate" in the decadent big city.

Those desolate days dragged on for three days. Chang Geng suddenly started crying one night. Then, at dawn, he quietly threw the three children into the well at the stone bridge. When he returned, he looked at the sleeping Granny Chang Geng, knelt down quietly, kowtowed to her, and then hanged himself with a rope from the beam...

Everything had changed, but everything was also the old world! Now, the days were so terrifying, and it was unknown where this cruelty and ruthlessness came from. This was something that Granny Chang Geng and her contemporaries could not have imagined. Even more unimaginable was Granny Chang Geng herself. She had "cultivated" herself for a lifetime, endured a lifetime of suffering, but couldn't even manage to have a "good death." Neither she nor others would have believed that an eighty-year-old person would have to die by hanging, die in the water, and send off her children and grandchildren...

Granny Chang Geng finally died by hanging. She had cried for the old world, but this world was ultimately not the old one anymore...

A Small Tempest

— Si Er

The boss's first wife was always happy to scold people from morning till night, and today she was scolding even more vigorously. Her scolding was always the same: "Witch! Harlot! Sleeping with a man five nights a month isn't enough for you. I brought you in to be a maid, and I've been extraordinarily polite to you, but you still don't know what's good for you, and you always want to get the upper hand! Do you really want to force me to leave?..." But today, she added a lot of fresh curses to her tantrum:

"Rare! Rare! So you're capable of having a child!"

The concubine sat on the bed, unbuttoned her blouse, and held the baby to breastfeed. The boss leaned against the edge of the bed, holding a small teacup in his hand, stirring something. He frowned when he heard his wife's shouting, slowly raised his head to look at her standing angrily in the doorway, and said in a low voice,

"That's enough! Don't make such a scene. You like the child too. Bringing her in, we hoped to have a child soon to inherit the Wang family line, and now it's finally come true. Besides, it was your idea to bring her in, wasn't it?"

"Who likes her child! Who's quarreling with you! Can't I say a few words to her without you losing patience? Yes, the child is your darling treasure, but I don't care about him! I've already raised three children for your Wang family, haven't I?" The first wife pointed a finger at the boss.

"Yes, you raised three, but unfortunately, they all... Otherwise, why would we have brought her in?"

"They all died! It's because your Wang family doesn't have the fortune to keep children! How dare you say that?" She stamped her foot.

"No fortune to keep children? Haven't we gotten another one now, thanks to Heaven's blessing? That's why I advise you to be more generous and take good care of this child." He put the small teacup on the table, sat down on the edge of the bed, turned to look at the baby suckling, and asked the concubine, "Aren't you full yet?"

"..." The concubine didn't say anything, only turned her head away to show her impatience.

"Goo! Goo! Goo!" The baby cried in the concubine's arms.

"See how arrogant she's getting, that witch! Sometimes I tell her not to feed the baby too much, but she always ignores me." The first wife glared at the concubine.

"If you don't like the baby, why do you insist on interfering with whether she's full or not?" The concubine retorted.

"Hmph! You harlot! You have no respect for me now, daring to argue with me so boldly! Is the child really yours? Let me tell you: even though you gave birth to this child, he's from the Wang family line. You're raising him, but you're just lending your womb to give birth to him. He'll still be my heir in the future!" The first wife couldn't restrain herself, provoked by the concubine's words. She shouted loudly, rolled up her sleeves, strode towards the bed, snatched the baby from the concubine's arms, and ran out angrily: "You don't want me to interfere, but I insist on interfering, let's see what you do!"

The concubine collapsed on the bed in anger, and the boss just stared at the ceiling.

"Goo! Goo! Goo!" A burst of the baby's cries drifted in from afar.

Life

— Meng Hua

That sound, passionate yet mournful, especially in the quiet and cold winter night. The cold lamplight shone on the snow, and the human figures imprinted on the snow were large and blurry. But they were moving step by step. Why were their palms red and swollen? Why were they trembling all over? Why did they not want a home, the warmth of home at night?

"Okay, I'll sell it to you. Just two more alleys and I'll be home, such cold weather." They said, exhaling puffs of hot air. I knew they loved their homes too, but they couldn't help walking on the road covered with thick snow. What were they busy with, you say? What were they doing it for?

In the morning, perhaps the snow was still falling. For those lying in warm blankets, this was the perfect time for reverie. But outside the door, there was the creaking sound of a waterwheel. A Shandong man was pushing a waterwheel. No need to ask what the weather was like, the entire wheel was covered in hard ice. This water carrier took off his carrying pole, hooked on the buckets, and carried the water in. Perhaps it wasn't even dawn yet, but he had to carry it and carry it, all the way until dusk. Weren't they tired? Weren't they annoyed? Why did they furrow their brows so tightly, as if they had endless hidden pain?

Looking out from the glass window of my room, in front of me was a large square, where many people were busy erecting beams, and many people were busy transporting sand and soil. Many people were standing on the high ridges, carrying tiles. From a distance, they looked as small as monkeys. This often reminded me of the monkey shows I watched in the countryside when I was a child. The monkeys wore red robes, wore masks, and spun around on a high bamboo pole. If a gust of wind came, wouldn't they be blown down? The plasterers were busy all day long. Perhaps they had seen their companions fall down, twitching hopelessly, and had even seen the gray-white brain matter. But they still had to climb up. Who said they didn't think about their own lives, their wives and children?

What were they all doing it for? If you asked them, they would surely answer that they didn't know. Yet they kept struggling on, day after day, until they stopped moving altogether, then they let go and handed their entrance ticket to life to God.

Is life like this? Why live like this?

Loquat

— Er He

Loquats have probably been on the market in the city for some time now, right? But in the countryside, now is just the time when loquats are ripening.

After spending many years mixed up in the city, happily eating loquats is just a matter of memory. This year in the countryside, when it was snowing in the spring, my family specifically told the workers to shake the spring snow off the loquat trees in the loquat orchard, saying that this year's loquats probably wouldn't be as good as last year's, because the frequent spring snow was harmful to the loquats. I thought to myself, this is fate, I'm in the countryside, but the spring snow is falling so heavily.

Recently, I received a letter from home saying that the loquats were turning yellow, and that I had to come back this time no matter what. So I entrusted matters at school and took three days off, sat on a long-distance bus for two hours, and then stepped into my own home. As soon as my father saw me, he said, "The loquats aren't as good as they were last year, but they're not too bad, thanks to the workers shaking off the spring snow." I sat down and hadn't even finished a cup of tea when the workers had already placed many loquats on the table. I used the same skilled technique I had used more than ten years ago to peel the skin and swallow them whole, then swallowed one or two seeds immediately. I swallowed and swallowed until my stomach was a little bloated before stopping.

After lunch, I woke up from a nap, and the sun was already setting at a severe angle. I opened the back window and looked into the loquat orchard, and I saw that the countless golden loquats were like stars in the sky, with an indescribable beauty in the dark green foliage. I thought that to taste the true flavor, I had to climb the tree and pick them myself, so I quietly left through the back door and went to the loquat orchard to climb the loquat tree. After all, I hadn't climbed a tree in many years, so even though the loquat tree was easy to climb, I was a little afraid. I carefully grabbed the branches, stood firmly, then grabbed the branches again, moved my feet, and after doing this many times, I finally stood at the top. I poked my head out from the dark green foliage and looked down at the countless golden loquats from above. I leaned against the tree and picked the most golden-colored one, and still used the same skilled technique I had used more than ten years ago to peel the skin and swallow it whole, then spit out one or two seeds immediately. These seeds rustled against the countless branches and leaves a few times, lingered a few times, slipped a few times, and finally rolled onto the ground with a thud.

In the orchard, there were two kinds of loquats, one was red sand and the other was white sand. The skin and flesh of the red sand loquats were rotten red, and the taste was just sweet. The skin and flesh of the white sand loquats were light yellow, and the taste was more delicious than the red sand loquats. To put it more precisely, the taste of red sand loquats was the taste of rotten brown sugar, while the taste of white sand loquats was the taste of snow-white sugar.

I climbed from the red sand loquat tree to the white sand loquat tree, swallowing one after another, until I finally couldn't swallow anymore. People who live in the city can eat the famous loquats from Dongting Mountain, but the flavor of standing on the tree yourself and picking and eating one yourself cannot be appreciated.

I am a weary traveler returning home, so in addition to resolving my longing for loquats, I also have a strong sense of sadness. Although it doesn't reach the point of "stroking old objects and shedding tears," a kind of melancholy nostalgia is enough to crush my fragile feelings. Recalling the things I did as a child more than ten years ago, secretly climbing the tree to steal loquats in the dusk and late at night for fear of my grandmother's scolding, is like a distant dream, blurry and faded, and other than leaving a bunch of intangible sorrow, there seems to be nothing left.

In the setting sun, in the dilapidated courtyard, only the loquat trees tell old stories. Now, my grandmother is dead, my mother is dead, and my siblings are dead. Only an old father is guarding the loquat trees. The loquat trees must also feel lonely, right?

I stayed at home for three days, and now I'm back at school, burying myself in my studies. Like saying goodbye to a long-lost friend, now I am missing the loquat trees. May they
